import psycopg2

# ?곕━媛 ?곕뜕 DB ?묒냽 ?뺣낫 洹몃?濡??ъ슜
conn = psycopg2.connect(
    host="localhost", port=5432, database="autotrader_db", user="admin", password="password123"
)
cur = conn.cursor()

print("=" * 40)
print("?렞 trades ?뚯씠釉?而щ읆 紐⑸줉 ?뺤씤")
print("=" * 40)

# trades ?뚯씠釉붿쓽 而щ읆 ?대쫫怨??곗씠?????媛?몄삤湲?
cur.execute("""
    SELECT column_name, data_type 
    FROM information_schema.columns 
    WHERE table_name = 'trades'
    ORDER BY ordinal_position;
""")

rows = cur.fetchall()
for row in rows:
    print(f"{row[0]:<15} | {row[1]}")

cur.close()
conn.close()


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\create_db.py ===

"""
autotrader_db ?곗씠?곕쿋?댁뒪 ?앹꽦 ?ㅽ겕由쏀듃.

PostgreSQL 而⑦뀒?대꼫??蹂몄씤 遊??꾩슜 DB瑜?留뚮뱺??
?대? 議댁옱?섎㈃ ?ㅽ궢 (?ъ떎???덉쟾).

?ㅽ뻾: python create_db.py
"""
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extensions import ISOLATION_LEVEL_AUTOCOMMIT


# ?쒖뒪??DB 'postgres'濡??묒냽?댁꽌 ??DB ?앹꽦
ADMIN_CONFIG = {
    "host":     "localhost",
    "port":     5432,
    "database": "postgres",     # ?쒖뒪??DB
    "user":     "admin",
    "password": "password123",
}

NEW_DB_NAME = "autotrader_db"


def create_database():
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"??DB ?앹꽦: {NEW_DB_NAME}")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**ADMIN_CONFIG)
        # CREATE DATABASE???몃옖??뀡 ?덉뿉???ㅽ뻾 紐???
        # ??AUTOCOMMIT 紐⑤뱶 ?꾩슂
        conn.set_isolation_level(ISOLATION_LEVEL_AUTOCOMMIT)
        cur = conn.cursor()
        
        # 1. ?대? 議댁옱?섎뒗吏 ?뺤씤
        cur.execute(
            "SELECT 1 FROM pg_database WHERE datname = %s",
            (NEW_DB_NAME,)
        )
        exists = cur.fetchone()
        
        if exists:
            print(f"?좑툘 '{NEW_DB_NAME}' ?대? 議댁옱. ?ㅽ궢.")
        else:
            # 2. ??DB ?앹꽦
            cur.execute(f'CREATE DATABASE "{NEW_DB_NAME}"')
            print(f"??'{NEW_DB_NAME}' ?앹꽦 ?꾨즺!")
        
        # 3. ?꾩옱 DB 紐⑸줉 ?뺤씤
        cur.execute("""
            SELECT datname 
            FROM pg_database 
            WHERE datistemplate = false 
            ORDER BY datname
        """)
        dbs = [row[0] for row in cur.fetchall()]
        print(f"\n?꾩옱 DB 紐⑸줉 ({len(dbs)}媛?: {dbs}")
        
        cur.close()
        conn.close()
        
        # 4. ??DB濡??묒냽 ?뚯뒪??
        print(f"\n--- '{NEW_DB_NAME}' ?묒냽 ?뚯뒪??---")
        test_conn = psycopg2.connect(
            host="localhost",
            port=5432,
            database=NEW_DB_NAME,
            user="admin",
            password="password123",
        )
        test_cur = test_conn.cursor()
        test_cur.execute("SELECT current_database(), current_user")
        db, user = test_cur.fetchone()
        print(f"???묒냽 ?깃났: DB={db}, User={user}")
        
        # ?뚯씠釉?紐⑸줉 (鍮꾩뼱?덉쓣 嫄?
        test_cur.execute("""
            SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.tables 
            WHERE table_schema = 'public'
        """)
        count = test_cur.fetchone()[0]
        print(f"   ?꾩옱 ?뚯씠釉??? {count}媛?(?뺤긽 - 鍮꾩뼱?덉쓬)")
        
        test_cur.close()
        test_conn.close()
        
        print("\n??紐⑤뱺 ?묒뾽 ?꾨즺")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"???먮윭 諛쒖깮: {type(e).__name__}: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    create_database()

"""
autotrader_db ?뚯씠釉??앹꽦 ?ㅽ겕由쏀듃.
?뚯뒪??肄붾뱶(test_repository.py)???붽뎄?ы빆??紐⑤몢 諛섏쁺??理쒖쥌 踰꾩쟾.
"""
import psycopg2

DB_CONFIG = {
    "host":     "localhost",
    "port":     5432,
    "database": "autotrader_db",
    "user":     "admin",
    "password": "password123",
}

# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????
# ?뚯씠釉??뺤쓽 (?뚯뒪??肄붾뱶 留욎땄??
# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????

CREATE_TRADES = """
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS trades;

CREATE TABLE trades (
    id              SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    trade_date      DATE DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,
    
    stock_code      VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    stock_name      VARCHAR(50),
    
    -- 留ㅼ닔 ?뺣낫
    buy_price       INT,
    buy_quantity    INT,
    buy_amount      BIGINT,  -- ?몚 ?덈줈 異붽? (留ㅼ닔 湲덉븸)
    strategy_phase  INT,
    entry_reason    VARCHAR(100),
    buy_time        TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- ?곹깭 愿由?
    status          VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'open',  -- 'open' ?먮뒗 'closed'
    
    -- 留ㅻ룄 ?뺣낫
    sell_price      INT,
    sell_quantity   INT,
    sell_amount     BIGINT,  -- ?몚 ?덈줈 異붽? (留ㅻ룄 湲덉븸)
    exit_reason     VARCHAR(100),
    sell_time       TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- 鍮꾩슜 諛??섏씡
    fee             INT DEFAULT 0,
    tax             INT DEFAULT 0,
    profit_rate     NUMERIC(6,2),
    profit_amount   INT,
    
    created_at      TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_trades_date ON trades(trade_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_trades_code ON trades(stock_code);
CREATE INDEX idx_trades_status ON trades(status);
"""

CREATE_WATCH_LIST_LOG = """
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS watch_list_log;

CREATE TABLE watch_list_log (
    id                   SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    trade_date           DATE DEFAULT CURRENT_DATE,
    
    stock_code           VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    stock_name           VARCHAR(50),
    added_time           TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
    
    -- ?뚯뒪??肄붾뱶 ?붽뎄 而щ읆??
    phase                INT,
    open_price           INT,
    current_price        INT,
    surge_rate           NUMERIC(6,2),
    volume_ratio         NUMERIC(10,2),
    ma5                  NUMERIC(10,2),
    is_bought            BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    
    -- ?깅줉 ???곹깭
    initial_price        INT,
    today_open           INT,
    
    -- 留ㅼ닔 寃곌낵
    bought_in_phase1     BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    bought_in_phase2     BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
    phase1_attempts      INT DEFAULT 0,
    phase2_attempts      INT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- ?ы썑 遺꾩꽍 (??留덇컧 ??湲곕줉)
    today_high           INT,
    today_close          INT,
    high_pct             NUMERIC(6,2),
    close_pct            NUMERIC(6,2),
    
    created_at           TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_watch_date ON watch_list_log(trade_date);
CREATE INDEX idx_watch_code ON watch_list_log(stock_code);
"""

CREATE_DAILY_SUMMARY = """
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS daily_summary;

CREATE TABLE daily_summary (
    id                  SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,     -- ?몚 ?덈줈 異붽???怨좎쑀 踰덊샇(id)
    trade_date          DATE UNIQUE NOT NULL,   -- 湲곗〈 PRIMARY KEY?먯꽌 UNIQUE濡?蹂寃?
    
    -- ?뚯뒪??肄붾뱶 ?붽뎄 而щ읆??
    total_trades        INT DEFAULT 0,
    winning_trades      INT DEFAULT 0,
    losing_trades       INT DEFAULT 0,
    win_rate            NUMERIC(5,2),
    net_profit          INT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- 湲곗〈 而щ읆 ?좎?
    total_buys          INT DEFAULT 0,
    total_sells         INT DEFAULT 0,
    time_stopped        INT DEFAULT 0,
    force_closed        INT DEFAULT 0,
    phase1_buys         INT DEFAULT 0,
    phase2_buys         INT DEFAULT 0,
    total_pnl           INT DEFAULT 0,
    total_buy_amount    BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_sell_amount   BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    phase1_pnl          INT DEFAULT 0,
    phase2_pnl          INT DEFAULT 0,
    watch_list_size     INT DEFAULT 0,
    watch_list_bought   INT DEFAULT 0,
    notes               TEXT,
    
    created_at          TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);
"""

CREATE_SYSTEM_EVENTS = """
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS system_events;

CREATE TABLE system_events (
    id              SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    timestamp       TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW(),
    event_type      VARCHAR(30),
    severity        VARCHAR(10),
    event_message   TEXT,
    created_at      TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_events_timestamp ON system_events(timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_events_type      ON system_events(event_type);
"""

# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????
# ?ㅽ뻾 濡쒖쭅
# ???????????????????????????????????????????????????

TABLES = [
    ("trades",          CREATE_TRADES,           "留ㅻℓ 湲곕줉"),
    ("watch_list_log",  CREATE_WATCH_LIST_LOG,   "Watch List 湲곕줉"),
    ("daily_summary",   CREATE_DAILY_SUMMARY,    "?쇱씪 ?붿빟"),
    ("system_events",   CREATE_SYSTEM_EVENTS,    "?쒖뒪???대깽??),
]

def create_tables():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("autotrader_db ?뚯씠釉??앹꽦 (珥덇린??諛??ъ꽕??")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
        cur = conn.cursor()
        
        for table_name, sql, description in TABLES:
            print(f"\n[{table_name}] {description}")
            try:
                cur.execute(sql)
                conn.commit()
                print(f"  ???앹꽦/?뺤씤 ?꾨즺")
            except Exception as e:
                conn.rollback()
                print(f"  ???ㅽ뙣: {e}")
                raise
        
        cur.close()
        conn.close()
        print("\n??紐⑤뱺 ?뚯씠釉??앹꽦 ?꾨즺")
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n???먮윭: {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
        raise

if __name__ == "__main__":
    create_tables()


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\main.py ===

"""
?먮룞留ㅻℓ 遊?吏꾩엯??
?ㅽ뻾: python main.py
醫낅즺: Ctrl+C
"""
import asyncio
import time
from datetime import datetime

from api.auth import get_access_token, send_telegram
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from api.kiwoom_ws import KiwoomWS
from core.order_manager import OrderManager, FORCE_CLOSE_TIME, MAX_POSITIONS
from core.phase1b_controller import Phase1BController
from core.strategy_manager import StrategyManager
from core.strategy.portfolio_optimizer import PortfolioOptimizer
from config import settings
from utils.logger import logger


POSITION_CHECK_INTERVAL = 30
SYNC_INTERVAL = 60
STATUS_REPORT_INTERVAL = 1800
TOKEN_REFRESH_INTERVAL = 23 * 3600
SIGNAL_WATCHDOG_INTERVAL = 300
SIGNAL_TIMEOUT = 1800
STRATEGY_TICK_INTERVAL = 10
SNAPSHOT_STAGGER_SEC = 0.5  # ?ㅻ깄??醫낅ぉ 泥섎━ 媛꾧꺽


def _extract_stock_name(raw: dict, stock_code: str) -> str:
    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
        return stock_code
    for key in ("302", "hng_name", "stock_name", "name", "kor_name", "jongmok"):
        v = raw.get(key)
        if v and isinstance(v, str) and v.strip():
            return v.strip()
    return stock_code


class TradingBot:
    def __init__(self):
        self.token: str = ""
        self.rest: KiwoomREST = None
        self.ws: KiwoomWS = None
        self.order_mgr: OrderManager = None
        self.phase1b_ctrl: Phase1BController = None
        self.optimizer: PortfolioOptimizer = None
        self.strategy_mgr: StrategyManager = None
        self._stop = False

        self._signal_stats = {"insert": 0, "delete": 0, "buy_attempted": 0, "snapshot": 0}
        self._subscribed: set[str] = set()
        self._raw_keys_logged = False
        self.surge_seqs: set[str] = set()   # 湲됰벑 利됱떆留ㅼ닔 ???議곌굔 seq

    async def setup(self):
        logger.info("=" * 60)
        logger.info("?먮룞留ㅻℓ 遊??쒖옉")
        logger.info(f"   紐⑤뱶: {'紐⑥쓽?ъ옄' if settings.IS_MOCK else '?ㅼ쟾'}")
        logger.info(f"   議곌굔?? {settings.CONDITION_NAMES}")
        logger.info("=" * 60)

        self.token = get_access_token()
        if not self.token:
            raise RuntimeError("?좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")

        self.rest = KiwoomREST(self.token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)
        self.order_mgr = OrderManager(self.rest)
        self.order_mgr.sync_positions_from_server()

        self.phase1b_ctrl = Phase1BController()
        self.optimizer = PortfolioOptimizer(rest_api=self.rest)
        from core.strategy.phase3_controller import Phase3Controller
        self.phase3_ctrl = Phase3Controller()
        self.strategy_mgr = StrategyManager(
            kiwoom_rest=self.rest,
            order_manager=self.order_mgr,
            phase1b_controller=self.phase1b_ctrl,
            phase3_controller=self.phase3_ctrl,
            portfolio_optimizer=self.optimizer,
        )

        self.ws = KiwoomWS(
            self.token,
            is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK,
            on_signal=self._on_signal,
            on_trade=self._on_trade,
            on_orderbook=self._on_orderbook,
        )
        await self.ws.connect()
        await self.ws.fetch_condition_list()
        self._resolve_surge_seqs()
        await self._subscribe_conditions()

        # ???좉퇋: ?꾩옱 吏꾩엯 醫낅ぉ ?ㅻ깄??泥섎━
        await self._process_initial_snapshot()

        deposit = self.rest.get_orderable_amount()
        msg = (f"?먮룞留ㅻℓ 遊??쒖옉\n"
               f"紐⑤뱶: {'紐⑥쓽?ъ옄' if settings.IS_MOCK else '?ㅼ쟾'}\n"
               f"議곌굔?? {', '.join(settings.CONDITION_NAMES)}\n"
               f"二쇰Ц媛?? {deposit:,}??n"
               f"蹂댁쑀: {len(self.strategy_mgr.holdings)}醫낅ぉ "
               f"(1A={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('1A')}, "
               f"1B={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('1B')}, "
               f"2={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('2')}, "
                f"3={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('3')})\n"
               f"?숈쟻 鍮꾩쨷: ?쒖꽦 (Kelly+Volatility)\n"
               f"珥덇린 ?ㅻ깄?? {self._signal_stats['snapshot']}醫낅ぉ 泥섎━")
        send_telegram(msg, target="signal")
        logger.info(msg)

    def _resolve_surge_seqs(self):
        """SURGE_CONDITION_NAMES(?대쫫) ???꾩옱 議곌굔 seq 吏묓빀?쇰줈 ?댁꽍."""
        cond_map = self.ws.condition_map
        name_to_seq = {name: seq for seq, name in cond_map.items()}
        surge_names = getattr(settings, "SURGE_CONDITION_NAMES", []) or []
        self.surge_seqs = {name_to_seq[n] for n in surge_names if n in name_to_seq}
        missing = [n for n in surge_names if n not in name_to_seq]
        logger.info(f"??湲됰벑 議곌굔 seq: {sorted(self.surge_seqs)} (??? {surge_names})")
        if missing:
            logger.warning(f"?좑툘 湲됰벑 議곌굔 ?대쫫 留ㅼ묶 ?ㅽ뙣: {missing} (?곸썒臾??대쫫怨??議?")
  
    async def _subscribe_conditions(self):
        cond_map = self.ws.condition_map
        name_to_seq = {name: seq for seq, name in cond_map.items()}

        for name in settings.CONDITION_NAMES:
            seq = name_to_seq.get(name)
            if seq:
                await self.ws.subscribe_condition(seq)
                logger.info(f"   '{name}' -> seq={seq}")
            else:
                logger.warning(f"   '{name}' 議곌굔???놁쓬")

        if not settings.CONDITION_NAMES and settings.CONDITION_NOS:
            for seq in settings.CONDITION_NOS:
                if seq in cond_map:
                    await self.ws.subscribe_condition(seq)

    async def _process_initial_snapshot(self):
        """遊??쒖옉 ??議곌굔?앹뿉 ?대? ?ㅼ뼱?덈뒗 醫낅ぉ?ㅼ쓣 媛?몄???泥섎━.
        ?ㅼ? ?ㅼ떆媛?援щ룆? ?깅줉 ?댄썑 ?좉퇋 ?몄엯留??뚮젮二쇰?濡??닿쾶 ?놁쑝硫?泥??덈룄?곕? ?볦묠.
        議곌굔蹂?異쒖쿂(湲됰벑 ?щ?)瑜?醫낅ぉ???쒓퉭?댁꽌 strategy濡??꾨떖."""
        cond_map = self.ws.condition_map
        name_to_seq = {name: seq for seq, name in cond_map.items()}

        code_is_surge: dict[str, bool] = {}
        for name in settings.CONDITION_NAMES:
            seq = name_to_seq.get(name)
            if not seq:
                continue
            is_surge = seq in self.surge_seqs
            try:
                codes = await self.ws.fetch_condition_snapshot(seq)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"議곌굔???ㅻ깄???ㅽ뙣: {name}")
                continue
            for c in codes:
                # 媛숈? 醫낅ぉ???щ윭 議곌굔???ㅻ㈃ 湲됰벑(True)???곗꽑
                code_is_surge[c] = code_is_surge.get(c, False) or is_surge

        if not code_is_surge:
            logger.info("?벝 珥덇린 ?ㅻ깄?? 吏꾩엯 醫낅ぉ ?놁쓬")
            return

        logger.info(f"?벝 珥덇린 ?ㅻ깄??泥섎━ ?쒖옉: {len(code_is_surge)}醫낅ぉ")
        for code, is_surge in code_is_surge.items():
            self._signal_stats["snapshot"] += 1
            stock_name = self._fetch_stock_name(code)

            try:
                self.strategy_mgr.on_condition_hit(code, stock_name, is_surge=is_surge)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"[{code}] ?ㅻ깄??on_condition_hit ?덉쇅")

            if code not in self._subscribed:
                try:
                    await self.ws.subscribe_realtime([code], ["0B", "0D"])
                    self._subscribed.add(code)
                except Exception:
                    logger.exception(f"[{code}] ?ㅻ깄???ㅼ떆媛?援щ룆 ?ㅽ뙣")

            await asyncio.sleep(SNAPSHOT_STAGGER_SEC)

        logger.info(f"?벝 珥덇린 ?ㅻ깄??泥섎━ ?꾨즺: {len(code_is_surge)}醫낅ぉ")
    def _fetch_stock_name(self, stock_code: str) -> str:
        """REST濡?醫낅ぉ紐?議고쉶 (罹먯떆 ?쒖슜)."""
        try:
            return self.order_mgr.get_stock_name(stock_code)
        except Exception:
            return stock_code

    async def _on_signal(self, stock_code: str, signal_type: str,
                         raw: dict = None, cond_seq: str = None):
        if signal_type == 'I':
            self._signal_stats["insert"] += 1
            self._signal_stats["buy_attempted"] += 1

            is_surge = bool(cond_seq) and str(cond_seq) in self.surge_seqs

            stock_name = _extract_stock_name(raw, stock_code)
            # raw??醫낅ぉ紐낆씠 ?놁쑝硫?REST濡?議고쉶 (紐⑥쓽?ъ옄 fallback)
            if stock_name == stock_code:
                stock_name = self._fetch_stock_name(stock_code)
                if not self._raw_keys_logged and raw:
                    logger.info(
                        f"[{stock_code}] raw??醫낅ぉ紐??놁쓬 (?? {list(raw.keys())}), "
                        f"REST 議고쉶 ??'{stock_name}'"
                    )
                    self._raw_keys_logged = True

           try:
                # ?쇄뼹??蹂寃쎈맖: 議곌굔???대쫫??李얠븘???④퍡 ?섍꺼以??쇄뼹??
                cond_name = self.ws.condition_map.get(str(cond_seq), "") if cond_seq else ""
                self.strategy_mgr.on_condition_hit(
                    stock_code, stock_name, is_surge=is_surge, cond_name=cond_name
                )
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"[{stock_code}] on_condition_hit ?덉쇅")

            if stock_code not in self._subscribed:
                try:
                    await self.ws.subscribe_realtime([stock_code], ["0B", "0D"])
                    self._subscribed.add(stock_code)
                except Exception:
                    logger.exception(f"[{stock_code}] ?ㅼ떆媛?援щ룆 ?ㅽ뙣")

        elif signal_type == 'D':
            self._signal_stats["delete"] += 1

    async def _on_trade(self, parsed_trade: dict):
        try:
            self.strategy_mgr.on_trade(parsed_trade)
        except Exception:
            logger.exception("on_trade ?덉쇅")

    async def _on_orderbook(self, parsed_orderbook: dict):
        try:
            self.strategy_mgr.on_orderbook(parsed_orderbook)
        except Exception:
            logger.exception("on_orderbook ?덉쇅")

    async def task_strategy_tick(self):
        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(STRATEGY_TICK_INTERVAL)
            try:
                self.strategy_mgr.tick()
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("Strategy tick ?덉쇅")

    async def task_holdings_price_fallback(self):
        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(POSITION_CHECK_INTERVAL)
            try:
                for code in list(self.strategy_mgr.holdings.keys()):
                    candles = self.rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=1)
                    if candles:
                        self.strategy_mgr.on_price_update(code, candles[0]["close"])
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("蹂댁쑀 醫낅ぉ 媛寃??대쭅 ?덉쇅")

    async def task_balance_sync(self):
        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(SYNC_INTERVAL)
            try:
                self.order_mgr.sync_positions_from_server()
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("?붽퀬 ?숆린???덉쇅")

    async def task_status_report(self):
        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(STATUS_REPORT_INTERVAL)
            try:
                deposit = self.rest.get_orderable_amount()
                h = self.strategy_mgr.holdings
                lines = [
                    f"[?뺢린蹂닿퀬] {datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M')}",
                    f"二쇰Ц媛?? {deposit:,}??,
                    f"?좏샇: ?몄엯 {self._signal_stats['insert']}嫄?/ "
                    f"?댄깉 {self._signal_stats['delete']}嫄?/ "
                    f"?ㅻ깄??{self._signal_stats['snapshot']}嫄?,
                    f"留ㅼ닔?쒕룄: {self._signal_stats['buy_attempted']}嫄?,
                    f"蹂댁쑀: {len(h)}醫낅ぉ "
                    f"(1A=..., 1B=..., 2=..., 3={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('3')})",
                    f"媛먯떆 以?(1B FSM): {len(self.phase1b_ctrl.watched)}醫낅ぉ, "
                    f"(3 FSM): {len(self.phase3_ctrl.watched)}醫낅ぉ",
                ]
                send_telegram("\n".join(lines), target="signal")
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("?곹깭 蹂닿퀬 ?덉쇅")

    async def task_token_refresh(self):
        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(TOKEN_REFRESH_INTERVAL)
            try:
                new_token = get_access_token()
                if new_token:
                    self.token = new_token
                    self.rest.token = new_token
                    logger.info("?좏겙 媛깆떊 ?꾨즺")
            except Exception:
                logger.exception("?좏겙 媛깆떊 ?덉쇅")

    async def task_force_close_watcher(self):
        initial_skip = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M") >= FORCE_CLOSE_TIME
        if initial_skip:
            logger.info(
                "遊??쒖옉 ?쒖젏???λ쭏媛??댄썑 ???ㅻ뒛 媛뺤젣泥?궛 嫄대꼫?, "
                "?ㅼ쓬 嫄곕옒???湲?
            )
        triggered = initial_skip
        last_check_date = datetime.now().date()

        while not self._stop:
            now = datetime.now()
            today = now.date()
            if today > last_check_date:
                triggered = False
                last_check_date = today

            now_str = now.strftime("%H:%M")
            if now_str >= FORCE_CLOSE_TIME and not triggered:
                triggered = True
                logger.info("?λ쭏媛?媛뺤젣泥?궛 ?쒖옉")
                for code in list(self.strategy_mgr.holdings.keys()):
                    try:
                        candles = self.rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=1)
                        if candles:
                            self.strategy_mgr._execute_sell(
                                code, candles[0]["close"], "?λ쭏媛?媛뺤젣泥?궛"
                            )
                    except Exception:
                        logger.exception(f"[{code}] 媛뺤젣泥?궛 ?ㅽ뙣")
                await asyncio.sleep(60)
            await asyncio.sleep(10)

    async def task_signal_watchdog(self):
        last_signal_count = 0
        last_signal_time = time.time()

        while not self._stop:
            await asyncio.sleep(SIGNAL_WATCHDOG_INTERVAL)

            if len(self.strategy_mgr.holdings) >= MAX_POSITIONS:
                last_signal_time = time.time()
                continue

            current_count = self._signal_stats["insert"]
            if current_count > last_signal_count:
                last_signal_count = current_count
                last_signal_time = time.time()
                continue

            elapsed = time.time() - last_signal_time
            if elapsed > SIGNAL_TIMEOUT:
                minutes = int(elapsed / 60)
                logger.warning(f"{minutes}遺꾧컙 ?좏샇 ?놁쓬 -> 議곌굔???щ벑濡?)
                try:
                    await self._subscribe_conditions()
                    last_signal_time = time.time()
                    send_telegram(
                        f"議곌굔???먮룞 ?щ벑濡?({minutes}遺?臾댁떊??媛먯?)",
                        target="signal"
                    )
                except Exception:
                    logger.exception("議곌굔???щ벑濡??ㅽ뙣")

    async def run(self):
        await self.setup()
        try:
            await asyncio.gather(
                self.ws.listen(),
                self.task_strategy_tick(),
                self.task_holdings_price_fallback(),
                self.task_balance_sync(),
                self.task_status_report(),
                self.task_token_refresh(),
                self.task_force_close_watcher(),
                self.task_signal_watchdog(),
            )
        except asyncio.CancelledError:
            pass

    async def shutdown(self):
        logger.info("遊?醫낅즺 ?덉감 ?쒖옉")
        self._stop = True

        logger.info(f"理쒖쥌 ?좏샇 ?듦퀎: {self._signal_stats}")
        if self.strategy_mgr:
            h = self.strategy_mgr.holdings
            logger.info(
                f"蹂댁쑀: {len(h)}醫낅ぉ "
                f"(1A={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('1A')}, "
                f"1B={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('1B')}, "
                f"2={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('2')}, "
                f"3={self.strategy_mgr.count_holdings_by_strategy('3')})"
            )

        if self.ws:
            try:
                await self.ws.close()
            except Exception:
                pass

        msg = (f"遊?醫낅즺 ({datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')})\n"
               f"蹂댁쑀: {len(self.strategy_mgr.holdings) if self.strategy_mgr else 0}醫낅ぉ")
        send_telegram(msg, target="signal")
        logger.info("?덈뀞??)


async def main():
    bot = TradingBot()
    try:
        await bot.run()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        pass
    except Exception:
        logger.exception("遊??ㅽ뻾 以?移섎챸???덉쇅")
        send_telegram(f"遊?鍮꾩젙??醫낅즺", target="signal")
    finally:
        await bot.shutdown()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        asyncio.run(main())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n醫낅즺")


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\observe_realtime.py ===

"""
?ㅼ떆媛?泥닿껐/?멸? ?곗씠??愿李??ㅽ겕由쏀듃
?????????????????????????????????????
09:00~吏?뺤떆媛??숈븞 議곌굔寃???몄엯 醫낅ぉ??泥닿껐(0B) + ?멸?(0D) ?곗씠?곕?
JSONL ?뚯씪濡???? ?댄썑 遺꾩꽍?쇰줈 ?꾨왂 ?뚮씪誘명꽣(泥닿껐媛뺣룄/留ㅻ룄踰??꾧퀎媛??? 寃곗젙.

?ъ슜:
    python observe_realtime.py                  # 09:20 源뚯?
    python observe_realtime.py --until 10:40    # ?쒓컙 吏??
    python observe_realtime.py --duration 5     # 5遺꾨쭔 (?뚯뒪?몄슜)
"""
import argparse
import asyncio
import json
import os
import signal
import sys
from datetime import datetime, time, timedelta

from api.kiwoom_ws import KiwoomWS
from api.auth import get_access_token
from config import settings

OUTPUT_DIR = "observations"
os.makedirs(OUTPUT_DIR, exist_ok=True)


class Observer:
    def __init__(self):
        ts = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
        self.trade_file = open(f"{OUTPUT_DIR}/trades_{ts}.jsonl", "w", encoding="utf-8")
        self.orderbook_file = open(f"{OUTPUT_DIR}/orderbook_{ts}.jsonl", "w", encoding="utf-8")
        self.signal_file = open(f"{OUTPUT_DIR}/signals_{ts}.jsonl", "w", encoding="utf-8")

        # ?듦퀎 移댁슫??
        self.subscribed: set[str] = set()
        self.trade_count = 0
        self.orderbook_count = 0
        self.signal_count = 0

        self.ws: KiwoomWS | None = None

    async def on_signal(self, stock_code, signal_type, raw):
        """?몄엯 ??0B + 0D 援щ룆 異붽?"""
        self.signal_count += 1
        record = {
            "ts": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="milliseconds"),
            "stock_code": stock_code,
            "signal_type": signal_type,
            "raw": raw,
        }
        self.signal_file.write(json.dumps(record, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
        self.signal_file.flush()

        if signal_type == "I" and stock_code not in self.subscribed:
            await self.ws.subscribe_realtime([stock_code], ["0B", "0D"])
            self.subscribed.add(stock_code)
            print(f"  ?뱻 {stock_code} 援щ룆 異붽? (?꾩쟻 {len(self.subscribed)}醫낅ぉ)")

    async def on_trade(self, data):
        self.trade_count += 1
        record = {"ts": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="milliseconds"), **data}
        self.trade_file.write(json.dumps(record, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) + "\n")

    async def on_orderbook(self, data):
        self.orderbook_count += 1
        record = {"ts": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="milliseconds"), **data}
        self.orderbook_file.write(json.dumps(record, ensure_ascii=False, default=str) + "\n")

    def flush(self):
        for f in (self.trade_file, self.orderbook_file, self.signal_file):
            f.flush()

    def close(self):
        for f in (self.trade_file, self.orderbook_file, self.signal_file):
            f.close()

    def stats(self) -> str:
        return (
            f"醫낅ぉ {len(self.subscribed)}媛?| "
            f"?좏샇 {self.signal_count} | "
            f"泥닿껐 {self.trade_count} | "
            f"?멸? {self.orderbook_count}"
        )


async def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument("--until", type=str, default="09:20",
                        help="醫낅즺 ?쒓컖 HH:MM (湲곕낯 09:20)")
    parser.add_argument("--duration", type=int, default=None,
                        help="吏???쒓컙(遺?. 吏????--until 臾댁떆. ?뚯뒪?몄슜.")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # 醫낅즺 ?쒓컖 寃곗젙
    if args.duration:
        end_at = datetime.now() + timedelta(minutes=args.duration)
        print(f"?? {args.duration}遺??숈븞 愿李?(醫낅즺 ~ {end_at.strftime('%H:%M:%S')})")
    else:
        hh, mm = map(int, args.until.split(":"))
        end_time = time(hh, mm)
        now = datetime.now()
        end_at = now.replace(hour=hh, minute=mm, second=0, microsecond=0)
        if end_time <= now.time():
            print(f"?좑툘 醫낅즺 ?쒓컖({args.until})???대? 吏?? ?ㅼ쓬?좊줈 ?≫옄 ???덉쓬.")
        print(f"?? {args.until} 源뚯? 愿李?)

    # ?좏겙 諛쒓툒
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣. config.ini??APP_KEY/SECRET_KEY ?뺤씤 ?꾩슂.")
        return

    obs = Observer()
    ws = KiwoomWS(
        token=token,
        is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK,
        on_signal=obs.on_signal,
        on_trade=obs.on_trade,
        on_orderbook=obs.on_orderbook,
    )
    obs.ws = ws

    # SIGINT 泥섎━
    stop_event = asyncio.Event()
    def handle_sigint():
        print("\n?ъ슜??以묐떒 ?붿껌")
        stop_event.set()
    try:
        loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
        loop.add_signal_handler(signal.SIGINT, handle_sigint)
    except NotImplementedError:
        pass  # Windows?먯꽌??KeyboardInterrupt濡??≫옒

    listen_task = None
    try:
        # 1. ?곌껐 + 議곌굔???깅줉
        await ws.connect()
        await ws.fetch_condition_list()

        targets = settings.CONDITION_NAMES or []
        if not targets:
            print("?좑툘 config.ini??[SYSTEM] CONDITION_NAMES 鍮꾩뼱?덉쓬. 醫낅즺.")
            return

        subscribed_seqs = []
        for name in targets:
            seq = next((s for s, n in ws.condition_map.items() if n == name), None)
            if seq:
                await ws.subscribe_condition(seq)
                subscribed_seqs.append((seq, name))
            else:
                print(f"?좑툘 議곌굔??'{name}'??李얠쓣 ???놁쓬")
        if not subscribed_seqs:
            print("?깅줉??議곌굔???놁쓬. 醫낅즺.")
            return

        print(f"\n愿李??쒖옉. {len(subscribed_seqs)}媛?議곌굔???깅줉.\n")

        # 2. ?섏떊 猷⑦봽 (諛깃렇?쇱슫??
        listen_task = asyncio.create_task(ws.listen())

        # 3. 醫낅즺 議곌굔 ?湲?(?쒓컙 ?꾨떖 or Ctrl+C)
        while not stop_event.is_set():
            if datetime.now() >= end_at:
                print(f"\n??醫낅즺 ?쒓컖 ?꾨떖")
                break
            # 留?30珥덈쭏??吏꾪뻾 ?곹솴 異쒕젰
            await asyncio.sleep(30)
            obs.flush()
            print(f"  [{datetime.now().strftime('%H:%M:%S')}] {obs.stats()}")

    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n?ъ슜??以묐떒 (Ctrl+C)")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n?먮윭: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
    finally:
        if listen_task and not listen_task.done():
            listen_task.cancel()
        try:
            await ws.close()
        except Exception:
            pass
        obs.close()
        print(f"\n?뱤 理쒖쥌: {obs.stats()}")
        print(f"?뱚 ????꾩튂: {OUTPUT_DIR}/")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        asyncio.run(main())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        pass

import sys
import json
from datetime import datetime

from api.auth import get_access_token

def raw_call(rest, stock_code, base_dt_mode):
    """
    base_dt_mode:
      'today'  ???ㅻ뒛 ?좎쭨 紐낆떆
      'empty'  ??鍮?臾몄옄??
      'absent' ?????먯껜瑜??ｌ? ?딆쓬
    raw ?묐떟??row 媛쒖닔? 泥섏쓬/???쒓컙??諛섑솚.
    """
    body = {
        "stk_cd": stock_code,
        "tic_scope": "1",
        "upd_stkpc_tp": "1",
    }
    if base_dt_mode == "today":
        body["base_dt"] = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
    elif base_dt_mode == "empty":
        body["base_dt"] = ""
    # 'absent'??base_dt ???먯껜瑜????ｌ쓬

    result = rest._request("/api/dostk/chart", "ka10080", body)
    rc = result.get("return_code")
    rows = result.get("stk_min_pole_chart_qry", []) or []
    n = len(rows)
    first = rows[0].get("cntr_tm") if n else "-"
    last = rows[-1].get("cntr_tm") if n else "-"
    return rc, n, first, last, result.get("return_msg", "")


def main():

    print("=" * 70)
    print(f"{'base_dt 諛⑹떇':<14}{'return':>7}{'row??:>7}   泥섏쓬 ~ ??)
    print("=" * 70)

    for mode, label in [("today", "?ㅻ뒛紐낆떆"), ("empty", "鍮덈Ц?먯뿴"), ("absent", "?ㅼ뾾??)]:
        rc, n, first, last, msg = raw_call(rest, code, mode)
        print(f"{label:<14}{rc:>7}{n:>7}   {first} ~ {last}")
        if rc != 0:
            print(f"               ??msg: {msg}")

    print("=" * 70)
    print("\n?댁꽍:")
    print(" - ?μ쨷???뚮┫ 寃? '?ㅻ뒛紐낆떆'媛 1媛? ?ㅻⅨ 寃?留롮씠 ?ㅻ㈃ 洹멸쾶 ?먯씤 ?뺤젙.")

"""ChemulEvaluator FSM ?쒕굹由ъ삤 ?뚯뒪??""
import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from core.strategy.orderbook import OrderbookTracker
from core.strategy.trade_flow import TradeFlowTracker
from core.strategy.wall_detector import WallDetector, WallState
from core.strategy.chemul_evaluator import ChemulEvaluator, ChemulState


CODE = "005930"


def _build():
    """湲곕낯 ?몃옒而??명듃 + ChemulEvaluator ?앹꽦."""
    ob = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=120)
    wd = WallDetector(ob, detect_multiplier=5.0,
                      shrink_ratio=0.7, disappear_ratio=0.2,
                      avg_window_sec=60)
    tf = TradeFlowTracker(max_window_sec=120)
    ev = ChemulEvaluator(
        trade_flow=tf, wall_detector=wd, orderbook=ob,
        pullback_pct=-1.5, pullback_window_sec=60,
        strength_short_window=10, strength_long_window=30,
        strength_min=180, state_timeout_sec=60,
    )
    return ob, wd, tf, ev


def _push_ob(ob, wd, ask1_vol, now):
    """?멸? push + wall_detector ?낅뜲?댄듃."""
    ob.update(CODE, {
        "ask_prices": [101], "ask_volumes": [ask1_vol] + [100]*9,
        "bid_prices": [100], "bid_volumes": [100]*10,
    }, now=now)
    wd.on_orderbook(CODE, now=now)


def _build_baseline(ob, wd, tf, base):
    """t=0~30: 媛寃?1000, ?멸? 100, 洹좏삎 泥닿껐 (baseline)."""
    for i in range(30):
        _push_ob(ob, wd, 100, base + i)
        tf.add_tick(CODE, 1000, "buy", 100, now=base + i)
        tf.add_tick(CODE, 1000, "sell", 100, now=base + i)


# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
def t1_initial_state():
    print("\n[1] 珥덇린 ?곹깭 = WAITING_PULLBACK")
    _, _, _, ev = _build()
    state = ev.evaluate(CODE, now=100.0)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK
    print(f"  ??{state.value}")


def t2_pullback_then_wall():
    print("\n[2] ?뚮┝ ??WAITING_WALL ??WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH")
    ob, wd, tf, ev = _build()
    base = 1000.0
    _build_baseline(ob, wd, tf, base)

    # 1遺꾧컙 -1.5% ?뚮┝
    tf.add_tick(CODE, 985, "sell", 100, now=base + 60)
    state = ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 60)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_WALL, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ???뚮┝ 媛먯? ??{state.value}")

    # 留ㅻ룄踰??깆옣: ask1=800 (baseline ?됯퇏 100??8諛?
    _push_ob(ob, wd, 800, base + 65)
    state = ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 65)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??踰??깆옣 ??{state.value}")


def t3_full_happy_path():
    print("\n[3] 5?④퀎 happy path ??READY_TO_BUY")
    ob, wd, tf, ev = _build()
    base = 1000.0
    _build_baseline(ob, wd, tf, base)

    # ?뚮┝
    tf.add_tick(CODE, 985, "sell", 100, now=base + 60)
    ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 60)

    # 踰??깆옣 (800)
    _push_ob(ob, wd, 800, base + 65)
    ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 65)

    # 踰?異뺤냼 (500, < 800*0.7=560) + 媛뺥븳 留ㅼ닔 泥닿껐 (10珥덇컙 留ㅼ닔 ??＜)
    _push_ob(ob, wd, 500, base + 70)
    for i in range(60, 71):  # 11 ticks of buy@100
        tf.add_tick(CODE, 1000, "buy", 100, now=base + i)
    tf.add_tick(CODE, 1000, "sell", 50, now=base + 65)  # ?뚮웾 留ㅻ룄

    state = ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 70)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_DISAPPEAR, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??異뺤냼+媛뺣룄 ??{state.value}")

    # 踰??뚯떎 (100, < 800*0.2=160)
    _push_ob(ob, wd, 100, base + 75)
    state = ev.evaluate(CODE, now=base + 75)
    assert state == ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??踰??뚯떎 ??{state.value}")

"""

import psycopg2


# DB ?묒냽 ?뺣낫 (docker-compose.yml?먯꽌 異붿텧)
DB_CONFIG = {
    "host":     "localhost",
    "port":     5432,
    "database": "analytics_db",
    "user":     "admin",
    "password": "password123",
}


def test_connection():
    """湲곕낯 ?묒냽 ?뚯뒪??""
    print("=" * 60)
    print("PostgreSQL ?묒냽 ?뚯뒪??)
    print("=" * 60)
    print(f"  Host:     {DB_CONFIG['host']}")
    print(f"  Port:     {DB_CONFIG['port']}")
    print(f"  Database: {DB_CONFIG['database']}")
    print(f"  User:     {DB_CONFIG['user']}")
    print()
    
    try:
        # ?묒냽 ?쒕룄
        conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
        cur = conn.cursor()
        
        # 1. PostgreSQL 踰꾩쟾 議고쉶
        cur.execute("SELECT version();")
        version = cur.fetchone()[0]
        print(f"???묒냽 ?깃났!")
        print(f"   PostgreSQL 踰꾩쟾: {version}\n")
        
        # 2. ?꾩옱 ?곗씠?곕쿋?댁뒪 紐⑸줉
        cur.execute("SELECT datname FROM pg_database WHERE datistemplate = false;")
        databases = [row[0] for row in cur.fetchall()]
        print(f"   ?꾩옱 DB 紐⑸줉: {databases}\n")
        
        # 3. ?꾩옱 ?뚯씠釉?紐⑸줉 (analytics_db ??
        cur.execute("""
            SELECT table_name 
            FROM information_schema.tables 
            WHERE table_schema = 'public'
            ORDER BY table_name;
        """)
        tables = [row[0] for row in cur.fetchall()]
        print(f"   ?꾩옱 ?뚯씠釉?({len(tables)}媛?: {tables if tables else '(?놁쓬, ?뺤긽)'}\n")
        
        # 4. ?뺣━
        cur.close()
        conn.close()
        print("??紐⑤뱺 寃利??듦낵")
        return True
        
    except psycopg2.OperationalError as e:
        print(f"???묒냽 ?ㅽ뙣 (OperationalError):")
        print(f"   {e}")
        print("\n?먯씤 媛?μ꽦:")
        print("  1. PostgreSQL 而⑦뀒?대꼫媛 ?뺤???(Docker Desktop ?뺤씤)")
        print("  2. ?ы듃 5432 異⑸룎 (?ㅻⅨ PostgreSQL ?ㅽ뻾 以?)")
        print("  3. 諛⑺솕踰?李⑤떒")
        return False
        
    except psycopg2.errors.InvalidPassword:
        print(f"??鍮꾨?踰덊샇 ?由?)
        return False
        
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"???덉긽移?紐삵븳 ?먮윭: {type(e).__name__}: {e}")
        return False


if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_connection()

"""
indicators.py ?⑤룆 ?뚯뒪??
?ㅼ젣 遺꾨큺 ?곗씠?곕줈 蹂몄씤 ?꾨왂??留ㅼ닔 議곌굔 寃利?

?ㅽ뻾: python test_indicators.py
"""
from datetime import datetime

from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from config import settings
from core.strategy.indicators import (
    calc_ma,
    is_ma_touch,
    is_volume_breakout,
    get_volume_ratio,
    is_bullish_candle,
    get_today_first_candle,
    calc_rise_pct_from_open,
)


def evaluate_phase1(candles: list[dict], target_date: str) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
    """
    Phase 1: 5MA ?곗튂 留ㅼ닔 議곌굔 ?됯?.
    
    議곌굔:
    1. ?쒖큹媛 ?鍮?+5% ?댁긽 湲됰벑
    2. 5MA ?곗튂 (짹0.3%)
    3. ?묐큺
    4. 嫄곕옒??1.5諛??댁긽
    """
    info = {}
    
    if len(candles) < 6:
        return False, {"reason": f"1遺꾨큺 遺議?({len(candles)}媛?"}
    
    latest = candles[0]
    current = latest["close"]
    info["current"] = current
    
    # 議곌굔 1: 湲됰벑 ?곹깭 (+5% ?댁긽)
    today_first = get_today_first_candle(candles, target_date)
    if today_first:
        rise_pct = calc_rise_pct_from_open(current, today_first["open"])
        info["rise_pct"] = round(rise_pct, 2)
        if rise_pct < 5:
            return False, {**info, "reason": f"湲됰벑 誘명솗??({rise_pct:+.2f}%)"}
    else:
        info["rise_pct"] = None  # ?ㅻ뒛 ?곗씠???놁쓬
    
    # 議곌굔 2: 5MA ?곗튂
    ma5 = calc_ma(candles, 5)
    info["ma5"] = round(ma5, 0)
    if ma5 == 0:
        return False, {**info, "reason": "5MA 怨꾩궛 遺덇?"}
    
    diff5 = (current - ma5) / ma5 * 100
    info["ma5_diff_pct"] = round(diff5, 2)
    
    if not is_ma_touch(current, ma5, 0.3):
        return False, {**info, "reason": f"5MA 誘명꽣移?({diff5:+.2f}%)"}
    
    # 議곌굔 3: ?묐큺
    if not is_bullish_candle(latest):
        return False, {**info, "reason": "?뚮큺 (諛섎벑 誘명솗??"}
    
    # 議곌굔 4: 嫄곕옒??1.5諛?
    vol_ratio = get_volume_ratio(candles, 5)
    info["volume_ratio"] = round(vol_ratio, 2)
    if not is_volume_breakout(candles, 1.5):
        return False, {**info, "reason": f"嫄곕옒??遺議?({vol_ratio:.2f}諛?"}
    
    return True, {**info, "reason": "紐⑤뱺 議곌굔 異⑹”!"}


def evaluate_phase2(candles: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
    """
    Phase 2: 60MA ?곗튂 留ㅼ닔 議곌굔 ?됯?.
    """
    info = {}
    
    if len(candles) < 60:
        return False, {"reason": f"1遺꾨큺 遺議?({len(candles)}媛? 60媛??꾩슂)"}
    
    latest = candles[0]
    current = latest["close"]
    info["current"] = current
    
    # 議곌굔 1: 60MA ?곗튂
    ma60 = calc_ma(candles, 60)
    info["ma60"] = round(ma60, 0)
    if ma60 == 0:
        return False, {**info, "reason": "60MA 怨꾩궛 遺덇?"}
    
    diff60 = (current - ma60) / ma60 * 100
    info["ma60_diff_pct"] = round(diff60, 2)
    
    if not is_ma_touch(current, ma60, 0.3):
        return False, {**info, "reason": f"60MA 誘명꽣移?({diff60:+.2f}%)"}
    
    # 議곌굔 2: ?묐큺
    if not is_bullish_candle(latest):
        return False, {**info, "reason": "?뚮큺"}
    
    # 議곌굔 3: 嫄곕옒??
    vol_ratio = get_volume_ratio(candles, 5)
    info["volume_ratio"] = round(vol_ratio, 2)
    if not is_volume_breakout(candles, 1.5):
        return False, {**info, "reason": f"嫄곕옒??遺議?({vol_ratio:.2f}諛?"}
    
    return True, {**info, "reason": "紐⑤뱺 議곌굔 異⑹”!"}


def main():
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return
    print(f"???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺\n")
    
    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)
    
    # ?뚯뒪?명븷 醫낅ぉ??(?⑦? ?멸린 醫낅ぉ ?꾩＜)
    targets = [
        ("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄"),
        ("000660", "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"),
        ("042700", "?쒕?諛섎룄泥?),
    ]
    
    # 留덉?留?嫄곕옒??(5/8 湲덉슂??
    target_date = "20260508"
    
    print("=" * 70)
    print(f"蹂몄씤 ?꾨왂 留ㅼ닔 議곌굔 ?쒕??덉씠??(??곸씪: {target_date})")
    print("=" * 70)
    print(f"\n議곌굔 ?뺣━:")
    print(f"  Phase 1: ?쒖큹媛+5% & 5MA?곗튂(짹0.3%) & ?묐큺 & 嫄곕옒??1.5諛?)
    print(f"  Phase 2: 60MA?곗튂(짹0.3%) & ?묐큺 & 嫄곕옒??1.5諛?)
    
    for code, name in targets:
        print(f"\n{'='*70}")

        # 1遺꾨큺 70媛?媛?몄삤湲?
        candles = rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=70, base_date=target_date)
        
        if not candles:
            print(f"  ?좑툘 遺꾨큺 ?곗씠???놁쓬")
            continue
        
        latest = candles[0]
        print(f"  理쒓렐 遊? {latest['time_str']}")
        print(f"  ?꾩옱媛:   {latest['close']:>10,}??)
        
        ma5 = calc_ma(candles, 5) if len(candles) >= 5 else 0
        ma60 = calc_ma(candles, 60) if len(candles) >= 60 else 0
        if ma5:
            print(f"  5MA:    {ma5:>10,.0f}?? (?鍮?{(latest['close']-ma5)/ma5*100:+.2f}%)")
        if ma60:
            print(f"  60MA:   {ma60:>10,.0f}?? (?鍮?{(latest['close']-ma60)/ma60*100:+.2f}%)")
        
        vol_ratio = get_volume_ratio(candles, 5)
        print(f"  嫄곕옒?됰퉬: {vol_ratio:.2f}諛?(吏곸쟾 5遊??됯퇏 ?鍮?")
        
        # ????? Phase 1 ?됯? ?????
        print(f"\n  [Phase 1 ?됯?]")
        passed, info = evaluate_phase1(candles, target_date)
        result = "??留ㅼ닔 ?몃━嫄?" if passed else "??留ㅼ닔 ????
        print(f"  {result}: {info.get('reason')}")
        
        # ????? Phase 2 ?됯? ?????
        print(f"\n  [Phase 2 ?됯?]")
        passed, info = evaluate_phase2(candles)
        result = "??留ㅼ닔 ?몃━嫄?" if passed else "??留ㅼ닔 ????
        print(f"  {result}: {info.get('reason')}")
    
    print(f"\n{'='*70}")
    print("???쒕??덉씠???꾨즺")
    print(f"{'='*70}")

=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_ma_compare.py ===

"""
?댁젣 09:21~10:40 援ш컙?먯꽌 30MA vs 60MA ?좏샇 鍮덈룄 鍮꾧탳.

媛숈? 援ш컙쨌媛숈? ?⑤윭?곗뒪?먯꽌 MA 湲곌컙留?30/60?쇰줈 諛붽퓭
?꾩껜議곌굔(MA?곗튂 AND ?묐큺 AND 嫄곕옒??.5x) 異⑹” '遺? ?섎? ?섎????쇰떎.

?ㅽ뻾: python test_ma_compare.py
"""
from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from config import settings

from core.strategy.indicators import (
    calc_ma,
    is_ma_touch,
    is_bullish_candle,
    get_volume_ratio,
)

VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO = 1.5
VOLUME_LOOKBACK = 5
TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES = [0.3, 0.5, 1.0]
MA_PERIODS = [30, 60]

WINDOW_START = "0921"
WINDOW_END = "1040"
FETCH_COUNT = 450

TARGETS = [
    ("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄"),
    ("000660", "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"),
    ("042700", "?쒕?諛섎룄泥?),
    ("035720", "移댁뭅??),
    ("035420", "NAVER"),
    ("247540", "?먯퐫?꾨줈鍮꾩뿞"),
    ("196170", "?뚰뀒?ㅼ젨"),
    ("373220", "LG?먮꼫吏?붾（??),
]


def hhmm_of(candle):
    return candle["time_str"][8:12]


def eval_full(candles, idx, period, tolerance):
    """candles[idx]瑜??꾩옱遊됱쑝濡?蹂닿퀬 (MA period, tolerance)?먯꽌 ?꾩껜議곌굔 留뚯”?"""
    sub = candles[idx:]
    if len(sub) < period:
        return None
    cur = sub[0]
    ma = calc_ma(sub, period)
    if not ma:
        return None
    touch = is_ma_touch(cur["close"], ma, tolerance)
    bullish = is_bullish_candle(cur)
    vol_ok = get_volume_ratio(sub, VOLUME_LOOKBACK) >= VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO
    return bool(touch and bullish and vol_ok), bool(touch)


def main():
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return
    print(f"???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺: {token[:20]}...\n")

    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)

    results = []
    for code, name in TARGETS:
        candles = rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=FETCH_COUNT)
        if not candles:
            continue
        window_idx = [i for i, c in enumerate(candles)
                      if WINDOW_START <= hhmm_of(c) <= WINDOW_END]
        if not window_idx:
            continue

        # full[period][tol] = 遺???
        full = {p: {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES} for p in MA_PERIODS}
        n_eval = 0
        for i in window_idx:
            counted = False
            for p in MA_PERIODS:
                for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
                    r = eval_full(candles, i, p, t)
                    if r is None:
                        continue
                    counted = True
                    if r[0]:
                        full[p][t] += 1
            if counted:
                n_eval += 1
        results.append({"name": name, "n_eval": n_eval, "full": full})

    # ?? ?? 醫낅ぉ蹂?30MA vs 60MA ?꾩껜議곌굔 遺?????
    print("=" * 88)
    print("?꾩껜議곌굔(?곗튂 AND ?묐큺 AND 嫄곕옒??.5x) 異⑹” 遺?????30MA vs 60MA")
    print("=" * 88)
    print(f"{'醫낅ぉ':<14}{'?됯?':>5}"
          f"{'30짹0.3':>8}{'30짹0.5':>8}{'30짹1':>7}"
          f"{'60짹0.3':>8}{'60짹0.5':>8}{'60짹1':>7}")
    print("-" * 88)
    totals = {p: {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES} for p in MA_PERIODS}
    for r in results:
        f = r["full"]
        print(f"{r['name']:<14}{r['n_eval']:>5}"
              f"{f[30][0.3]:>8}{f[30][0.5]:>8}{f[30][1.0]:>7}"
              f"{f[60][0.3]:>8}{f[60][0.5]:>8}{f[60][1.0]:>7}")
        for p in MA_PERIODS:
            for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
                totals[p][t] += f[p][t]
    print("-" * 88)
    print(f"{'?⑷퀎':<14}{'':>5}"
          f"{totals[30][0.3]:>8}{totals[30][0.5]:>8}{totals[30][1.0]:>7}"
          f"{totals[60][0.3]:>8}{totals[60][0.5]:>8}{totals[60][1.0]:>7}")

    print("\n?댁꽍:")
    print(" - 30MA媛 60MA蹂대떎 ?좏샇 遺??섍? ?щ㈃ '?????≫엺??????")
    print(" - ?? ?좏샇媛 留롫떎怨?醫뗭? 寃??꾨땲???몄씠利덉꽦 吏꾩엯???섏뼱??吏????.")
    print(" - 媛숈? ?⑤윭?곗뒪?쇰━ 30 vs 60 鍮꾧탳媛 ?듭떖.")
    print("\n???꾨즺")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

"""4媛?留덉씠?щ줈援ъ“ ?몃옒而??⑥쐞 ?뚯뒪??

import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from core.strategy.orderbook import OrderbookTracker
from core.strategy.trade_flow import TradeFlowTracker
from core.strategy.wall_detector import WallDetector, WallState


# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
# OrderbookTracker
# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
def t1_orderbook_basic():
    print("\n[1] OrderbookTracker ??湲곕낯 update/議고쉶")
    ob = OrderbookTracker()
    snap = {
        "ask_prices":  [101, 102, 103, 104, 105, 106, 107, 108, 109, 110],
        "ask_volumes": [100, 200, 300, 400, 500, 600, 700, 800, 900, 1000],
        "bid_prices":  [100, 99, 98, 97, 96, 95, 94, 93, 92, 91],
        "bid_volumes": [150, 250, 350, 450, 550, 650, 750, 850, 950, 1050],
    }
    ob.update("005930", snap, now=1000.0)

    assert ob.get_ask_volume("005930", 1) == 100
    assert ob.get_ask_volume("005930", 5) == 500
    assert ob.get_bid_volume("005930", 1) == 150
    assert ob.get_top_ask("005930") == (101, 100)
    assert ob.get_top_bid("005930") == (100, 150)
    print(f"  ???멸? 議고쉶 OK / 留ㅻ룄1={ob.get_top_ask('005930')} / 留ㅼ닔1={ob.get_top_bid('005930')}")


def t2_orderbook_avg_and_window():
    print("\n[2] OrderbookTracker ???쒓컙 ?덈룄???됯퇏")
    ob = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=10)
    base = 1000.0
    for i, vol in enumerate([100, 200, 300, 400, 500]):
        ob.update("005930", {
            "ask_prices": [101], "ask_volumes": [vol],
            "bid_prices": [100], "bid_volumes": [100],
        }, now=base + i * 2)
    avg_all = ob.get_ask_volume_avg("005930", 1)
    assert avg_all == 300, f"?꾩껜 ?됯퇏 湲곕? 300, ?ㅼ젣 {avg_all}"
    print(f"  ???꾩껜 ?됯퇏 = {avg_all}")
    avg_recent = ob.get_ask_volume_avg("005930", 1, window_sec=5)
    assert avg_recent == 400, f"吏곸쟾 5珥?湲곕? 400, ?ㅼ젣 {avg_recent}"
    print(f"  ??吏곸쟾 5珥??됯퇏 = {avg_recent}")


# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
# TradeFlowTracker (湲곕낯)
# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
def t3_trade_simple_stats():
    print("\n[3] TradeFlowTracker ??湲곕낯 stats")
    tf = TradeFlowTracker(max_window_sec=60)
    base = 1000.0
    for i in range(5):
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 200, now=base + i)
    for i in range(5):
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "sell", 100, now=base + 10 + i)

    stats = tf.get_stats("005930", window_sec=30, now=base + 20)
    assert stats["count"] == 10
    assert stats["buy_vol"] == 1000
    assert stats["sell_vol"] == 500
    assert stats["strength_simple"] == 200.0
    print(f"  ??simple={stats['strength_simple']} / count={stats['count']}")


def t4_trade_weighted_recent_dominates():
    print("\n[4] TradeFlowTracker ??媛以?媛뺣룄??理쒓렐 泥닿껐????諛섏쁺")
    tf = TradeFlowTracker()
    base = 1000.0
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "sell", 1000, now=base)
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy",  1000, now=base + 28)

    now = base + 30
    simple = 100  # 1000/1000*100
    weighted = tf.compute_strength("005930", window_sec=30, now=now)
    assert weighted > 200, f"媛以?媛뺣룄媛 ?⑥닚蹂대떎 ?⑥뵮 而ㅼ빞: {weighted}"
    print(f"  ??simple={simple} vs weighted={weighted:.1f} (理쒓렐 留ㅼ닔 ??諛섏쁺??")


def t5_trade_rising_strength():
    print("\n[5] TradeFlowTracker ???④린 > ?κ린 媛뺣룄 ?곸듅 媛먯?")
    tf = TradeFlowTracker()
    base = 1000.0
    for i in range(10):
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 100, now=base + i)
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "sell", 100, now=base + i)
    for i in range(10):
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 300, now=base + 20 + i)
        tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "sell", 100, now=base + 20 + i)

    now = base + 30
    rising = tf.is_strength_rising("005930", short_window=10, long_window=30, now=now)
    assert rising, "?④린 媛뺣룄媛 ?κ린蹂대떎 媛뺥빐????
    s10 = tf.compute_strength("005930", 10, now)
    s30 = tf.compute_strength("005930", 30, now)
    print(f"  ??10珥?媛뺣룄={s10:.1f} > 30珥?媛뺣룄={s30:.1f}")


def t6_trade_window_cutoff():
    print("\n[6] TradeFlowTracker ???ㅻ옒?????먮룞 ?쒓굅")
    tf = TradeFlowTracker(max_window_sec=10)
    base = 1000.0
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 100, now=base)

    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 100, now=base + 15)
    assert len(tf.ticks["005930"]) == 2
    print(f"  ???덈룄??寃쎄퀎 而?OK (remaining={len(tf.ticks['005930'])})")


# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
# WallDetector
# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
def _push_ob(ob, code, ask1_vol, ts):
    ob.update(code, {
        "ask_prices": [101], "ask_volumes": [ask1_vol] + [100]*9,
        "bid_prices": [100], "bid_volumes": [100]*10,
    }, now=ts)


def t7_wall_detection():
    print("\n[7] WallDetector ??IDLE ??DETECTED")
    ob = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=60)
    wd = WallDetector(ob, detect_multiplier=5.0)
    base = 1000.0
    for i in range(10):
        _push_ob(ob, "005930", 100, base + i)
        st = wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + i)
        assert st == WallState.IDLE
    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 700, base + 11)
    st = wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 11)
    assert st == WallState.DETECTED, f"DETECTED 湲곕?, ?ㅼ젣 {st}"
    info = wd.get_info("005930")
    assert info["initial_volume"] == 700
    print(f"  ??DETECTED / initial_volume={info['initial_volume']} / level={info['level']}")


def t8_wall_shrink_disappear():
    print("\n[8] WallDetector ??DETECTED ??SHRINKING ??DISAPPEARED")
    ob = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=60)
    wd = WallDetector(ob, detect_multiplier=5.0,
                      shrink_ratio=0.7, disappear_ratio=0.2)
    base = 1000.0
    for i in range(10):
        _push_ob(ob, "005930", 100, base + i)
        wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + i)
    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 1000, base + 11)
    assert wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 11) == WallState.DETECTED

    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 600, base + 12)
    st = wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 12)
    assert st == WallState.SHRINKING, f"SHRINKING 湲곕?, ?ㅼ젣 {st}"
    print(f"  ??SHRINKING (600 ??1000횞0.7)")

    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 150, base + 13)
    st = wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 13)
    assert st == WallState.DISAPPEARED, f"DISAPPEARED 湲곕?, ?ㅼ젣 {st}"
    print(f"  ??DISAPPEARED (150 ??1000횞0.2)")


def t9_wall_grows():
    print("\n[9] WallDetector ??踰쎌씠 ??而ㅼ?硫?initial 媛깆떊")
    ob = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=60)
    wd = WallDetector(ob, detect_multiplier=5.0)
    base = 1000.0
    for i in range(10):
        _push_ob(ob, "005930", 100, base + i)
        wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + i)
    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 700, base + 11)
    wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 11)
    _push_ob(ob, "005930", 1500, base + 12)
    wd.on_orderbook("005930", now=base + 12)
    info = wd.get_info("005930")
    assert info["initial_volume"] == 1500, f"媛깆떊 湲곕? 1500, ?ㅼ젣 {info['initial_volume']}"
    assert info["state"] == WallState.DETECTED
    print(f"  ??initial_volume 700 ??1500 媛깆떊")

def t10_price_latest():
    print("\n[10] TradeFlowTracker ??理쒖떊 媛寃?議고쉶")

    assert tf.get_latest_price("005930") is None

def t11_price_around():
    print("\n[11] TradeFlowTracker ??N珥???媛寃?)
    tf = TradeFlowTracker()
    base = 1000.0
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 100, now=base)
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1020, "buy", 100, now=base + 10)
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1050, "buy", 100, now=base + 30)

    now = base + 30
    # 30珥???= t=base ?쒖젏 ??媛寃?1000
    assert tf.get_price_around("005930", seconds_ago=30, now=now) == 1000
    # 20珥???= t=base+10 ?쒖젏 ??媛寃?1020
    assert tf.get_price_around("005930", seconds_ago=20, now=now) == 1020
    # 100珥???= ?곗씠???놁쓬
    assert tf.get_price_around("005930", seconds_ago=100, now=now) is None
    print(f"  ??30珥???1000 / 20珥???1020 / 100珥???None")


def t12_price_change_pct():
    print("\n[12] TradeFlowTracker ??媛寃?蹂?붿쑉 (?뚮┝ 媛먯?)")
    tf = TradeFlowTracker()
    base = 1000.0
    # 60珥???1000?? ?꾩옱 985????-1.5%
    tf.add_tick("005930", 1000, "buy", 100, now=base)
    tf.add_tick("005930", 985, "sell", 100, now=base + 60)

    pct = tf.get_price_change_pct("005930", seconds_ago=60, now=base + 60)
    assert abs(pct - (-1.5)) < 0.001, f"湲곕? -1.5, ?ㅼ젣 {pct}"
    print(f"  ??1遺꾧컙 蹂??= {pct:.2f}% (?뚮┝ 媛먯? 媛??")

=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_minute_candles.py ===

"""
遺꾨큺 議고쉶 + ?대룞?됯퇏 怨꾩궛 ?뚯뒪??

?ㅽ뻾: python test_minute_candles.py
"""
from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from config import settings


def calc_ma(candles, period):
    """?대룞?됯퇏??怨꾩궛 (吏곸쟾 period媛?醫낃? ?됯퇏)"""
    if len(candles) < period:
        return 0
    closes = [c["close"] for c in candles[:period]]
    return sum(closes) / period


def main():
    # ?좏겙 諛쒓툒
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return
    print(f"???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺: {token[:20]}...")

    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)

    # ????? ?뚯뒪??1: 1遺꾨큺 5媛?(媛寃??묒닔 ?뺤씤) ?????
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("?뚯뒪??1: ?쇱꽦?꾩옄(005930) 1遺꾨큺 5媛???媛寃??묒닔 ?뺤씤")
    print("=" * 60)

    candles = rest.get_minute_candles("005930", interval=1, count=5)
    print(f"諛쏆? 遊?媛쒖닔: {len(candles)}")

    for i, c in enumerate(candles):
        diff = c["close"] - c["open"]
        if diff > 0:
            sign = f"?묐큺 +{diff:,}??
        elif diff < 0:
            sign = f"?뚮큺 {diff:,}??
        else:
            sign = "蹂댄빀"
        print(f"\n[{i}] {c['time_str']}")
        print(f"  ??{c['open']:>9,}  怨?{c['high']:>9,}  "
              f"?:{c['low']:>9,}  醫?{c['close']:>9,}")
        print(f"  嫄곕옒?? {c['volume']:>10,}  ({sign})")

    # ????? ?뚯뒪??2: 60遺꾨큺 5媛??????
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("?뚯뒪??2: ?쇱꽦?꾩옄(005930) 60遺꾨큺 5媛?)
    print("=" * 60)

    candles_60 = rest.get_minute_candles("005930", interval=60, count=5)
    print(f"諛쏆? 遊?媛쒖닔: {len(candles_60)}")

    for i, c in enumerate(candles_60):
        print(f"  [{i}] {c['time_str']}  "
              f"??{c['open']:,}  怨?{c['high']:,}  "
              f"?:{c['low']:,}  醫?{c['close']:,}")

    # ????? ?뚯뒪??3: 5MA / 60MA 怨꾩궛 (?듭떖) ?????
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("?뚯뒪??3: ?쇱꽦?꾩옄 5MA / 60MA ??蹂몄씤 ?꾨왂 ?듭떖 吏??)
    print("=" * 60)

    candles_70 = rest.get_minute_candles("005930", interval=1, count=70)
    print(f"諛쏆? 1遺꾨큺 媛쒖닔: {len(candles_70)}")

    if len(candles_70) >= 5:
        ma5 = calc_ma(candles_70, 5)
        print(f"  5MA  = {ma5:>11,.0f}??  (理쒓렐 5遊??됯퇏)")

    if len(candles_70) >= 60:

        print(f"  ?꾩옱媛  = {current:>11,}??)
        if len(candles_70) >= 5:
            diff5 = (current - ma5) / ma5 * 100
            print(f"  5MA  ?鍮? {diff5:+.2f}%")
        if len(candles_70) >= 60:
            diff60 = (current - ma60) / ma60 * 100
            print(f"  60MA ?鍮? {diff60:+.2f}%")

    # ????? ?뚯뒪??4: ?ㅻⅨ 醫낅ぉ??鍮꾧탳 ?????
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("?뚯뒪??4: ?ㅻⅨ 醫낅ぉ??5MA / 60MA")
    print("=" * 60)

    targets = [
        ("000660", "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"),
        ("042700", "?쒕?諛섎룄泥?),
    ]

    for code, name in targets:

"""Phase1BController ?듯빀 ?뚯뒪????wrapper + WS 肄쒕갚 ?명꽣?섏씠??寃利?""
import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from core.phase1b_controller import Phase1BController
from core.strategy.chemul_evaluator import ChemulState


CODE = "005930"


def _ob_msg(ask1_vol, code=CODE):
    """on_orderbook???뚯떛???멸? dict ?앹꽦."""
    return {
        "stock_code": code,
        "ask_prices": [101] * 10,
        "ask_volumes": [ask1_vol] + [100] * 9,
        "bid_prices": [100] * 10,
        "bid_volumes": [100] * 10,
    }


def _tr_msg(price, side, volume, code=CODE):
    """on_trade???뚯떛??泥닿껐 dict ?앹꽦."""
    return {"stock_code": code, "price": price, "side": side, "volume": volume}


def _push_baseline(ctrl, base):
    """t=0~29: 媛寃?1000, ask1=100, 洹좏삎 泥닿껐 (baseline)."""
    for i in range(30):
        ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(100), now=base + i)
        ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=base + i)
        ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "sell", 100), now=base + i)


# ?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧?먥븧
def t1_watch_lifecycle():
    print("\n[1] start_watching / stop_watching / is_watching")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    assert not ctrl.is_watching(CODE)

    ctrl.start_watching(CODE)
    assert ctrl.is_watching(CODE)
    print("  ??start_watching ??True")

    ctrl.stop_watching(CODE)
    assert not ctrl.is_watching(CODE)
    print("  ??stop_watching ??False")


def t2_untracked_returns_none():
    print("\n[2] 媛먯떆 ????醫낅ぉ 肄쒕갚 ??None")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    r1 = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=100.0)
    r2 = ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(500), now=100.0)
    assert r1 is None and r2 is None
    print("  ??on_trade=None, on_orderbook=None")


def t3_initial_state():
    print("\n[3] 媛먯떆 ?쒖옉 吏곹썑 泥?肄쒕갚 ??WAITING_PULLBACK")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    ctrl.start_watching(CODE)
    state = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=100.0)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK
    print(f"  ??{state.value}")


def t4_full_happy_path():
    print("\n[4] ?꾩껜 happy path ??READY_TO_BUY (WS 肄쒕갚 ?듯빀)")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    ctrl.start_watching(CODE)
    base = 1000.0

    # baseline
    _push_baseline(ctrl, base)

    # ?뚮┝ (985 sell at t=60)
    state = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(985, "sell", 100), now=base + 60)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_WALL, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ???뚮┝ ??{state.value}")

    # 留ㅻ룄踰??깆옣 (ask1=800 at t=65)
    state = ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(800), now=base + 65)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??踰??깆옣 ??{state.value}")

    # 媛뺥븳 留ㅼ닔 ??＜ (t=60~70: 留ㅼ닔 11??+ ?뚮웾 留ㅻ룄 1??
    for i in range(60, 71):
        ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=base + i)
    ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "sell", 50), now=base + 65)

    # 踰?異뺤냼 (ask1=500 at t=70) ??SHRINKING + 媛뺣룄????WAITING_DISAPPEAR
    state = ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(500), now=base + 70)
    assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_DISAPPEAR, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??異뺤냼+媛뺣룄 ??{state.value}")

    # 踰??뚯떎 (ask1=100 at t=75) ??DISAPPEARED ??READY_TO_BUY
    state = ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(100), now=base + 75)
    assert state == ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY, f"got {state}"
    print(f"  ??踰??뚯떎 ??{state.value}")


def t5_stop_watching_clears_memory():
    print("\n[5] stop_watching ???대? ?몃옒而?紐⑤몢 ?뺣━")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    ctrl.start_watching(CODE)
    base = 1000.0

    # ?곗씠??醫 ?볤린
    for i in range(5):
        ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=base + i)
        ctrl.on_orderbook(_ob_msg(500), now=base + i)

    # ?몃옒而ㅼ뿉 ?곗씠???덈뒗吏 ?뺤씤
    assert CODE in ctrl.trade_flow.ticks
    assert CODE in ctrl.orderbook.snapshots

    ctrl.stop_watching(CODE)

    # 紐⑤몢 鍮꾩썙議뚮뒗吏
    assert CODE not in ctrl.trade_flow.ticks
    assert CODE not in ctrl.orderbook.snapshots
    assert CODE not in ctrl.orderbook.history
    assert CODE not in ctrl.evaluator._state
    assert ctrl.wall_detector.get_info(CODE) is None
    print("  ??4媛??몃옒而?硫붾え由?紐⑤몢 cleanup")


def t6_multi_stock_watching():
    print("\n[6] ?щ윭 醫낅ぉ ?숈떆 媛먯떆 媛??)
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    codes = ["005930", "000660", "035720"]
    for c in codes:
        ctrl.start_watching(c)
    assert all(ctrl.is_watching(c) for c in codes)

    # 媛?醫낅ぉ蹂꾨줈 ?낅┰?곸씤 ?곹깭 異붿쟻
    for c in codes:
        state = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100, code=c), now=100.0)
        assert state == ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK

    # ??醫낅ぉ留?stop
    ctrl.stop_watching(codes[0])
    assert not ctrl.is_watching(codes[0])
    assert ctrl.is_watching(codes[1])
    assert ctrl.is_watching(codes[2])
    print(f"  ??3醫낅ぉ ?낅┰ 異붿쟻 / 1醫낅ぉ留??좏깮??stop")


def t7_callback_with_unknown_stock_in_msg():
    print("\n[7] msg???ㅻⅨ 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶 ?ㅼ뼱???媛먯떆 醫낅ぉ ?꾨땲硫?臾댁떆")
    ctrl = Phase1BController()
    ctrl.start_watching(CODE)  # 005930留?媛먯떆

    # ?ㅻⅨ 醫낅ぉ ?곗씠???ㅼ뼱??
    result = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100, code="999999"), now=100.0)
    assert result is None

    # 媛먯떆 醫낅ぉ ?곗씠?곕뒗 ?뺤긽 泥섎━
    result = ctrl.on_trade(_tr_msg(1000, "buy", 100), now=100.0)
    assert result == ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK
    print("  ??鍮꾧컧??醫낅ぉ 臾댁떆 / 媛먯떆 醫낅ぉ ?뺤긽 泥섎━")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Phase1BController 寃利?)
    print("=" * 60)
    try:
        t1_watch_lifecycle()
        t2_untracked_returns_none()
        t3_initial_state()
        t4_full_happy_path()
        t5_stop_watching_clears_memory()
        t6_multi_stock_watching()
        t7_callback_with_unknown_stock_in_msg()
        print("\n" + "=" * 60)
        print("???꾩껜 ?듦낵")
        print("=" * 60)
    except AssertionError as e:
        print(f"\n??寃利??ㅽ뙣: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n???덉쇅: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_phase2_backtest.py ===

"""
?댁젣 09:21~10:40 (?ㅼ젣 Phase2 援ш컙)?먯꽌 留?遺꾨큺留덈떎 吏꾩엯議곌굔???됯?.

遺꾨큺? 理쒖떊??[0]=理쒖떊)?대?濡? idx踰덉㎏ 遊됱쓣 '洹??쒖젏???꾩옱遊??쇰줈 蹂대젮硫?
candles[idx:] ?щ씪?댁뒪媛 洹??쒖젏 湲곗? 怨쇨굅 ?곗씠?곌? ?쒕떎.
??媛??쒖젏留덈떎 evaluate_phase2 ? ?숈씪??怨꾩궛???ы쁽?댁꽌
   "洹?80遺??숈븞 醫낅ぉ蹂꾨줈 紐?踰??꾩껜議곌굔??留뚯”?덈굹"瑜??쇰떎.

?ㅽ뻾: python test_phase2_backtest.py
"""
from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from config import settings

from core.strategy.indicators import (
    calc_ma,
    is_ma_touch,
    is_bullish_candle,
    get_volume_ratio,
)

VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO = 1.5
VOLUME_LOOKBACK = 5
TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES = [0.3, 0.5, 1.0]

# ?됯????쒓컙? (HHMM, ?ы븿)
WINDOW_START = "0921"
WINDOW_END = "1040"

# ?댁젣 09:21源뚯? ?우쑝?ㅻ㈃ 異⑸텇???ш쾶 (15:35 - 09:21 ??374遺?+ 60MA ?ъ쑀)
FETCH_COUNT = 450

TARGETS = [
    ("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄"),
    ("000660", "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"),
    ("042700", "?쒕?諛섎룄泥?),
    ("035720", "移댁뭅??),
    ("035420", "NAVER"),
    ("247540", "?먯퐫?꾨줈鍮꾩뿞"),
    ("196170", "?뚰뀒?ㅼ젨"),
    ("373220", "LG?먮꼫吏?붾（??),
]


def hhmm_of(candle):
    """time_str(YYYYMMDDHHMMSS) ??HHMM."""
    return candle["time_str"][8:12]


def evaluate_at(candles, idx, tolerance):
    """
    candles[idx]瑜??꾩옱遊됱쑝濡?蹂닿퀬 Phase2 議곌굔 ?됯?.
    ?щ씪?댁뒪 candles[idx:] 媛 洹??쒖젏 怨쇨굅 ?곗씠??
    諛섑솚: (touch, bullish, vol_ok, full, diff_pct, vol_ratio) ?먮뒗 None(遺꾨큺遺議?
    """
    sub = candles[idx:]
    if len(sub) < 60:
        return None
    cur = sub[0]
    ma60 = calc_ma(sub, 60)
    if not ma60:
        return None
    price = cur["close"]
    touch = is_ma_touch(price, ma60, tolerance)
    bullish = is_bullish_candle(cur)
    vol_ratio = get_volume_ratio(sub, VOLUME_LOOKBACK)
    vol_ok = vol_ratio >= VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO
    diff_pct = (price - ma60) / ma60 * 100
    full = touch and bullish and vol_ok
    return (touch, bullish, vol_ok, full, diff_pct, vol_ratio)


def main():
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return
    print(f"???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺: {token[:20]}...")

    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)

    print(f"\n?됯? ?쒓컙?: {WINDOW_START[:2]}:{WINDOW_START[2:]} ~ "
          f"{WINDOW_END[:2]}:{WINDOW_END[2:]}  (遺꾨큺 {FETCH_COUNT}媛??붿껌)\n")

    # 醫낅ぉ蹂?寃곌낵: 媛??⑤윭?곗뒪留덈떎 ?꾩껜議곌굔 留뚯” 遺??? ??
    summary = []

    for code, name in TARGETS:
        candles = rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=FETCH_COUNT)
        if not candles:
            print(f"  {name} ({code}): ?곗씠???놁쓬")
            continue

        # ?쒓컙????대떦?섎뒗 ?몃뜳??異붿텧
        window_idx = [
            i for i, c in enumerate(candles)
            if WINDOW_START <= hhmm_of(c) <= WINDOW_END
        ]
        if not window_idx:
            print(f"  {name} ({code}): ?대떦 ?쒓컙? 遊??놁쓬 "
                  f"(諛쏆? 踰붿쐞 [0]={candles[0]['time_str']} ~ [-1]={candles[-1]['time_str']})")
            continue

        # 媛??⑤윭?곗뒪蹂?移댁슫??
        cnt_full = {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES}
        cnt_touch = {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES}
        cnt_bullish = 0
        cnt_volok = 0
        n_eval = 0
        best_vol = 0.0

        for i in window_idx:
            r = evaluate_at(candles, i, TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES[0])
            if r is None:
                continue
            n_eval += 1
            _, bullish, vol_ok, _, _, vol_ratio = r
            if bullish:
                cnt_bullish += 1
            if vol_ok:
                cnt_volok += 1
            best_vol = max(best_vol, vol_ratio)
            for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
                touch, b, v, full, _, _ = evaluate_at(candles, i, t)
                if touch:
                    cnt_touch[t] += 1
                if full:
                    cnt_full[t] += 1

        summary.append({
            "name": name, "code": code, "n_eval": n_eval,
            "cnt_full": cnt_full, "cnt_touch": cnt_touch,
            "cnt_bullish": cnt_bullish, "cnt_volok": cnt_volok,
            "best_vol": best_vol,
            "range": (candles[0]["time_str"], candles[-1]["time_str"]),
        })

    # ?? 寃곌낵 ????
    print("\n" + "=" * 84)
    print("?댁젣 09:21~10:40 援ш컙 ??醫낅ぉ蹂?議곌굔 異⑹” '遺? ??(遺꾨え=?됯? 媛??遺???")
    print("=" * 84)
    print(f"{'醫낅ぉ':<14}{'?됯?遺?:>6}{'?묐큺':>6}{'嫄곕옒??.5x':>10}"
          f"{'?곗튂짹0.3':>9}{'?곗튂짹0.5':>9}{'?곗튂짹1':>8}"
          f"{'?꾩껜짹0.3':>9}{'?꾩껜짹0.5':>9}{'?꾩껜짹1':>8}")
    print("-" * 84)
    for s in summary:
        print(f"{s['name']:<14}{s['n_eval']:>6}{s['cnt_bullish']:>6}{s['cnt_volok']:>10}"
              f"{s['cnt_touch'][0.3]:>9}{s['cnt_touch'][0.5]:>9}{s['cnt_touch'][1.0]:>8}"
              f"{s['cnt_full'][0.3]:>9}{s['cnt_full'][0.5]:>9}{s['cnt_full'][1.0]:>8}")

    print("-" * 84)
    # ?⑷퀎
    tot = {t: sum(s["cnt_full"][t] for s in summary) for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES}
    print(f"{'?꾩껜議곌굔 ?⑷퀎':<14}", end="")
    print(f"{'':>22}{'':>26}", end="")
    print(f"{tot[0.3]:>9}{tot[0.5]:>9}{tot[1.0]:>8}")

    print("\n?댁꽍:")
    print(" - '?꾩껜짹t'媛 0?대㈃, 洹??쒓컙???Phase2 留ㅼ닔 ?좏샇媛 ??踰덈룄 ???대떎????")
    print(" - ?묐큺/嫄곕옒??移몄씠 ??쑝硫?洹멸쾶 蹂묐ぉ. ?곗튂 移몄씠 ??쑝硫?60MA媛 蹂묐ぉ.")
    print(" - '嫄곕옒??.5x'媛 0?대㈃ 嫄곕옒??1.5諛?議곌굔??洹?醫낅ぉ쨌?쒓컙??먯꽑 ?ъ떎??遺덇?.")
    print("\n???꾨즺")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_phase2_tolerance.py ===

"""
Phase2 吏꾩엯議곌굔(60MA ?곗튂 + ?묐큺 + 嫄곕옒??1.5諛? 誘쇨컧???먭?.

遊뉕낵 100% ?숈씪??怨꾩궛???꾪빐 core.strategy.indicators 瑜?洹몃?濡?import.
?⑤윭?곗뒪瑜??щ윭 媛믪쑝濡?諛붽퓭媛硫?醫낅ぉ蹂??듦낵 ?щ?瑜??쒕줈 異쒕젰?쒕떎.

?ㅽ뻾: python test_phase2_tolerance.py
二쇱쓽: ???쒖옉 ?꾩뿉 ?뚮━硫?吏곸쟾 嫄곕옒??留됲뙋 ?쒖젏 湲곗? ?됯?媛 ?쒕떎.
      (?ㅼ젣 Phase2 援ш컙 09:21~10:40 ?ы쁽? ?꾨떂 ???⑤윭?곗뒪 誘쇨컧???뚯븙??
"""
from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST
from config import settings

from core.strategy.indicators import (
    calc_ma,
    is_ma_touch,
    is_bullish_candle,
    get_volume_ratio,
)

# strategy_manager.py ??Phase2 ?곸닔? ?숈씪
VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO = 1.5
VOLUME_LOOKBACK = 5
MA_TOUCH_TOLERANCE_PCT = 0.3   # 湲곕낯媛?(짹0.3%)

# 鍮꾧탳???⑤윭?곗뒪 ?꾨낫 (%)
TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES = [0.3, 0.5, 1.0, 2.0]

# ?먭???醫낅ぉ (code, name) ???꾩슂?섎㈃ ?먯쑀濡?쾶 異붽?
TARGETS = [
    ("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄"),
    ("000660", "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"),
    ("042700", "?쒕?諛섎룄泥?),
    ("035720", "移댁뭅??),
    ("035420", "NAVER"),
    ("247540", "?먯퐫?꾨줈鍮꾩뿞"),
    ("196170", "?뚰뀒?ㅼ젨"),
    ("373220", "LG?먮꼫吏?붾（??),
]


def evaluate_phase2_components(candles):
    """
    Phase2 議곌굔??援ъ꽦?붿냼蹂꾨줈 遺꾪빐?댁꽌 諛섑솚.
    ?ㅼ젣 evaluate_phase2 濡쒖쭅怨??숈씪??怨꾩궛???ъ슜?섎릺,
    ?곗튂 ?먯젙? ?⑤윭?곗뒪蹂꾨줈 ?곕줈 怨꾩궛?????덇쾶 raw 媛믪쓣 ?뚮젮以??
    """
    if len(candles) < 60:
        return {"enough": False, "n": len(candles)}

    cur = candles[0]
    current_price = cur["close"]
    ma60 = calc_ma(candles, 60)
    if not ma60:
        return {"enough": False, "n": len(candles)}

    diff_pct = (current_price - ma60) / ma60 * 100
    bullish = is_bullish_candle(cur)
    vol_ratio = get_volume_ratio(candles, VOLUME_LOOKBACK)

    return {
        "enough": True,
        "n": len(candles),
        "current_price": current_price,
        "ma60": ma60,
        "diff_pct": diff_pct,
        "bullish": bullish,
        "vol_ratio": vol_ratio,
        "vol_ok": vol_ratio >= VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO,
    }


def main():
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return
    print(f"???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺: {token[:20]}...")

    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=settings.IS_MOCK)

    rows = []
    for code, name in TARGETS:
        candles = rest.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=70)
        comp = evaluate_phase2_components(candles)
        comp["code"] = code
        comp["name"] = name
        rows.append(comp)

    # ?? 援ъ꽦?붿냼 ????
    print("\n" + "=" * 78)
    print("Phase2 援ъ꽦?붿냼 吏꾨떒 (?꾩옱媛 / 60MA ?鍮?/ ?묐큺 / 嫄곕옒?됰퉬)")
    print("=" * 78)
    print(f"{'醫낅ぉ':<14}{'?꾩옱媛':>10}{'60MA?鍮?:>11}{'?묐큺':>6}{'嫄곕옒?됰퉬':>10}")
    print("-" * 78)
    for r in rows:
        if not r.get("enough"):
            print(f"{r['name']:<14}  遺꾨큺 遺議?({r.get('n', 0)}媛? ??60MA 怨꾩궛 遺덇?")
            continue
        print(f"{r['name']:<14}"
              f"{r['current_price']:>10,}"
              f"{r['diff_pct']:>+10.2f}%"
              f"{'O' if r['bullish'] else 'X':>6}"
              f"{r['vol_ratio']:>9.2f}x")

    # ?? ?⑤윭?곗뒪蹂??듦낵 吏묎퀎 ??
    print("\n" + "=" * 78)
    print("?⑤윭?곗뒪蹂?Phase2 ?꾩껜議곌굔 ?듦낵 (?곗튂 AND ?묐큺 AND 嫄곕옒?됤돟1.5x)")
    print("=" * 78)
    header = f"{'醫낅ぉ':<14}"
    for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
        header += f"짹{t}%".rjust(9)
    print(header)
    print("-" * 78)

    pass_count = {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES}
    touch_count = {t: 0 for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES}

    for r in rows:
        line = f"{r['name']:<14}"
        if not r.get("enough"):
            for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
                line += "遺議?.rjust(8)
            print(line)
            continue
        for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
            touch = is_ma_touch(r["current_price"], r["ma60"], t)
            if touch:
                touch_count[t] += 1
            full = touch and r["bullish"] and r["vol_ok"]
            if full:
                pass_count[t] += 1
            # ?꾩껜?듦낵 O / ?곗튂留?t / ?꾨??덈씫 X
            mark = "O" if full else ("t" if touch else "X")
            line += mark.rjust(9)
        print(line)

    print("-" * 78)
    n_valid = sum(1 for r in rows if r.get("enough"))
    print(f"{'?곗튂留??듦낵':<14}", end="")
    for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
        print(f"{touch_count[t]}/{n_valid}".rjust(9), end="")
    print()
    print(f"{'?꾩껜議곌굔 ?듦낵':<14}", end="")
    for t in TOLERANCE_CANDIDATES:
        print(f"{pass_count[t]}/{n_valid}".rjust(9), end="")
    print()

    print("\n踰붾?: O=?꾩껜議곌굔 ?듦낵 / t=60MA ?곗튂???덉쑝???묐큺쨌嫄곕옒?됱뿉???덈씫 / X=?곗튂 ?ㅽ뙣")
    print("?????쒖옉 ???ㅽ뻾 ??吏곸쟾 嫄곕옒??留됲뙋 湲곗? ???⑤윭?곗뒪 誘쇨컧???뚯븙??)
    print("\n???꾨즺")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
