"""Phase3Controller ?⑥쐞 ?뚯뒪??""
import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from core.strategy.phase3_controller import (
    Phase3Controller, Phase3State, HOLD_DURATION, MAX_TOTAL_WAIT,
)


def _make_ctrl(start: datetime = None):
    now_holder = [start or datetime(2026, 5, 19, 11, 0, 0)]
    ctrl = Phase3Controller(now_func=lambda: now_holder[0])
    ctrl._set_now = lambda t: now_holder.__setitem__(0, t)
    return ctrl


def _trade(code, strength):
    return {"stock_code": code, "strength": strength, "price": 1000, "side": "buy"}


def t1_normal_flow():
    print("\n[1] ?뺤긽 ?먮쫫 (120??50??80??遺?hold?뭃EADY)")
    base = datetime(2026, 5, 19, 11, 0, 0)
    ctrl = _make_ctrl(base)
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")

    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.WATCHING_150
    print(f"  ??120 ?듦낵 ??WATCHING_150")

    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 155))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.WATCHING_180
    print(f"  ??150 ?듦낵 ??WATCHING_180")

    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 185))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.HOLD_180
    print(f"  ??180 ?꾨떖 ??HOLD_180")

    # 1遺?寃쎄낵
    ctrl._set_now(base + timedelta(seconds=61))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 190))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.READY_TO_BUY
    print(f"  ??1遺?????READY_TO_BUY")


def t2_120_retreat():
    print("\n[2] 120 ?꾨떖 ???꾪눜 ???먭린")
    ctrl = _make_ctrl()
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 115))   # 120 誘몃쭔
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.ABANDONED
    print(f"  ??120 ?꾪눜 (115) ??ABANDONED")


def t3_150_retreat():
    print("\n[3] 150 ?꾨떖 ???꾪눜 ???먭린")
    ctrl = _make_ctrl()
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 155))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 145))   # 150 誘몃쭔
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.ABANDONED
    print(f"  ??150 ?꾪눜 (145) ??ABANDONED")


def t4_180_retreat():
    print("\n[4] 180 ?꾨떖 ???꾪눜 ???먭린")
    ctrl = _make_ctrl()
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 155))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 185))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 175))   # 180 誘몃쭔
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.ABANDONED
    print(f"  ??180 ?꾪눜 (175) ??ABANDONED")


def t5_jump_to_180():
    print("\n[5] ??踰덉뿉 180 ?먰봽")
    base = datetime(2026, 5, 19, 11, 0, 0)
    ctrl = _make_ctrl(base)
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 200))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.HOLD_180
    print(f"  ??120??80 ?먰봽 ??HOLD_180")

    ctrl._set_now(base + timedelta(seconds=61))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 200))
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.READY_TO_BUY
    print(f"  ??1遺?????READY_TO_BUY")


def t6_total_timeout():
    print("\n[6] 5遺??덉뿉 180 紐?李띿쓬 ???먭린")
    base = datetime(2026, 5, 19, 11, 0, 0)
    ctrl = _make_ctrl(base)
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))   # WATCHING_150 ?뺤껜

    ctrl._set_now(base + MAX_TOTAL_WAIT + timedelta(seconds=1))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 145))   # 150 誘몃떖
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.ABANDONED
    print(f"  ??5遺? 珥덇낵 ??ABANDONED")


def t7_tick_ready_without_trade():
    print("\n[7] HOLD 以?泥닿껐 ?놁씠 1遺?寃쎄낵 ??tick?쇰줈 READY")
    base = datetime(2026, 5, 19, 11, 0, 0)
    ctrl = _make_ctrl(base)
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 200))   # HOLD_180

    # 60珥?寃쎄낵 ??tick留??몄텧 (異붽? 泥닿껐 ?놁쓬)
    ctrl._set_now(base + timedelta(seconds=61))
    ready = ctrl.tick()
    assert "005930" in ready
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.READY_TO_BUY
    print(f"  ??泥닿껐 ?놁씠 tick?쇰줈 READY 媛??)


def t8_is_watching_excludes_done():
    print("\n[8] is_watching - READY/ABANDONED ?쒖쇅")
    ctrl = _make_ctrl()
    ctrl.start_watching("005930")
    assert ctrl.is_watching("005930")

    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 115))   # ?쒖옉遺??120 誘몃떖 ??蹂???놁쓬
    assert ctrl.get_state("005930") == Phase3State.WATCHING_120
    assert ctrl.is_watching("005930")
    print(f"  ??WATCHING_120 ?곹깭 = is_watching True")

    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 125))
    ctrl.on_trade(_trade("005930", 115))   # ?꾪눜 ??ABANDONED
    assert not ctrl.is_watching("005930")
    print(f"  ??ABANDONED ??is_watching False")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Phase3Controller 寃利?)
    print("=" * 60)
    try:
        t1_normal_flow()
        t2_120_retreat()
        t3_150_retreat()
        t4_180_retreat()
        t5_jump_to_180()
        t6_total_timeout()
        t7_tick_ready_without_trade()
        t8_is_watching_excludes_done()
        print("\n" + "=" * 60)
        print("???꾩껜 ?듦낵 (8媛?")
        print("=" * 60)
    except AssertionError as e:
        print(f"\n??寃利??ㅽ뙣: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n???덉쇅: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_portfolio_optimizer.py ===

"""PortfolioOptimizer ?⑥쐞 ?뚯뒪??""
import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch
from core.strategy.portfolio_optimizer import (
    PortfolioOptimizer, kelly_fraction, compute_atr, _trade_profit,
)


def _candles(opens, highs, lows, closes, vols=None):
    """oldest?뭤ewest ?낅젰 ??newest-first 諛섑솚"""
    n = len(opens)
    if vols is None:
        vols = [1000] * n
    oldest_first = [
        {"open": opens[i], "high": highs[i], "low": lows[i],
         "close": closes[i], "volume": vols[i]}
        for i in range(n)
    ]
    return list(reversed(oldest_first))


def t1_kelly_basic():
    print("\n[1] 耳덈━ 怨듭떇")
    # ?밸쪧 60%, ?됯퇏?댁씡 200, ?됯퇏?먯떎 100 ??b=2, p=0.6
    # f* = (0.6*2 - 0.4)/2 = 0.4 ??cap 0.25 ?곸슜
    f = kelly_fraction(0.6, 200, 100, max_fraction=0.25)
    assert abs(f - 0.25) < 1e-6
    print(f"  ???밸쪧60%/?먯씡鍮? ??cap ??f*={f}")

    # ?먯씡鍮?1, ?밸쪧 50% ??f*=0
    f = kelly_fraction(0.5, 100, 100)
    assert f == 0.0
    print(f"  ??臾댁쐞??踰좏똿 ??f*=0")

    # ?먯떎 湲곕? ?쒕굹由ъ삤
    f = kelly_fraction(0.3, 100, 200)
    assert f == 0.0
    print(f"  ???먯떎 湲곕? ??f*=0")

    # ?뺤긽 遺꾩닔 耳덈━
    # ?밸쪧 55%, ?먯씡鍮?1.5 ??b=1.5, p=0.55, q=0.45
    # f* = (0.55*1.5 - 0.45)/1.5 = 0.375/1.5 = 0.25 (=cap)
    # ?밸쪧 55%, ?먯씡鍮?1.2 ??b=1.2, f* = (0.55*1.2 - 0.45)/1.2 = 0.175
    f = kelly_fraction(0.55, 120, 100)
    assert abs(f - 0.175) < 0.01
    print(f"  ???밸쪧55%/?먯씡鍮?.2 ??f*={f:.3f}")


def t2_atr():
    print("\n[2] ATR 怨꾩궛")
    candles = _candles(
        opens=[100]*15, highs=[105]*15, lows=[100]*15, closes=[102]*15,
    )
    atr = compute_atr(candles, period=14)
    assert atr is not None
    assert 4.5 <= atr <= 5.5, f"got {atr}"
    print(f"  ???쇱젙 蹂?숈꽦 ??ATR={atr:.2f}")

    # 遺議?遺꾨큺
    short = _candles(opens=[100]*5, highs=[101]*5, lows=[99]*5, closes=[100]*5)
    assert compute_atr(short, period=14) is None
    print(f"  ??遺꾨큺 遺議???None")


def t3_trade_profit_extraction():
    print("\n[3] 嫄곕옒 ?먯씡 異붿텧 (?ㅼ뼇??而щ읆)")
    # profit_amount ?덈뒗 寃쎌슦
    p = _trade_profit({"profit_amount": 1234})
    assert p == 1234.0
    # ?놁쑝硫?怨꾩궛
    p = _trade_profit({"sell_price": 1100, "buy_price": 1000, "buy_quantity": 10})
    assert p == 1000.0
    # ???놁쑝硫?None
    p = _trade_profit({})
    assert p is None
    print(f"  ??3媛吏 而щ읆 ?⑦꽩 泥섎━")


def t4_volatility_high_low():
    print("\n[4] 蹂?숈꽦 multiplier: ?믪? 蹂?숈꽦 ???묒? 鍮꾩쨷, ??? 蹂?숈꽦 ????鍮꾩쨷")
    opt = PortfolioOptimizer(rest_api=MagicMock(), target_volatility=0.02)

    # 蹂?숈꽦 4% 醫낅ぉ (high-low=4, close=100 ??atr??%)
    opt.api.get_minute_candles.return_value = _candles(
        opens=[100]*30, highs=[104]*30, lows=[100]*30, closes=[100]*30,
    )
    mult, pct = opt._compute_volatility("AAA")
    assert mult is not None and mult < 1.0
    print(f"  ??蹂?숈꽦 {pct*100:.2f}% ??{mult:.2f}x (?묒븘吏?")

    # 蹂?숈꽦 1% 醫낅ぉ
    opt.api.get_minute_candles.return_value = _candles(
        opens=[100]*30, highs=[101]*30, lows=[100]*30, closes=[100]*30,
    )
    mult2, pct2 = opt._compute_volatility("BBB")
    assert mult2 is not None and mult2 > 1.0
    print(f"  ??蹂?숈꽦 {pct2*100:.2f}% ??{mult2:.2f}x (而ㅼ쭚)")


def t5_kelly_insufficient_data():
    print("\n[5] 耳덈━ ?곗씠??遺議???multiplier=1.0")
    opt = PortfolioOptimizer(rest_api=MagicMock(), min_trades_for_kelly=20)

    with patch("core.strategy.portfolio_optimizer.TradeRepository") as mt:
        mt.find_closed_by_substrategy.return_value = [
            {"profit_amount": 100, "buy_quantity": 10}
        ] * 5  # 5嫄대쭔 (20 誘몃쭔)
        f = opt._compute_kelly("1A")
        assert f is None
    print(f"  ??5嫄?< 20嫄???Kelly None")


def t6_kelly_with_data():
    print("\n[6] 耳덈━ ?곗씠??異⑸텇 ??怨꾩궛 ?숈옉")
    opt = PortfolioOptimizer(rest_api=MagicMock(), min_trades_for_kelly=10)

    # ?밸쪧 60% (12??8??, ?됯퇏?댁씡 200, ?됯퇏?먯떎 100
    trades = [{"profit_amount": 200, "buy_quantity": 10}] * 12 + \
             [{"profit_amount": -100, "buy_quantity": 10}] * 8

    with patch("core.strategy.portfolio_optimizer.TradeRepository") as mt:
        mt.find_closed_by_substrategy.return_value = trades
        f = opt._compute_kelly("1A")
        assert f is not None
        assert 0 < f <= opt.kelly_cap
    print(f"  ??20嫄??곗씠????f*={f:.3f}")


def t7_integration():
    print("\n[7] ?듯빀 怨꾩궛 (Kelly None + ?뺤긽 Vol)")
    opt = PortfolioOptimizer(
        rest_api=MagicMock(),
        base_amount=2_000_000,
    )
    opt.api.get_minute_candles.return_value = _candles(
        opens=[1000]*30, highs=[1010]*30, lows=[1000]*30, closes=[1000]*30,
    )

    with patch("core.strategy.portfolio_optimizer.TradeRepository") as mt:
        mt.find_closed_by_substrategy.return_value = []
        info = opt.calculate_position_amount("005930", "1A")

    assert info["kelly_fraction"] is None
    assert info["kelly_multiplier"] == 1.0
    assert info["amount"] > 0
    assert info["amount"] % 1000 == 0  # 1000???⑥쐞
    print(f"  ??amount={info['amount']:,}?? weight={info['final_weight']:.2f}x")
    for r in info["reasons"]:
        print(f"     쨌 {r}")


def t8_clipping():

    print(f"  ???ㅻ뒛 由ъ뒪??{len(todays)}嫄?)


def t4_trade_lifecycle():
    print("\n[4] trades ?쇱씠?꾩궗?댄겢 (留ㅼ닔?믩ℓ??")
    tid = TradeRepository.insert_buy(
        stock_code="005930",
        stock_name=TEST_MARKER,
        buy_price=73500,
        buy_quantity=27,
        strategy_phase=1,
        entry_reason="Phase1 5MA ?곗튂 ?묐큺",
    )
    print(f"  ??buy id={tid}")

    holdings = TradeRepository.find_holdings()
    assert any(h["id"] == tid for h in holdings)
    print(f"  ??holdings {len(holdings)}嫄?)

    TradeRepository.update_sell(
        trade_id=tid,
        sell_price=75300,
        sell_quantity=27,
        exit_reason="?듭젅 +2.5%",
        fee=500,
        tax=130,
    )
    closed = TradeRepository.find_by_id(tid)
    assert closed["status"] == "closed"
    print(f"  ??sell ?꾨즺 / ?섏씡瑜?{float(closed['profit_rate']):.2f}% / ?섏씡 {float(closed['profit_amount']):,.0f}??)

    print("\n[5] daily_summary")
    today = date.today()
    sid = DailySummaryRepository.upsert(today, {
        "total_trades": 5,
        "winning_trades": 3,
        "losing_trades": 2,
        "win_rate": 60.0,
        "net_profit": 50000,
    })
    assert sid is not None
    print(f"  ??upsert (insert) id={sid}")

    DailySummaryRepository.upsert(today, {
        "total_trades": 6,
        "win_rate": 66.6,
    })
    print(f"  ??upsert (update)")

    s = DailySummaryRepository.find_by_date(today)
    assert s["total_trades"] == 6
    print(f"  ??議고쉶: total_trades={s['total_trades']}")


def cleanup():
    """TEST_MARKER ?ㅼ뼱媛?row留??뺣━"""
    print("\n[6] ?뚯뒪???곗씠???뺣━")
    with get_cursor() as cur:
        cur.execute("DELETE FROM trades WHERE stock_name = %s", (TEST_MARKER,))
        n1 = cur.rowcount
        cur.execute("DELETE FROM watch_list_log WHERE stock_name = %s", (TEST_MARKER,))
        n2 = cur.rowcount
        cur.execute("DELETE FROM system_events WHERE event_message = %s", (TEST_MARKER,))
        n3 = cur.rowcount
        cur.execute(
            "DELETE FROM daily_summary WHERE trade_date = %s AND total_trades = 6",
            (date.today(),),
        )
        n4 = cur.rowcount
    print(f"  ??trades={n1}, watch={n2}, events={n3}, summary={n4}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Repository 寃利??쒖옉")

        t1_connection()

        print(f"\n??寃利??ㅽ뙣: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n???덉쇅: {e}")
        import traceback; traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)
    finally:
        close_pool()

def main():
    print("=" * 50)
    print("?㎦ KiwoomREST ?⑤룆 ?뚯뒪??)
    print("=" * 50)

    # 1) ?좏겙
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return

    rest = KiwoomREST(token, is_mock=True)

    # 2) ?덉닔湲?議고쉶
    print("\n[1] ?덉닔湲?議고쉶")
    deposit = rest.get_deposit()
    print(f"  return_code: {deposit.get('return_code')}")
    print(f"  ?덉닔湲?        {rest._safe_int(deposit.get('entr')):>12,} ??)

    # 3) 二쇰Ц媛?κ툑?〓쭔 源붾걫?섍쾶
    print(f"\n[2] 二쇰Ц媛?κ툑??(?ы띁): {rest.get_orderable_amount():,} ??)

    # 4) 蹂댁쑀醫낅ぉ
    print("\n[3] 蹂댁쑀醫낅ぉ 議고쉶")
    holdings = rest.get_holdings()
    if holdings:
        for code, info in holdings.items():
            print(f"  {info['name']} ({code}): "
                  f"{info['qty']}二?@ {info['avg_price']:,}??"

    else:
        print("  蹂댁쑀醫낅ぉ ?놁쓬")

    # 5) ?꾩옱媛 議고쉶 (?쇱꽦?꾩옄)
    print("\n[4] ?쇱꽦?꾩옄(005930) ?꾩옱媛")
    price = rest.get_current_price("005930")
    print(f"  ?꾩옱媛: {price:,} ??)

    # 6) ?좑툘 留ㅼ닔 二쇰Ц ?뚯뒪??(紐⑥쓽?ъ옄?먯꽌留?)
    #    ?ㅽ뻾?섍퀬 ?띠쑝硫??꾨옒 二쇱꽍 ?댁젣
    # print("\n[5] ?쇱꽦?꾩옄 1二??쒖옣媛 留ㅼ닔 (紐⑥쓽?ъ옄)")
    # result = rest.buy_market_order("005930", qty=1, trde_tp="3")
    # print(f"  寃곌낵: {result}")

    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("?뚯뒪??醫낅즺")
    print("=" * 50)


if __name__ == "__main__":

"""StrategyManager ?⑥쐞 ?뚯뒪??(API/二쇰Ц 紐⑦궧) ??5/19 ?⑥튂 諛섏쁺"""
import sys, os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from datetime import datetime, time, timedelta
from unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch

from core.strategy_manager import (
    StrategyManager, PHASE1_START, PHASE1_END, PHASE2_END,
    POSITION_AMOUNT, MAX_HOLDINGS, MAX_SELL_FAIL, REBUY_COOLDOWN, RESTART_WARMUP,
    TRAILING_ARM_RATE, TRAILING_DROP, TRAILING_MIN_PROFIT,
)
from core.strategy.chemul_evaluator import ChemulState


def _make_sm(now_dt: datetime, optimizer=None):
    """DB 蹂듭썝 ?고쉶??StrategyManager ?앹꽦"""
    sm = StrategyManager.__new__(StrategyManager)
    sm.api = MagicMock()
    sm.order_manager = MagicMock()
    sm.phase1b = None
    sm.phase3 = None
    sm.optimizer = optimizer
    sm._now = lambda: now_dt
    sm.holdings = {}
    sm.watch_list_today = set()
    sm.pending = set()
    sm._stock_names = {}
    sm._sell_fail_count = {}
    sm._sell_blocked = set()
    sm._sold_at = {}
    return sm


def _make_sm_with_phase1b(now_dt: datetime, phase1b=None, optimizer=None):
    sm = StrategyManager.__new__(StrategyManager)
    sm.api = MagicMock()
    sm.order_manager = MagicMock()
    sm.phase1b = phase1b or MagicMock()
    sm.phase3 = None
    sm.optimizer = optimizer
    sm._now = lambda: now_dt
    sm.holdings = {}
    sm.watch_list_today = set()
    sm.pending = set()
    sm._stock_names = {}
    sm._sell_fail_count = {}
    sm._sell_blocked = set()
    sm._sold_at = {}
    return sm

def _build_candles(open_price, closes, volumes):
    oldest_first = [{"open": open_price, "close": open_price,
                     "high": open_price, "low": open_price,
                     "volume": volumes[0]}]
    prev_close = open_price
    for c, v in zip(closes, volumes[1:]):
        oldest_first.append({
            "open": prev_close, "close": c,
            "high": max(prev_close, c), "low": min(prev_close, c),
            "volume": v,
        })
        prev_close = c
    return list(reversed(oldest_first))


def _make_position(buy_price=1000, buy_time=None, warmup_until=None,
                   sub_strategy="1A", quantity=10, highest=None):
    return {
        "trade_id": 99,
        "buy_price": buy_price,
        "buy_quantity": quantity,
        "buy_time": buy_time or datetime.now(),
        "stock_name": "?뚯뒪??,
        "strategy_phase": 1,
        "sub_strategy": sub_strategy,
        "highest_price": highest or buy_price,
        "trailing_armed": False,
        "position_weight": 1.0,
        "warmup_until": warmup_until,
    }


def t1_phase_detection():
    print("\n[1] Phase ?쒓컙? ?먮퀎")
    cases = [
        (time(8, 59),  None),  # ???쒖옉 ??
        (time(9, 0),   1),     # Phase 1A ?쒖옉
        (time(9, 19),  1),     # Phase 1A
        (time(9, 20),  None),  # ??09:20~09:21 怨듬갚 (?섎룄??
        (time(9, 21),  2),     # ??Phase 2 ?쒖옉
        (time(10, 39), 2),     # Phase 2
        (time(10, 40), None),  # ??10:40~10:41 怨듬갚 (?섎룄??
        (time(10, 41), 3),     # ??Phase 3 ?쒖옉
        (time(14, 59), 3),     # ??Phase 3
        (time(15, 0),  None),  # ??Phase 3 醫낅즺
        (time(15, 30), None),  # ??留덇컧 ??
    ]
    for t, expected in cases:
        sm = _make_sm(datetime.combine(datetime.today(), t))
        assert sm.get_current_phase() == expected, f"{t} expected {expected}, got {sm.get_current_phase()}"
        print(f"  ??{t} ??{expected}")
   


def t2_volume_ratio():
    print("\n[2] 嫄곕옒??鍮꾩쑉")
    sm = _make_sm(datetime.now())
    candles = _build_candles(100, [100]*6, [1000]*6 + [2000])
    ratio = sm._volume_ratio(candles)
    assert abs(ratio - 2.0) < 0.01
    print(f"  ??{ratio:.2f}諛?)

    ok, info = sm.evaluate_phase1(c)

def t6_exit_signals():
    """5/19 ?⑥튂: ?몃젅?쇰쭅 臾댁옣 +1.5%, drop -1.2%, min_profit +0.5%"""
    print("\n[6] ?섏씠釉뚮━??泥?궛 (5/19 ?⑥튂 諛섏쁺)")
    base = datetime.now()
    def fresh():
        sm = _make_sm(base)
        sm.holdings["005930"] = _make_position(buy_price=1000, buy_time=base)
        sm._execute_sell = MagicMock()
        return sm

    # ?먯젅 -1.5% ??985???댄븯
    sm = fresh(); sm.on_price_update("005930", 984)
    assert sm._execute_sell.called and "?먯젅" in sm._execute_sell.call_args[0][2]
    print(f"  ???먯젅 (984?? -1.6%)")

    # ?듭젅 罹?+2.5% ??1025???댁긽
    sm = fresh(); sm.on_price_update("005930", 1026)
    assert sm._execute_sell.called and "?듭젅 罹? in sm._execute_sell.call_args[0][2]
    print(f"  ???듭젅 罹?(1026?? +2.6%)")

    # ?몃젅?쇰쭅 臾댁옣 (+1.5%) but 泥?궛 X (drop 誘몃떖)
    sm = fresh(); sm.on_price_update("005930", 1015)  # +1.5%
    assert not sm._execute_sell.called
    assert sm.holdings["005930"]["trailing_armed"] is True
    print(f"  ???몃젅?쇰쭅 臾댁옣留?(1015?? +1.5%)")

    # 臾댁옣 誘몃떖 (+1.2%) ??5/19 ?⑥튂濡?+1.5% 誘몃쭔? 臾댁옣 X
    sm = fresh(); sm.on_price_update("005930", 1012)
    assert not sm._execute_sell.called
    assert sm.holdings["005930"]["trailing_armed"] is False
    print(f"  ??臾댁옣 誘몃떖 (1012?? +1.2% < +1.5%)")

    # ?몃젅?쇰쭅 泥?궛: +2% 臾댁옣 ??-1.2% drop & rate +0.5% ?댁긽
    sm = fresh()
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1020)   # +2% 臾댁옣, 怨좎젏=1020
    sm._execute_sell.reset_mock()
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1006)   # drop=1.37%, rate=+0.6%
    assert sm._execute_sell.called and "?몃젅?쇰쭅" in sm._execute_sell.call_args[0][2]
    print(f"  ???몃젅?쇰쭅 泥?궛 (1020??006, drop 1.37% + rate +0.6%)")

    # ???좉퇋: min_profit 誘몃떖 ???몃젅?쇰쭅 泥?궛 李⑤떒
    sm = fresh()
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1020)   # +2% 臾댁옣
    sm._execute_sell.reset_mock()
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1003)   # drop=1.67%, rate=+0.3% < +0.5%
    assert not sm._execute_sell.called
    print(f"  ???몃젅?쇰쭅 李⑤떒 (rate +0.3% < min_profit +0.5%)")

    # ?쒓컙?뺣━
    sm = fresh(); sm._now = lambda: base + timedelta(minutes=31)
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1005)
    assert sm._execute_sell.called and "?쒓컙?뺣━" in sm._execute_sell.call_args[0][2]
    print(f"  ???쒓컙?뺣━ (31遺?寃쎄낵)")


def t7_buy_flow_integration():
    print("\n[7] 留ㅼ닔 ?뚮줈??(optimizer ?놁쓬)")

        100, [103, 105, 105, 106, 104, 105], [1000]*6 + [2000]
    )
    sm.order_manager.buy.return_value = {"success": True}

    with patch("core.strategy_manager.TradeRepository") as mt, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.WatchListRepository") as mw, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.SystemEventRepository"):
        mt.insert_buy.return_value = 123
        mw.find_by_date.return_value = []
        sm.on_condition_hit("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄")

    assert "005930" in sm.holdings
    assert sm.holdings["005930"]["sub_strategy"] == "1A"
    expected_qty = int(POSITION_AMOUNT // 105)

def t15_sell_failure_blocking():
    """留ㅻ룄 3???ㅽ뙣 ??holdings ?쒓굅 + sell_blocked"""
    print("\n[15] 留ㅻ룄 ?ㅽ뙣 泥섎━ (3???ㅽ뙣 ??李⑤떒)")
    base = datetime.now()
    sm = _make_sm(base)
    sm.holdings["005930"] = _make_position(buy_price=1000, buy_time=base)
    sm.order_manager.sell.return_value = {"success": False, "error": "?붽퀬 遺議?}

    with patch("core.strategy_manager.TradeRepository"), \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.SystemEventRepository"):
        # 1???ㅽ뙣
        sm._execute_sell("005930", 985, "?뚯뒪??)
        assert sm._sell_fail_count["005930"] == 1
        assert "005930" in sm.holdings
        assert "005930" not in sm._sell_blocked
        print(f"  ??1???ㅽ뙣: 移댁슫??1, holdings ?좎?")

        # 2???ㅽ뙣
        sm._execute_sell("005930", 985, "?뚯뒪??)
        assert sm._sell_fail_count["005930"] == 2
        assert "005930" in sm.holdings
        print(f"  ??2???ㅽ뙣: 移댁슫??2, holdings ?좎?")

        # 3???ㅽ뙣 ??李⑤떒 + ?쒓굅
        sm._execute_sell("005930", 985, "?뚯뒪??)
        assert sm._sell_fail_count["005930"] == 3
        assert "005930" in sm._sell_blocked
        assert "005930" not in sm.holdings
        print(f"  ??3???ㅽ뙣: 李⑤떒 + holdings ?쒓굅")

    # 李⑤떒 醫낅ぉ? ???댁긽 泥?궛 ?쒕룄 ????
    sm.order_manager.sell.reset_mock()
    sm._execute_sell("005930", 985, "?뚯뒪??)
    sm.order_manager.sell.assert_not_called()
    print(f"  ??李⑤떒 ??異붽? 留ㅻ룄 ?쒕룄 ?놁쓬")


def t16_rebuy_cooldown():
    """留ㅻ룄 ??10遺??숈븞 媛숈? 醫낅ぉ ?щℓ??李⑤떒"""
    print("\n[16] ?щℓ??荑⑤떎??)
    base = datetime.combine(datetime.today(), time(9, 5))
    sm = _make_sm_with_phase1b(base)
    sm.api.get_minute_candles.return_value = _build_candles(
        100, [103, 105, 105, 106, 104, 105], [1000]*6 + [2000]
    )

    # 留ㅻ룄 吏곹썑 留덊궧
    sm._sold_at["005930"] = base
    sm.phase1b.is_watching = MagicMock(return_value=False)

    with patch("core.strategy_manager.TradeRepository") as mt, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.WatchListRepository") as mw, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.SystemEventRepository"):
        mw.find_by_date.return_value = []
        sm.on_condition_hit("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄")

    # 荑⑤떎???붿뿬 ?숈븞? 留ㅼ닔 X
    assert "005930" not in sm.holdings
    sm.order_manager.buy.assert_not_called()
    print(f"  ??留ㅻ룄 吏곹썑: 留ㅼ닔 李⑤떒")

    # 荑⑤떎??醫낅즺 ??(10遺?1珥?寃쎄낵)
    sm._now = lambda: base + REBUY_COOLDOWN + timedelta(seconds=1)
    sm.order_manager.buy.return_value = {"success": True}
    with patch("core.strategy_manager.TradeRepository") as mt, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.WatchListRepository") as mw, \
         patch("core.strategy_manager.SystemEventRepository"):
        mt.insert_buy.return_value = 999
        mw.find_by_date.return_value = []
        sm.on_condition_hit("005930", "?쇱꽦?꾩옄")
    assert "005930" in sm.holdings
    print(f"  ??10遺?寃쎄낵 ?? 留ㅼ닔 OK")


def t17_restart_warmup():
    """?ъ떆????30珥??숈븞 泥?궛 ?됯? 蹂대쪟"""
    print("\n[17] ?ъ떆???뚮컢??)

    # ?뚮컢??以묒씤 ?ъ???(DB 蹂듭썝 吏곹썑 ?쒕??덉씠??
    sm.holdings["005930"] = _make_position(
        buy_price=1000, buy_time=base - timedelta(minutes=5),
        warmup_until=base + RESTART_WARMUP,
    )
    sm._execute_sell = MagicMock()

    # ?뚮컢??以? ?대뼡 媛寃⑸룄 泥?궛 諛쒕룞 X
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 984)   # ?먯젅 ?쇱씤
    assert not sm._execute_sell.called
    print(f"  ???뚮컢??以? ?먯젅 ?쇱씤(-1.6%)??泥?궛 ????)
    assert sm.holdings["005930"]["highest_price"] == 1000  # 984 < 1000
    
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 1050)  # ?듭젅 罹?珥덇낵
    assert not sm._execute_sell.called
    assert sm.holdings["005930"]["highest_price"] == 1050  # 媛깆떊? ??
    print(f"  ???뚮컢??以? ?듭젅 罹?+5%)??泥?궛 ???? 怨좎젏留?媛깆떊")

    # ?뚮컢??醫낅즺 ??
    sm._now = lambda: base + RESTART_WARMUP + timedelta(seconds=1)
    sm.on_price_update("005930", 984)
    assert sm._execute_sell.called
    print(f"  ??30珥?寃쎄낵 ?? ?먯젅 ?뺤긽 ?숈옉")

=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\test_ws.py ===

"""
WebSocket ?뚯뒪???ㅽ겕由쏀듃
- ?좏겙 諛쒓툒 ??WS ?곌껐 ??議곌굔??紐⑸줉 異쒕젰 ???ㅼ떆媛??깅줉 ???좏샇 ?湲?
"""
import asyncio
from api.auth import get_access_token
from api.kiwoom_ws import KiwoomWS
from config import settings


async def on_signal(stock_code, signal_type, raw):
    kind = "?몄엯" if signal_type == "I" else "?댄깉"
    print(f"?뱿 [{kind}] {stock_code}")


async def main():
    # 1) ?좏겙 諛쒓툒
    token = get_access_token()
    if not token:
        print("???좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?ㅽ뙣")
        return

    # 2) WS ?곌껐 (on_signal 肄쒕갚 ?깅줉)
    ws = KiwoomWS(token, is_mock=True, on_signal=on_signal)
    await ws.connect()

    # 3) 議곌굔??紐⑸줉 異쒕젰 (吏꾩쭨 踰덊샇 ?뺤씤??
    cond_map = await ws.fetch_condition_list()
    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("?뱥 ?ㅼ? ?쒕쾭???깅줉??議곌굔??紐⑸줉")
    print("=" * 50)
    for seq, name in cond_map.items():
        print(f"  seq={seq:>3}  ?? {name}")
    print("=" * 50 + "\n")

  # 4) 議곌굔???ㅼ떆媛??깅줉 - ?대쫫 湲곕컲 留ㅼ묶
    target_names = settings.CONDITION_NAMES
    target_seqs = []

    if target_names:
        print(f"?숋툘 ?깅줉??議곌굔?? {target_names}\n")
        # ?대쫫 ??seq ??ℓ移?
        name_to_seq = {name: seq for seq, name in cond_map.items()}
        for name in target_names:
            if name in name_to_seq:
                seq = name_to_seq[name]
                target_seqs.append(seq)
                print(f"   ??'{name}' ??seq={seq}")
            else:
                print(f"   ?좑툘 '{name}' ??瑜? 李얠? 紐삵뻽?듬땲??- ?곸썒臾?[0150] ?대쫫 ?뺤씤")
    else:
        # ?대갚: 踰덊샇 湲곕컲
        print(f"?숋툘 config.ini??議곌굔??踰덊샇濡??깅줉: {settings.CONDITION_NOS}\n")
        for seq in settings.CONDITION_NOS:
            seq = seq.strip()
            if seq in cond_map:
                target_seqs.append(seq)
            else:
                print(f"   ?좑툘 seq={seq} 媛 ?ㅼ? ?쒕쾭???놁뒿?덈떎")

    # ?깅줉 ?ㅽ뻾
    for seq in target_seqs:
        await ws.subscribe_condition(seq)
   
    # 5) 臾댄븳 ?섏떊 猷⑦봽
    await ws.listen()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        asyncio.run(main())
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n?몝 醫낅즺")

"""KiwoomWS ?ㅻ깄??+ 鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳 + main ?듯빀 ?⑥쐞 ?뚯뒪??""
import sys, os, asyncio
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

from unittest.mock import MagicMock, AsyncMock, patch
from api.kiwoom_ws import KiwoomWS, REG_INTERVAL_SEC


def _run(coro):
    return asyncio.run(coro)


def _make_ws():
    """?뚯뒪?몄슜 KiwoomWS ?몄뒪?댁뒪 (?ㅼ젣 ?곌껐 ?놁쓬)"""
    ws = KiwoomWS(token="test_token", is_mock=True)
    ws.ws = AsyncMock()
    ws.connected = True
    return ws


# ?????????????????????????????????????????????
# fetch_condition_snapshot
# ?????????????????????????????????????????????
def t1_snapshot_normal_response():
    print("\n[1] 議곌굔???ㅻ깄??- ?뺤긽 ?묐떟 (3醫낅ぉ)")

    async def run():
        ws = _make_ws()
        ws.condition_map = {"6": "?μ쨷湲됰벑?⑦?"}
        fake_response = {
            "trnm": "CNSRREQ",
            "data": [
                {"9001": "A005930"},
                {"9001": "A035720"},
                {"9001": "A000660"},
            ],
        }
        ws._wait_for = AsyncMock(return_value=fake_response)
        ws._send = AsyncMock()
        return await ws.fetch_condition_snapshot("6")

    codes = _run(run())
    assert codes == ["005930", "035720", "000660"], f"got {codes}"
    print(f"  ??3醫낅ぉ 異붿텧 + 'A' ?묐몢???쒓굅: {codes}")

    assert codes == [], f"got {codes}"
    print(f"  ??鍮?由ъ뒪??)

def t5_snapshot_dict_response():

# subscribe_realtime 鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳
# ?????????????????????????????????????????????
def t6_reg_rate_limit():
    print(f"\n[6] subscribe_realtime - ?곗냽 ?몄텧 ??{REG_INTERVAL_SEC*1000:.0f}ms 媛꾧꺽 蹂댁옣")

    async def run():
        ws = _make_ws()

        timestamps = []
        async def track_send(payload):
            timestamps.append(asyncio.get_event_loop().time())
        ws._send = track_send

        await ws.subscribe_realtime(["005930"], ["0B", "0D"])
        await ws.subscribe_realtime(["035720"], ["0B", "0D"])
        await ws.subscribe_realtime(["000660"], ["0B", "0D"])

        return timestamps

    timestamps = _run(run())
    assert len(timestamps) == 3
    gap1 = timestamps[1] - timestamps[0]
    gap2 = timestamps[2] - timestamps[1]
    assert gap1 >= REG_INTERVAL_SEC - 0.05, f"gap1={gap1}"
    assert gap2 >= REG_INTERVAL_SEC - 0.05, f"gap2={gap2}"
    print(f"  ??媛꾧꺽: {gap1*1000:.0f}ms, {gap2*1000:.0f}ms (??REG_INTERVAL_SEC*1000:.0f}ms)")


def t7_reg_first_call_immediate():
    print("\n[7] subscribe_realtime - 泥??몄텧? 利됱떆")

    async def run():
        ws = _make_ws()
        ws._send = AsyncMock()

        start = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()
        await ws.subscribe_realtime(["005930"], ["0B", "0D"])
        return asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start

    elapsed = _run(run())
    assert elapsed < 0.1, f"泥??몄텧??{elapsed*1000:.0f}ms 嫄몃┝"
    print(f"  ??泥??몄텧 {elapsed*1000:.1f}ms (sleep ?놁쓬)")

def t8_initial_snapshot_integration():
    print("\n[8] _process_initial_snapshot - ?듯빀 ?먮쫫 (以묐났 ?쒓굅, 留ㅼ닔 ?됯?, 援щ룆)")

    async def run():
        from main import TradingBot

        bot = TradingBot()

        bot.ws = MagicMock()
        bot.ws.condition_map = {"6": "?μ쨷湲됰벑?⑦?", "7": "?꾨줈遺덇린?λ떒?"}
        # 議곌굔??6怨?7?먯꽌 035720 以묐났
        bot.ws.fetch_condition_snapshot = AsyncMock(side_effect=[
            ["005930", "035720"],
            ["035720", "000660"],
        ])
        bot.ws.subscribe_realtime = AsyncMock()

        bot.strategy_mgr = MagicMock()

        bot.order_mgr = MagicMock()
        bot.order_mgr.get_stock_name = MagicMock(side_effect=lambda c: {
            "005930": "?쇱꽦?꾩옄",
            "035720": "移댁뭅??,
            "000660": "SK?섏씠?됱뒪",
        }.get(c, c))

        with patch("main.settings") as ms, \
             patch("main.SNAPSHOT_STAGGER_SEC", 0):  # ?뚯뒪???띾룄
            ms.CONDITION_NAMES = ["?μ쨷湲됰벑?⑦?", "?꾨줈遺덇린?λ떒?"]
            await bot._process_initial_snapshot()

        return bot

    bot = _run(run())

    # ?ㅻ깄??移댁슫?? 以묐났 ?쒓굅?섏뼱 3
    assert bot._signal_stats["snapshot"] == 3, f"got {bot._signal_stats}"
    print(f"  ??snapshot 移댁슫?? 3 (035720 以묐났 ?쒓굅)")

    # on_condition_hit 3踰?
    calls = bot.strategy_mgr.on_condition_hit.call_args_list
    assert len(calls) == 3, f"got {len(calls)}"
    actual_codes = {c.args[0] for c in calls}
    assert actual_codes == {"005930", "035720", "000660"}
    print(f"  ??on_condition_hit 3踰??몄텧: {sorted(actual_codes)}")

    # 醫낅ぉ紐??뺥솗???꾨떖
    code_name = {c.args[0]: c.args[1] for c in calls}
    assert code_name["005930"] == "?쇱꽦?꾩옄"
    assert code_name["035720"] == "移댁뭅??
    assert code_name["000660"] == "SK?섏씠?됱뒪"
    print(f"  ??醫낅ぉ紐?REST 議고쉶 fallback ?숈옉")

    # subscribe_realtime 3踰?
    sub_calls = bot.ws.subscribe_realtime.call_args_list
    assert len(sub_calls) == 3
    print(f"  ??subscribe_realtime 3踰??몄텧 (以묐났 ?놁쓬)")

import ast
import re
import sys
from pathlib import Path

ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent


def find(name: str, prefer_subdir: str = None):
    cands = []
    if prefer_subdir:
        cands.append(ROOT / prefer_subdir / name)
    cands.append(ROOT / name)
    for c in cands:
        if c.is_file():
            return c
    for p in ROOT.rglob(name):           # 理쒗썑?섎떒: ?ш? 寃??(.history ?쒖쇅)
        if ".history" not in p.parts:
            return p
    return None


def read(p):
    if not p:
        return ""
    try:
        return p.read_text(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
    except Exception:
        return ""


results = []  # (?뚯씪, ??ぉ, ?듦낵?щ?, 鍮꾧퀬)


def check(file, label, ok, detail=""):
    results.append((file, label, bool(ok), detail))


# ?? ?뚯씪 ?꾩튂 ??
f_ini = find("config.ini")

check("config.ini", "??SURGE_CONDITION_NAMES ?뺤쓽+媛?,
      bool(m and m.group(1).strip()),
      (m.group(1).strip() if m else "?놁쓬"))

      not re.search(r"PHASE1_END\s*=\s*time\(\s*9\s*,\s*20\s*\)", t))

    if file != cur:
        cur = file

        passed += 1
        mark = f"{GREEN}??RST}"
    else:
        failed += 1
        mark = f"{RED}??RST}"
    extra = f"  {DIM}({detail}){RST}" if detail and (not ok or "媛? in label or "諛쒓껄" in label) else ""
    print(f"  {mark} {label}{extra}")

                 ("core/strategy_manager.py", f_sm), ("config/settings.py", f_set)]:
    if not p:
        print(f"  {RED}??RST} {label}: ?뚯씪 紐?李얠쓬")
        syntax_fail += 1
        continue
    try:
        ast.parse(read(p), filename=str(p))
        print(f"  {GREEN}??RST} {label}: 臾몃쾿 OK")
    except SyntaxError as e:
        print(f"  {RED}??RST} {label}: 臾몃쾿 ?ㅻ쪟 ??{e.lineno}踰?以? {e.msg}")
        syntax_fail += 1

# ?? 醫낇빀 ??
print("\n" + "=" * 60)
print(f"  ??ぉ: {passed}媛??듦낵 / {failed}媛??ㅽ뙣   |   臾몃쾿?ㅻ쪟: {syntax_fail}媛?)
if failed == 0 and syntax_fail == 0:
    print(f"  {GREEN}?꾨? ?듦낵! 媛쒖옣 ??'python main.py'濡??뚮젮遊?{RST}")
else:

import requests
import json
from config import settings
from utils.logger import logger


def get_access_token():
    """?ㅼ? REST API 紐⑥쓽?ъ옄???묎렐?좏겙 諛쒓툒"""
    url = "https://mockapi.kiwoom.com/oauth2/token"

    payload = {
        "grant_type": "client_credentials",
        "appkey": settings.APP_KEY,
        "secretkey": settings.SECRET_KEY,
    }
    headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json;charset=UTF-8"}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, json=payload, headers=headers, timeout=10)
        res_json = response.json()

        token = res_json.get("token")

        if token:
            logger.info("?뵎 [?깃났] 紐⑥쓽?ъ옄??REST API ?좏겙 諛쒓툒 ?꾨즺!")
            return token
        else:
            logger.error(f"???좏겙??李얠? 紐삵뻽?듬땲?? {res_json.get('return_msg')}")
            return None

    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"???몄쬆 ?쒕쾭 ?곌껐 ?ㅻ쪟: {e}")
        return None


def send_telegram(message, target='signal'):
    """
    ?붾젅洹몃옩 ?뚮┝ ?꾩넚
    
    Args:
        message: 蹂대궪 硫붿떆吏 蹂몃Ц
        target: 'signal' (媛쒖씤 梨꾪똿) ?먮뒗 'order' (二쇰Ц 洹몃９ 梨꾪똿)
    """
    chat_id = (settings.TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID_ORDER 
               if target == 'order' 
               else settings.TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID_SIGNAL)
    url = f"https://api.telegram.org/bot{settings.TELEGRAM_TOKEN}/sendMessage"

    try:
        response = requests.post(
            url,
            json={"chat_id": chat_id, "text": message},
            timeout=5,
        )
        result = response.json()

        if not result.get("ok"):
            logger.warning(
                f"?좑툘 ?붾젅洹몃옩 ?꾩넚 ?ㅽ뙣 (target={target}): "
                f"{result.get('description', '?????녿뒗 ?ㅻ쪟')}"
            )
            return False
        return True

    except requests.Timeout:
        logger.warning(f"?좑툘 ?붾젅洹몃옩 ?꾩넚 ??꾩븘??(target={target})")
        return False
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning(f"?좑툘 ?붾젅洹몃옩 ?꾩넚 ?덉쇅 (target={target}): {e}")
        return False

# api/candle_cache.py
"""

================================
紐⑹쟻: ka10080 遺꾨큺 ?몄텧 ??＜ ??429 ??2珥?blocking ?ъ떆????strategy 猷⑦봽 ?뺤?(?딄?)/?쒓컙李??꾪솕

     ???ㅽ듃?뚰겕媛 ?붾뱾?ㅻ룄 猷⑦봽媛 硫덉텛吏 ?딆쓬(?딄? 諛⑹?). ?ロ뙣?ㅼ쓽 2珥?blocking ?ъ떆???쒓굅.
  3) hit / miss / stale / error ?듦퀎瑜??④꺼, ????dry-run ???ㅼ젣 ?몄텧 ?덇컧?됱쓣 ?뺤씤.

    60MA ?깆? '?꾩꽦遊? 湲곗??대?濡?8珥?staleness??臾댄빐. ?꾩옱媛??罹먯떆 留먭퀬 WebSocket tick???ъ슜.
  - ?쎌? 罹먯떆 議고쉶/湲곕줉留?蹂댄샇?섍퀬, ?ㅼ젣 ?ㅽ듃?뚰겕 ?몄텧? ??諛뽰뿉???섑뻾(?ㅻⅨ 醫낅ぉ 釉붾줈??諛⑹?).

?곌껐 諛⑸쾿 (?? api/kiwoom_rest.py)
    from api.candle_cache import CandleCache

    # 湲곗〈 ?먮낯 ?몄텧??_raw 濡??④꺼?먭퀬:
    #   def _raw_get_minute_candles(self, stock_code, ...): ... (吏湲덉쓽 get_minute_candles 蹂몃Ц)
    self._candle_cache = CandleCache(self._raw_get_minute_candles, ttl_sec=8.0, logger=log)

    # ?몄텧遺 援먯껜:
    def get_minute_candles(self, stock_code, *args, **kwargs):
        return self._candle_cache.get(stock_code, *args, **kwargs)

    # MA??'理쒖떊 ?뺤꽦遊???瑗??꾩슂??洹뱁엳 ?쇰? 吏?먮쭔:
    candles = self._candle_cache.get(stock_code, force=True)

    # Phase ?꾪솚 濡쒓렇(????醫낅즺 ?쒖젏??1??
    self._candle_cache.log_stats()
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import time
import threading
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional


class CandleCache:
    def __init__(
        self,
        fetch_fn: Callable[..., List[Dict[str, Any]]],
        ttl_sec: float = 8.0,
        stale_on_error: bool = True,
        logger: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        """
        fetch_fn       : ?ㅼ젣 遺꾨큺??媛?몄삤??肄쒕윭釉? (stock_code, *args, **kwargs) -> list[dict]
                         利?吏湲덉쓽 get_minute_candles 蹂몃Ц(_raw)??洹몃?濡??ｌ쑝硫???
        ttl_sec        : 罹먯떆 ?좏슚?쒓컙(珥?. 8珥덈㈃ ?꾩꽦遊?湲곗? 臾댄빐?섎㈃??ka10080 ?몄텧???ш쾶 ?덇컧.
        stale_on_error : True硫??몄텧 ?ㅽ뙣/鍮덉쓳????留덉?留??뺤긽 罹먯떆瑜?諛섑솚(?딄? 諛⑹?).
        logger         : 湲곗〈 'AutoTrader'/root 濡쒓굅. None?대㈃ 臾댁쓬.
        """
        self._fetch_fn = fetch_fn
        self._ttl = float(ttl_sec)
        self._stale_on_error = stale_on_error
        self._log = logger
        self._lock = threading.RLock()
        # key -> {"data": list, "ts": float}
        self._store: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
        self._hit = 0
        self._miss = 0
        self._stale = 0
        self._error = 0

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------ #
    @staticmethod
    def _key(stock_code: str, args: tuple, kwargs: dict) -> str:
        if not args and not kwargs:
            return stock_code
        return f"{stock_code}|{args}|{tuple(sorted(kwargs.items()))}"

    def get(self, stock_code: str, *args, force: bool = False, **kwargs):
        """
        罹먯떆媛 ?좎꽑?섎㈃ 罹먯떆 諛섑솚, ?꾨땲硫??ㅼ젣 ?몄텧.
        ?ㅽ뙣 ??stale_on_error???곕씪 吏곸쟾 罹먯떆 諛섑솚(?놁쑝硫?None).
        諛섑솚 ?뺤떇? fetch_fn怨??숈씪 (candle dict 由ъ뒪?? newest-first).
        """
        key = self._key(stock_code, args, kwargs)
        now = time.time()

        with self._lock:
            entry = self._store.get(key)
            if (not force) and entry and (now - entry["ts"] < self._ttl):
                self._hit += 1
                return entry["data"]

        # ---- 罹먯떆 誘몄뒪: ?ㅼ젣 ?몄텧 (??諛뽰뿉???섑뻾) ----
        try:
            data = self._fetch_fn(stock_code, *args, **kwargs)
        except Exception as e:  # noqa: BLE001  (429 ?ы븿 紐⑤뱺 ?몄텧 ?ㅽ뙣)
            self._error += 1
            with self._lock:
                entry = self._store.get(key)
            if self._stale_on_error and entry:
                self._stale += 1
                self._dbg(
                    f"?뱤 遺꾨큺 ?몄텧 ?ㅽ뙣({e}) ??stale 罹먯떆 諛섑솚 [{stock_code}] "
                    f"(age={now - entry['ts']:.1f}s)"
                )
                return entry["data"]
            self._warn(f"?뱤 遺꾨큺 ?몄텧 ?ㅽ뙣 & 罹먯떆?놁쓬 [{stock_code}]: {e}")
            return None

        if data:
            with self._lock:
                self._store[key] = {"data": data, "ts": time.time()}
                self._miss += 1
            return data

        # 鍮??묐떟([] / None): 媛?ν븯硫?吏곸쟾 罹먯떆 ?좎?(?쇱떆??鍮덉쓳?듭쑝濡??명븳 '遺꾨큺遺議? ?ㅽ뙋 諛⑹?)
        with self._lock:
            entry = self._store.get(key)
        if self._stale_on_error and entry:
            self._stale += 1
            return entry["data"]
        self._miss += 1
        return data  # [] ?먮뒗 None 洹몃?濡????몄텧遺??'遺꾨큺遺議? 泥섎━ ?먮쫫 ?좎?

    # ------------------------------------------------------------------ #
    def invalidate(self, stock_code: Optional[str] = None) -> None:
        """?뱀젙 醫낅ぉ(?먮뒗 ?꾩껜) 罹먯떆 臾댄슚?? 泥?궛 吏곹썑 ?щℓ???먮떒 ?깆뿉??媛뺤젣 媛깆떊??"""
        with self._lock:
            if stock_code is None:
                self._store.clear()
                return
            for k in [
                k for k in self._store
                if k == stock_code or k.startswith(stock_code + "|")
            ]:
                self._store.pop(k, None)

    def stats(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        total = self._hit + self._miss
        rate = (self._hit / total * 100.0) if total else 0.0
        return {
            "hit": self._hit,
            "miss": self._miss,
            "stale": self._stale,
            "error": self._error,
            "hit_rate_pct": round(rate, 1),
            "cached_codes": len(self._store),
        }

    def log_stats(self) -> None:
        s = self.stats()
        self._info(
            f"?뱤 遺꾨큺罹먯떆 ?듦퀎 hit={s['hit']} miss={s['miss']} "
            f"stale={s['stale']} err={s['error']} "
            f"hit??{s['hit_rate_pct']}% 醫낅ぉ??{s['cached_codes']}"
        )

    # ---- 濡쒓퉭 ?ы띁 (logger ?놁쑝硫?臾댁쓬) ----
    def _info(self, msg: str) -> None:
        if self._log:
            self._log.info(msg)

    def _warn(self, msg: str) -> None:
        if self._log:
            self._log.warning(msg)

    def _dbg(self, msg: str) -> None:
        if self._log:
            self._log.debug(msg)

"""
?ㅼ? REST API ?몄텧 紐⑤뱢
?????????????????????????????????????
??븷: 二쇰Ц, ?붽퀬/?덉닔湲?議고쉶, ?꾩옱媛 議고쉶, 遺꾨큺 李⑦듃 議고쉶
"""
import logging
import json
import time
import requests
from datetime import datetime

from utils.logger import logger


class KiwoomREST:
    """?ㅼ? REST API ?대씪?댁뼵??""

    MOCK_HOST = "https://mockapi.kiwoom.com"
    REAL_HOST = "https://api.kiwoom.com"

    # ?몄텧 鍮덈룄 ?쒖뼱 (1珥?5???쒗븳 ??0.6珥??덉쟾留덉쭊)
    MIN_INTERVAL = 0.6

    def __init__(self, token: str, is_mock: bool = True):
        self.token = token
        self.host = self.MOCK_HOST if is_mock else self.REAL_HOST
        self._last_request_ts = 0.0

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 怨듯넻 ?몄텧
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def _throttle(self):
        elapsed = time.time() - self._last_request_ts
        if elapsed < self.MIN_INTERVAL:
            time.sleep(self.MIN_INTERVAL - elapsed)
        self._last_request_ts = time.time()

    def _request(self, path: str, api_id: str, body: dict,
                 cont_yn: str = "N", next_key: str = "") -> dict:
        """怨듯넻 POST ?붿껌. 429???먮룞 ?ъ떆??"""
        self._throttle()
        url = f"{self.host}{path}"
        headers = {
            "Content-Type": "application/json;charset=UTF-8",
            "authorization": f"Bearer {self.token}",
            "cont-yn": cont_yn,
            "next-key": next_key,
            "api-id": api_id,
        }

        try:
            res = requests.post(url, headers=headers,
                                data=json.dumps(body), timeout=10)
            res.raise_for_status()
            data = res.json()

            if data.get("return_code") != 0:
                logger.warning(
                    f"?좑툘 [{api_id}] ?묐떟 ?ㅽ뙣: "
                    f"code={data.get('return_code')} "
                    f"msg={data.get('return_msg')}"
                )
            return data

        except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:
            status = e.response.status_code
            if status == 429:
                logger.warning(f"?좑툘 [{api_id}] 429 ?몄텧鍮덈룄 珥덇낵, 2珥??湲????ъ떆??)
                time.sleep(2)
                try:
                    res = requests.post(url, headers=headers,
                                        data=json.dumps(body), timeout=10)
                    res.raise_for_status()
                    return res.json()
                except Exception as e2:
                    logger.error(f"??[{api_id}] ?ъ떆???ㅽ뙣: {e2}")
                    return {"return_code": -1, "return_msg": "rate_limit_retry_failed"}
            logger.error(f"??[{api_id}] HTTP ?먮윭 {status}: {e.response.text[:200]}")
            return {"return_code": -1, "return_msg": str(e)}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"??[{api_id}] ?붿껌 ?덉쇅: {e}")
            return {"return_code": -1, "return_msg": str(e)}

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 二쇰Ц
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def buy_market_order(self, stock_code: str, qty: int,
                         price: int = 0, trde_tp: str = "3") -> dict:
        """留ㅼ닔 二쇰Ц (kt10000)"""
        body = {
            "dmst_stex_tp": "KRX",
            "stk_cd": stock_code,
            "ord_qty": str(qty),
            "ord_uv": str(price) if price > 0 else "",
            "trde_tp": trde_tp,
            "cond_uv": "",
        }
        result = self._request("/api/dostk/ordr", "kt10000", body)
        if result.get("return_code") == 0:
            logger.info(
                f"??留ㅼ닔二쇰Ц ?깃났 | {stock_code} | {qty}二?| "
                f"?④?={price if price > 0 else '?쒖옣媛'} | ord_no={result.get('ord_no')}"
            )
        return result

    def sell_market_order(self, stock_code: str, qty: int,
                          price: int = 0, trde_tp: str = "3") -> dict:
        """留ㅻ룄 二쇰Ц (kt10001)"""
        body = {
            "dmst_stex_tp": "KRX",
            "stk_cd": stock_code,
            "ord_qty": str(qty),
            "ord_uv": str(price) if price > 0 else "",
            "trde_tp": trde_tp,
            "cond_uv": "",
        }
        result = self._request("/api/dostk/ordr", "kt10001", body)
        if result.get("return_code") == 0:
            logger.info(
                f"??留ㅻ룄二쇰Ц ?깃났 | {stock_code} | {qty}二?| "
                f"?④?={price if price > 0 else '?쒖옣媛'} | ord_no={result.get('ord_no')}"
            )
        return result

    def cancel_order(self, orig_ord_no: str, stock_code: str,
                     cancel_qty: int = 0) -> dict:
        """二쇰Ц 痍⑥냼 (kt10003)"""
        body = {
            "dmst_stex_tp": "KRX",
            "orig_ord_no": orig_ord_no,
            "stk_cd": stock_code,
            "mdfy_qty": "",
            "cncl_qty": str(cancel_qty),
        }
        result = self._request("/api/dostk/ordr", "kt10003", body)
        if result.get("return_code") == 0:
            logger.info(f"??二쇰Ц 痍⑥냼 | orig_ord_no={orig_ord_no} | {stock_code}")
        return result

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?쒖꽭 議고쉶
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def get_current_price(self, stock_code: str) -> int:
        """二쇱떇湲곕낯?뺣낫 (ka10001) ???꾩옱媛"""
        result = self._request("/api/dostk/stkinfo", "ka10001",
                               {"stk_cd": stock_code})
        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            return 0
        return self._safe_price(result.get("cur_prc", "0"))

    def get_stock_info(self, stock_code: str) -> dict:
        """二쇱떇湲곕낯?뺣낫 ?꾩껜 (ka10001)"""
        return self._request("/api/dostk/stkinfo", "ka10001",
                             {"stk_cd": stock_code})

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 遺꾨큺 李⑦듃 議고쉶 (ka10080)
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def get_minute_candles(self, stock_code: str, interval: int = 1,
                           count: int = 60, base_date: str = None) -> list:
        """遺꾨큺 議고쉶 (ka10080). candles[0]???대뒓 ?쒖젏?몄????뱤 濡쒓렇濡??뺤씤.
        諛섑솚: [{time_str(14?먮━), open, high, low, close, volume}, ...]"""
        if not base_date:
            base_date = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")

        body = {
            "stk_cd": stock_code,
            "tic_scope": str(interval),
            "upd_stkpc_tp": "1",
            "base_dt": base_date,
        }

        result = self._request("/api/dostk/chart", "ka10080", body)
        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            return []

        rows = result.get("stk_min_pole_chart_qry", []) or []
        candles = []
        for row in rows[:count]:
            time_str = row.get("cntr_tm", "")
            if len(time_str) != 14:
                continue
            candles.append({
                "time_str": time_str,
                "open":   self._safe_price(row.get("open_pric")),
                "high":   self._safe_price(row.get("high_pric")),
                "low":    self._safe_price(row.get("low_pric")),
                "close":  self._safe_price(row.get("cur_prc")),
                "volume": self._safe_int(row.get("trde_qty")),
            })

        if candles:
            logger.info("[%s] ?뱤 遺꾨큺 %d媛? [0]=%s ~ [-1]=%s",
                        stock_code, len(candles),
                        candles[0]["time_str"], candles[-1]["time_str"])
        return candles
        
        
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 怨꾩쥖 議고쉶
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def get_deposit(self) -> dict:
        """?덉닔湲덉긽?명쁽??(kt00001)"""
        return self._request("/api/dostk/acnt", "kt00001",
                             {"qry_tp": "3"})

    def get_orderable_amount(self) -> int:
        """二쇰Ц媛?κ툑??""
        result = self.get_deposit()
        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            return 0
        return self._safe_int(result.get("ord_alow_amt", "0"))

    def get_balance(self) -> dict:
        """怨꾩쥖?됯??붽퀬?댁뿭 (kt00018)"""
        return self._request("/api/dostk/acnt", "kt00018",
                             {"qry_tp": "1", "dmst_stex_tp": "KRX"})

    def get_holdings(self) -> dict:
        """蹂댁쑀 醫낅ぉ ??{醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶: {?뺣낫}}"""
        result = self.get_balance()
        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            return {}

        holdings = {}
        for item in result.get("acnt_evlt_remn_indv_tot", []):
            code = (item.get("stk_cd") or "").strip()
            if code.startswith("A"):
                code = code[1:]
            if not code:
                continue
            holdings[code] = {
                "name": item.get("stk_nm", ""),
                "qty": self._safe_int(item.get("rmnd_qty", "0")),
                "avg_price": self._safe_price(item.get("pur_pric", "0")),
                "cur_price": self._safe_price(item.get("cur_prc", "0")),
                "eval_amt": self._safe_int(item.get("evlt_amt", "0")),
                "pnl": self._safe_int(item.get("evltv_prft", "0")),
                "pnl_rate": self._safe_float(item.get("prft_rt", "0")),
            }
        return holdings

    def get_unfilled_orders(self) -> dict:
        """誘몄껜寃?(ka10075)"""
        body = {
            "all_stk_tp": "0",
            "trde_tp": "0",
            "stex_tp": "0",
            "stk_cd": "",
        }
        return self._request("/api/dostk/acnt", "ka10075", body)

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?좏떥
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    @staticmethod
    def _safe_int(v) -> int:
        """
        臾몄옄?????뺤닔. ?뚯닔 蹂댁〈.
        ?먯씡(pnl), 嫄곕옒???깆뿉 ?ъ슜.
        """
        if v is None:
            return 0
        s = str(v).replace(",", "").replace("+", "").strip()
        try:
            return int(float(s))
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return 0

    @staticmethod
    def _safe_float(v) -> float:
        """
        臾몄옄?????ㅼ닔. ?뚯닔 蹂댁〈.
        ?먯씡瑜?pnl_rate) ?깆뿉 ?ъ슜.
        """
        if v is None:
            return 0.0
        s = str(v).replace(",", "").replace("+", "").strip()
        try:
            return float(s)
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return 0.0

    @staticmethod
    def _safe_price(v) -> int:
        """
        媛寃??꾩슜 蹂??
        ?ㅼ? API??媛寃??묐떟?먮뒗 ?깅씫 遺??'+'/'-')媛 遺숈뼱?덉쓬:
        - '+78800' = ?꾩씪?鍮??곸듅, 媛寃?78,800??
        - '-78800' = ?꾩씪?鍮??섎씫, 媛寃?78,800??
        遺?몃뒗 ?깅씫 ?쒖떆??肉?吏꾩쭨 ?뚯닔媛 ?꾨땲誘濡??덈뙎媛믪쑝濡?泥섎━.
        """
        if v is None:
            return 0
        s = str(v).replace(",", "").replace("+", "").replace("-", "").strip()
        try:
            return int(float(s))
        except (ValueError, TypeError):
            return 0

"""
?ㅼ? WebSocket ?대씪?댁뼵??(?뺤옣??
?????????????????????????????????????
??븷:
  - WS ?곌껐, 濡쒓렇?? PING ?먮룞 ?묐떟, ?먮룞 ?ъ뿰寃?
  - 議곌굔寃???ㅼ떆媛?(CNSRREQ search_type=1): ?몄엯/?댄깉 ?좏샇 肄쒕갚
  - 議곌굔寃??利됱떆 寃??(CNSRREQ search_type=0): ?꾩옱 吏꾩엯 醫낅ぉ ?ㅻ깄?? ???좉퇋
  - 醫낅ぉ蹂??ㅼ떆媛?(REG): 二쇱떇泥닿껐(0B) + 二쇱떇?멸??붾웾(0D) 肄쒕갚
  - ?ъ젒????議곌굔??+ ?ㅼ떆媛??먮룞 ?щ벑濡?
  - REG 援щ룆 ?ъ씠 sleep?쇰줈 鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳 ?뚰뵾  ???좉퇋
"""
import asyncio
import json
import websockets

from config import settings
from utils.logger import logger


TYPE_TRADE = "0B"
TYPE_ORDERBOOK = "0D"

# WS REG 鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳 ?뚰뵾 (?ㅼ? ?뺤콉)
REG_INTERVAL_SEC = 0.3


class KiwoomWS:
    MOCK_URL = "wss://mockapi.kiwoom.com:10000/api/dostk/websocket"
    REAL_URL = "wss://api.kiwoom.com:10000/api/dostk/websocket"

    def __init__(
        self,
        token: str,
        is_mock: bool = True,
        on_signal=None,
        on_trade=None,
        on_orderbook=None,
    ):
        self.token = token
        self.url = self.MOCK_URL if is_mock else self.REAL_URL
        self.on_signal = on_signal
        self.on_trade = on_trade
        self.on_orderbook = on_orderbook

        self.ws = None
        self.connected = False
        self._stop = False

        self._subscribed_seqs: list[str] = []
        self.condition_map: dict[str, str] = {}
        self._subscribed_realtime: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
        self._cond_keys_logged = False   # ?ㅼ떆媛?議곌굔 raw ??1??濡쒓퉭??

        # REG ?몄텧 吏곷젹??+ 鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳
        self._reg_lock = asyncio.Lock()
        self._last_reg_ts = 0.0

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 1. ?곌껐 & 濡쒓렇??
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def connect(self):
        logger.info(f"?뵆 WebSocket ?곌껐 ?쒕룄: {self.url}")
        self.ws = await websockets.connect(self.url, ping_interval=None)

        login_msg = {"trnm": "LOGIN", "token": self.token}
        await self.ws.send(json.dumps(login_msg))

        raw = await asyncio.wait_for(self.ws.recv(), timeout=10)
        resp = json.loads(raw)

        if resp.get("trnm") != "LOGIN":
            raise RuntimeError(f"LOGIN ?묐떟???꾨땶 硫붿떆吏 ?섏떊: {resp}")
        if resp.get("return_code") != 0:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"LOGIN ?ㅽ뙣: code={resp.get('return_code')} msg={resp.get('return_msg')}"
            )

        self.connected = True
        logger.info("??WebSocket 濡쒓렇???깃났")

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 2. 議곌굔??紐⑸줉 議고쉶
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def fetch_condition_list(self) -> dict[str, str]:
        await self._send({"trnm": "CNSRLST"})
        resp = await self._wait_for("CNSRLST", timeout=10)

        items = resp.get("data") or []
        result = {}
        for it in items:
            if isinstance(it, list):
                seq, name = str(it[0]), str(it[1])
            elif isinstance(it, dict):
                seq = str(it.get("seq") or it.get("Seq") or "")
                name = str(it.get("name") or it.get("Name") or "")
            else:
                continue
            if seq:
                result[seq] = name

        self.condition_map = result
        logger.info(f"?뱥 議곌굔??紐⑸줉 {len(result)}媛?議고쉶 ?꾨즺")
        for seq, name in result.items():
            logger.info(f"   seq={seq}  name={name}")

        if not result:
            logger.warning(
                "?좑툘 議곌굔?앹씠 0媛쒖엯?덈떎! ?곸썒臾? [0150]?먯꽌 議곌굔?앹쓣 留뚮뱾怨?"
                "'??議곌굔????????뚮??붿? ?뺤씤?섏꽭??"
            )
        return result

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 3. 議곌굔???ㅼ떆媛??깅줉/?댁젣
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def subscribe_condition(self, seq: str, stex_tp: str = "K"):
        seq = str(seq)
        msg = {
            "trnm": "CNSRREQ", "seq": seq, "search_type": "1",
            "stex_tp": stex_tp, "cont_yn": "N", "next_key": "",
        }
        await self._send(msg)
        if seq not in self._subscribed_seqs:
            self._subscribed_seqs.append(seq)
        name = self.condition_map.get(seq, "?")
        logger.info(f"?뱻 議곌굔???ㅼ떆媛??깅줉: seq={seq} ({name})")

    async def unsubscribe_condition(self, seq: str):
        seq = str(seq)
        await self._send({"trnm": "CNSRCLR", "seq": seq})
        if seq in self._subscribed_seqs:
            self._subscribed_seqs.remove(seq)
        logger.info(f"?벖 議곌굔???ㅼ떆媛??댁젣: seq={seq}")

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # ???좉퇋: 議곌굔??利됱떆 寃??(?꾩옱 吏꾩엯 醫낅ぉ ?ㅻ깄??
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def fetch_condition_snapshot(
        self, seq: str, stex_tp: str = "K", timeout: int = 10,
    ) -> list[str]:
        """search_type=0?쇰줈 ?꾩옱 ?쒖젏??議곌굔?앹뿉 ?ㅼ뼱?덈뒗 醫낅ぉ 紐⑸줉 1??議고쉶.

        Returns: 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶 由ъ뒪??(?? ['005930', '003690', ...])
        """
        seq = str(seq)
        await self._send({
            "trnm": "CNSRREQ", "seq": seq, "search_type": "0",
            "stex_tp": stex_tp, "cont_yn": "N", "next_key": "",
        })

        try:
            resp = await self._wait_for("CNSRREQ", timeout=timeout)
        except RuntimeError as e:
            logger.warning(f"?좑툘 議곌굔???ㅻ깄??[seq={seq}] ?묐떟 ?놁쓬: {e}")
            return []

        data = resp.get("data") or []
        if isinstance(data, dict):
            data = [data]

        codes = []
        for item in data:
            code = (
                item.get("9001") or item.get("jmcode") or item.get("stk_cd") or ""
            ).strip()
            if code.startswith("A"):
                code = code[1:]
            if code:
                codes.append(code)

        name = self.condition_map.get(seq, "?")
        logger.info(f"?벝 議곌굔???ㅻ깄??[seq={seq} {name}]: {len(codes)}醫낅ぉ ??{codes}")
        return codes

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 4. 醫낅ぉ蹂??ㅼ떆媛??깅줉 (0B/0D) ??鍮덈룄 ?쒗븳 ?뚰뵾
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def subscribe_realtime(
        self, items: list[str], types: list[str], grp_no: str = "1"
    ):
        if not items or not types:
            return
        async with self._reg_lock:
            # 吏곸쟾 REG ?몄텧怨쇱쓽 媛꾧꺽 蹂댁옣
            loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
            now = loop.time()
            elapsed = now - self._last_reg_ts
            if elapsed < REG_INTERVAL_SEC:
                await asyncio.sleep(REG_INTERVAL_SEC - elapsed)

            msg = {
                "trnm": "REG", "grp_no": grp_no,
                "refresh": "1",
                "data": [{"item": items, "type": types}],
            }
            await self._send(msg)
            self._last_reg_ts = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()

            for code in items:
                self._subscribed_realtime.setdefault(code, set()).update(types)
            logger.info(f"?뱻 ?ㅼ떆媛??깅줉: {items} types={types}")

    async def unsubscribe_realtime(
        self, items: list[str], types: list[str], grp_no: str = "1"
    ):
        if not items or not types:
            return
        msg = {
            "trnm": "REMOVE", "grp_no": grp_no,
            "data": [{"item": items, "type": types}],
        }
        await self._send(msg)
        for code in items:
            if code in self._subscribed_realtime:
                self._subscribed_realtime[code].difference_update(types)
                if not self._subscribed_realtime[code]:
                    del self._subscribed_realtime[code]
        logger.info(f"?벖 ?ㅼ떆媛??댁젣: {items} types={types}")

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 5. ?섏떊 猷⑦봽
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def listen(self):
        backoff = 1
        while not self._stop:
            try:
                if not self.connected:
                    await self.connect()
                    await self.fetch_condition_list()
                    for seq in list(self._subscribed_seqs):
                        await self.subscribe_condition(seq)
                    for code, types in list(self._subscribed_realtime.items()):
                        await self.subscribe_realtime([code], list(types))
                    backoff = 1

                async for raw in self.ws:
                    if self._stop:
                        break
                    await self._handle_message(raw)

            except websockets.ConnectionClosed as e:
                logger.warning(f"?뵆 ?곌껐 ?딄? (code={e.code}, reason={e.reason})")
            except asyncio.CancelledError:
                break
            except Exception as e:
                logger.exception(f"???섏떊 猷⑦봽 ?덉쇅: {e}")

            self.connected = False
            if self._stop:
                break

            logger.info(f"?삼툘 {backoff}珥????ъ뿰寃??쒕룄...")
            await asyncio.sleep(backoff)
            backoff = min(backoff * 2, 60)

    async def _handle_message(self, raw: str):
        try:
            msg = json.loads(raw)
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            logger.warning(f"?좑툘 JSON ?뚯떛 ?ㅽ뙣: {raw[:200]}")
            return

        trnm = msg.get("trnm")

        if trnm == "PING":
            await self.ws.send(raw)
            return

        if trnm in ("REAL", "CNSRREQ"):
            await self._dispatch_signal(msg)
            return

        logger.info(f"?뱿 WS msg trnm={trnm}: {str(msg)[:300]}")

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 6. ?붿뒪?⑥튂
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def _dispatch_signal(self, msg: dict):
        data = msg.get("data")
        if not data:
            return
        if isinstance(data, dict):
            data = [data]

        for item in data:
            item_type = item.get("type")
            if item_type == TYPE_TRADE:
                await self._dispatch_trade_item(item)
            elif item_type == TYPE_ORDERBOOK:
                await self._dispatch_orderbook_item(item)
            else:
                await self._dispatch_condition_item(item)

    async def _dispatch_condition_item(self, item: dict):
        stock_code = (
            item.get("9001") or item.get("jmcode") or item.get("stk_cd") or ""
        ).strip()
        if stock_code.startswith("A"):
            stock_code = stock_code[1:]
        signal_type = item.get("843") or item.get("insert_delete_tp") or "I"
        if not stock_code:
            return
        mark = "?뱢" if signal_type == "I" else "?뱣"
        kind = "?몄엯" if signal_type == "I" else "?댄깉"
        logger.info(f"{mark} {kind} ?좏샇: {stock_code}")
        if self.on_signal:
            try:
                await self.on_signal(stock_code, signal_type, item)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"on_signal 肄쒕갚 ?덉쇅: {stock_code}")

    async def _dispatch_trade_item(self, item: dict):
        if not self.on_trade:
            return
        stock_code = (item.get("item") or "").lstrip("A").strip()
        values = item.get("values") or {}

        price = self._parse_signed_int(values.get("10"))
        volume_signed = self._parse_signed_int(values.get("15"))

        if volume_signed > 0:
            side = "buy"
        elif volume_signed < 0:
            side = "sell"
        else:
            side = "neutral"

        parsed = {
            "stock_code": stock_code,
            "price": abs(price),
            "volume": abs(volume_signed),
            "side": side,
            "strength": self._parse_float(values.get("228")),
            "time": values.get("20", ""),
            "raw": values,
        }
        try:
            await self.on_trade(parsed)
        except Exception:
            logger.exception(f"on_trade 肄쒕갚 ?덉쇅: {stock_code}")

    async def _dispatch_condition_item(self, item: dict):
        stock_code = (
            item.get("9001") or item.get("jmcode") or item.get("stk_cd") or ""
        ).strip()
        if stock_code.startswith("A"):
            stock_code = stock_code[1:]
        signal_type = item.get("843") or item.get("insert_delete_tp") or "I"
        # 議곌굔 ?쇰젴踰덊샇(?대뒓 議곌굔?먯꽌 ?붾뒗吏). ?꾨뱶 異붿젙: 841 ???덈릺硫??ㅼ쓬 ??raw ??濡쒓렇濡??뺤젙
        cond_seq = str(
            item.get("841") or item.get("cond_idx") or item.get("seq") or ""
        ).strip()
        if not stock_code:
            return

        # ?ㅼ떆媛?議곌굔 ?꾩씠???ㅻ? 1?뚮쭔 濡쒓퉭 (seq ?꾨뱶 ?뺤젙??
        if not self._cond_keys_logged:
            logger.info(f"?뵎 議곌굔 ?ㅼ떆媛?raw ?? {list(item.keys())}")
            self._cond_keys_logged = True

        mark = "?뱢" if signal_type == "I" else "?뱣"
        kind = "?몄엯" if signal_type == "I" else "?댄깉"
        logger.info(f"{mark} {kind} ?좏샇: {stock_code} (seq={cond_seq or '?'})")
        if self.on_signal:
            try:
                await self.on_signal(stock_code, signal_type, item, cond_seq or None)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"on_signal 肄쒕갚 ?덉쇅: {stock_code}")
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 7. ?뚯떛 ?좏떥
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    @staticmethod
    def _parse_signed_int(s) -> int:
        if not s:
            return 0
        try:
            return int(str(s).strip())
        except ValueError:
            return 0

    @staticmethod
    def _parse_uint(s) -> int:
        if not s:
            return 0
        try:
            return abs(int(str(s).strip()))
        except ValueError:
            return 0

    @staticmethod
    def _parse_float(s) -> float:
        if not s:
            return 0.0
        try:
            return float(str(s).strip())
        except ValueError:
            return 0.0

    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    # 8. ?≪떊/?湲??좏떥
    # ?????????????????????????????????????????
    async def _send(self, payload: dict):
        if not self.ws:
            raise RuntimeError("WebSocket 誘몄뿰寃??곹깭")
        await self.ws.send(json.dumps(payload))

    async def _wait_for(self, trnm: str, timeout: int = 10) -> dict:
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        end = loop.time() + timeout
        while loop.time() < end:
            remaining = end - loop.time()
            try:
                raw = await asyncio.wait_for(self.ws.recv(), timeout=remaining)
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                raise RuntimeError(f"{trnm} ?묐떟 ??꾩븘??({timeout}s)")
            msg = json.loads(raw)
            if msg.get("trnm") == "PING":
                await self.ws.send(raw)
                continue
            if msg.get("trnm") == trnm:
                return msg
        raise RuntimeError(f"{trnm} ?묐떟 ??꾩븘??)

    async def close(self):
        self._stop = True
        if self.ws:
            try:
                for seq in list(self._subscribed_seqs):
                    await self.unsubscribe_condition(seq)
                for code, types in list(self._subscribed_realtime.items()):
                    await self.unsubscribe_realtime([code], list(types))
            except Exception:
                pass
            await self.ws.close()
        logger.info("?몝 WebSocket 醫낅즺")

# ws_supervisor.py
"""
WebSocket ?ъ뿰寃??덊띁諛붿씠? (WSSupervisor)
==========================================
紐⑹쟻: WS ?딄? ?????(a)?먮룞 ?ъ뿰寃?諛깆삤?? (b)half-open(?먮윭 ?놁씠 ?곗씠?곕쭔 ?딄?) 媛먯?,
      (c)?ъ뿰寃곕쭏??議곌굔寃???щ벑濡?媛뺤젣.

??媛??以묒슂 ??
  ?ㅼ? WS???딄꼈???ㅼ떆 遺숈쑝硫?議곌굔寃??0150] ?깅줉(CNSRREQ seq=6/7/8)???좎븘媛꾨떎.
  ?ъ뿰寃곕뤌???щ벑濡앹쓣 ???섎㈃ ?곌껐? 硫姨≫빐 蹂댁뿬???듭?媛 0嫄댁씠 ?쒕떎.
  ??議곌굔?깅줉 肄붾뱶??run_once_fn '??, ?곌껐+濡쒓렇??吏곹썑??'留ㅻ쾲' ?ｌ쓣 寃?
  (利앹긽 '議곌굔寃?됯낵 肄붾뵫 遺덉씪移?/ ?딄? / ?ㅻ깄??0醫낅ぉ'???좊젰?????먯씤.)

?쇱씠釉뚮윭由?鍮꾩쓽議?
  websocket-client(WebSocketApp)??websockets(asyncio)???곴??놁씠,
  '?곌껐 + 濡쒓렇??+ 議곌굔?깅줉 + ?섏떊猷⑦봽(釉붾줈??' ???⑹뼱由щ? run_once_fn?쇰줈 媛먯떥硫???

half-open 媛먯? (諛섏? 二쎌? ?뚯폆)
  - ?섏떊 肄쒕갚?먯꽌 留?硫붿떆吏留덈떎 sup.mark_alive() ?몄텧(?ㅼ? PINGPONG echo 吏?먯씠硫?異⑸텇).
  - heartbeat_timeout ?숈븞 ??嫄대룄 ???ㅻ㈃ 二쎌? ?곌껐濡?蹂닿퀬 媛뺤젣 ?ъ뿰寃?
  - ??釉붾줈??ws.recv()??stop_event留뚯쑝濡???源⑥쭊?? ??以??섎굹 ?꾩슂:
      (1) ?섏떊 ?뚯폆????꾩븘???ㅼ젙(ws.settimeout(5)) ??recv媛 二쇨린?곸쑝濡????stop_event ?뺤씤
      (2) on_force_close 肄쒕갚 ?쒓났 ???뚯튂?낆씠 ws.close()濡?媛뺤젣濡?源⑥?
    媛?ν븯硫?(1)+(2) ????沅뚯옣.

?곌껐 諛⑸쾿
  1) 湲곗〈 WS 肄붾뱶瑜??⑥닔 ?섎굹濡?臾띔린 (stop_event ?몄옄 諛쏄쾶):
       def _run_ws_once(stop_event):
           ws = connect()                 # ?곌껐
           ws.settimeout(5)               # ??沅뚯옣: recv媛 二쇨린?곸쑝濡??由ш쾶
           login(ws)                      # 濡쒓렇??
           register_conditions(ws)        # ?끸쁾 seq=6/7/8 議곌굔寃???щ벑濡?(留??곌껐留덈떎!)
           while not stop_event.is_set():
               try:
                   msg = ws.recv()        # 釉붾줈????꾩븘??5s)
               except TimeoutError:
                   continue               # ??꾩븘?껋? ?뺤긽 ??猷⑦봽 ?ы솗??
               sup.mark_alive()           # half-open 媛먯???
               handle(msg)                # PINGPONG echo / REAL / 議곌굔?듭? 泥섎━
           ws.close()

  2) ?덊띁諛붿씠? (遊?湲곕룞 ??:
       from ws_supervisor import WSSupervisor
       sup = WSSupervisor(
           _run_ws_once,
           heartbeat_timeout=30,          # 30s 臾댁닔????媛뺤젣 ?ъ뿰寃?(0?대㈃ ??
           on_force_close=lambda: ws_ref and ws_ref.close(),  # ?좏깮: 釉붾줈??recv 源⑥슦湲?
           logger=log,
       )
       sup.start()

  3) 醫낅즺: sup.stop()
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import time
import random
import threading
from typing import Any, Callable, Optional


class WSSupervisor:
    def __init__(
        self,
        run_once_fn: Callable[[threading.Event], Any],
        on_state: Optional[Callable[[str], None]] = None,
        on_force_close: Optional[Callable[[], None]] = None,
        base_backoff: float = 1.0,
        max_backoff: float = 30.0,
        healthy_reset_sec: float = 60.0,
        heartbeat_timeout: float = 0.0,   # 0?대㈃ half-open 媛먯? ??
        logger: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        """
        run_once_fn(stop_event): ?곌껐+濡쒓렇??議곌굔?깅줉+?섏떊猷⑦봽(釉붾줈??. ?딄린硫?由ы꽩/?덉쇅 ???ъ뿰寃?
        on_state(state)        : 'connecting'/'connected'/'disconnected'/'reconnecting' 肄쒕갚(?좏깮).
        on_force_close()       : ?뚯튂??醫낅즺 ??釉붾줈??recv瑜?源⑥슦湲??꾪븳 媛뺤젣 close(?좏깮, 沅뚯옣).
        base/max_backoff       : ?ъ뿰寃??湲?1s??s??s...??0s(jitter ?ы븿).
        healthy_reset_sec      : ???쒓컙 ?댁긽 遺숈뼱?덈떎 ?딄린硫?諛깆삤?꾨? base濡?由ъ뀑.
        heartbeat_timeout      : 臾댁닔?????쒓컙 珥덇낵 ??half-open?쇰줈 蹂닿퀬 媛뺤젣 ?ъ뿰寃?
        """
        self._run_once = run_once_fn
        self._on_state = on_state
        self._on_force_close = on_force_close
        self._base = float(base_backoff)
        self._max = float(max_backoff)
        self._healthy = float(healthy_reset_sec)
        self._hb_timeout = float(heartbeat_timeout)
        self._log = logger

        self._running = False
        self._sup_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None
        self._session_stop: Optional[threading.Event] = None
        self._last_alive = 0.0
        self._lock = threading.RLock()
        self._reconnects = 0

    # ---- lifecycle ----
    def start(self) -> None:
        if self._running:
            return
        self._running = True
        self._sup_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._supervise, name="ws_supervisor", daemon=True)
        self._sup_thread.start()
        self._info("?㏊ ws_supervisor ?쒖옉")

    def stop(self, timeout: float = 5.0) -> None:
        if not self._running:
            return
        self._running = False
        if self._session_stop:
            self._session_stop.set()
        self._force_close()   # 釉붾줈??recv 源⑥슦湲?
        if self._sup_thread:
            self._sup_thread.join(timeout=timeout)
        self._info(f"?㏊ ws_supervisor 醫낅즺 (?ъ뿰寃?{self._reconnects}??")

    def mark_alive(self) -> None:
        """?섏떊 肄쒕갚?먯꽌 留?硫붿떆吏留덈떎 ?몄텧. half-open 媛먯???湲곗???"""
        with self._lock:
            self._last_alive = time.time()

    def reconnect_count(self) -> int:
        return self._reconnects

    # ---- core loop ----
    def _supervise(self) -> None:
        backoff = self._base
        first = True
        while self._running:
            self._session_stop = threading.Event()
            self.mark_alive()
            self._emit_state("connecting" if first else "reconnecting")
            first = False
            t0 = time.time()

            wd = None
            if self._hb_timeout > 0:
                wd = threading.Thread(
                    target=self._watchdog, args=(self._session_stop,),
                    name="ws_heartbeat", daemon=True,
                )
                wd.start()

            try:
                self._emit_state("connected")
                self._run_once(self._session_stop)   # 釉붾줈?? ?딄린硫?由ы꽩/?덉쇅
            except Exception as e:  # noqa: BLE001
                self._err(f"?뵶 WS ?몄뀡 ?덉쇅: {e}")
            finally:
                self._session_stop.set()
                if wd:
                    wd.join(timeout=2.0)

            if not self._running:
                break

            self._reconnects += 1
            self._emit_state("disconnected")
            alive = time.time() - t0
            if alive >= self._healthy:
                backoff = self._base   # ?ㅻ옒 遺숈뼱?덉뿀?쇰㈃ 諛깆삤??由ъ뀑
            self._warn(f"?뵆 WS ?딄? (?좎? {alive:.0f}s) ??{backoff:.1f}s ???ъ뿰寃?(#{self._reconnects})")
            self._sleep_backoff(backoff)
            backoff = min(backoff * 2, self._max)

    def _watchdog(self, session_stop: threading.Event) -> None:
        while not session_stop.is_set() and self._running:
            time.sleep(1.0)
            with self._lock:
                silent = time.time() - self._last_alive
            if silent > self._hb_timeout:
                self._warn(f"?뮘 WS {silent:.0f}s 臾댁닔??half-open ?섏떖) ??媛뺤젣 ?ъ뿰寃?)
                session_stop.set()
                self._force_close()
                return

    # ---- helpers ----
    def _sleep_backoff(self, backoff: float) -> None:
        delay = backoff + random.uniform(0, backoff * 0.3)   # jitter
        end = time.time() + delay
        while time.time() < end and self._running:
            time.sleep(0.2)

    def _force_close(self) -> None:
        if self._on_force_close:
            try:
                self._on_force_close()
            except Exception as e:  # noqa: BLE001
                self._err(f"on_force_close ?덉쇅: {e}")

    def _emit_state(self, state: str) -> None:
        if self._on_state:
            try:
                self._on_state(state)
            except Exception as e:  # noqa: BLE001
                self._err(f"on_state 肄쒕갚 ?덉쇅: {e}")

    def _info(self, m: str):
        if self._log: self._log.info(m)
    def _warn(self, m: str):
        if self._log: self._log.warning(m)
    def _err(self, m: str):
        if self._log: self._log.error(m)

??븷:
