  - ?좏샇 ?꾪꽣留?(以묐났/?쒓컙/釉붾옓由ъ뒪??
  - ?좏샇 ?듦퀎 湲곕줉 (?몄엯/?댄깉 ?잛닔)
"""
import time
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional

from core.order_manager import OrderManager
from utils.logger import logger


# ?????????????????????????????????????
# ?좏샇 泥섎━ ?뚮씪誘명꽣
# ?????????????????????????????????????
DEDUP_WINDOW_SEC = 1.0           # 媛숈? 醫낅ぉ ?좏샇 以묐났 臾댁떆 (1珥??대궡)
SIGNAL_LOG_INTERVAL_SEC = 60     # ?좏샇 ?듦퀎 異쒕젰 二쇨린

# 醫낅ぉ 釉붾옓由ъ뒪??(愿由ъ쥌紐? 嫄곕옒?뺤?, 蹂몄씤???レ? 醫낅ぉ)
# 6?먮━ 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶 (?? '005930')
BLACKLIST: set[str] = {
    # "123456",  # ?덉떆 - 吏곸젒 異붽?
}


class ConditionManager:
    """?몄엯/?댄깉 ?좏샇 泥섎━"""

    def __init__(self, order_mgr: OrderManager):
        self.order_mgr = order_mgr

        # 以묐났 ?좏샇 ?꾪꽣: {醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶: 留덉?留??좏샇 ?쒓컖}
        self._last_signal_ts: dict[str, float] = {}

        # ?좏샇 ?듦퀎
        self._stats = {
            "insert": 0,        # ?몄엯 ?좏샇 珥?嫄댁닔
            "delete": 0,        # ?댄깉 ?좏샇 珥?嫄댁닔
            "filtered": 0,      # ?꾪꽣留곷맂 ?좏샇 (以묐났/釉붾옓由ъ뒪????
            "buy_attempted": 0, # OrderManager濡?留ㅼ닔 ?쒕룄 ?잛닔
        }
        self._stats_last_print = time.time()

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # WebSocket 肄쒕갚 吏꾩엯??
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    async def handle_signal(self, stock_code: str, signal_type: str, raw: dict):
        """
        KiwoomWS??on_signal 肄쒕갚?쇰줈 ?깅줉?섎뒗 ?⑥닔.
        signal_type: 'I'(?몄엯) | 'D'(?댄깉)
        """
        # 1. 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶 ?뺢퇋??('A005930' ??'005930')
        stock_code = self._normalize_code(stock_code)
        if not stock_code:
            return

        # 2. ?댄깉 ?좏샇: 濡쒓렇留??④린怨?醫낅즺
        if signal_type == "D":
            self._stats["delete"] += 1
            held = stock_code in self.order_mgr.positions
            held_mark = " (蹂댁쑀以?" if held else ""
            logger.info(f"?뱣 [?댄깉] {stock_code}{held_mark}")
            self._maybe_print_stats()
            return

        # 3. ?몄엯 ?좏샇 泥섎━
        self._stats["insert"] += 1

        # 3-1. 以묐났 ?좏샇 ?꾪꽣
        if self._is_duplicate(stock_code):
            self._stats["filtered"] += 1
            logger.debug(f"[?꾪꽣] {stock_code} 以묐났 ?좏샇 臾댁떆")
            return

        # 3-2. 釉붾옓由ъ뒪??泥댄겕
        if stock_code in BLACKLIST:
            self._stats["filtered"] += 1
            logger.info(f"[?꾪꽣] {stock_code} 釉붾옓由ъ뒪??)
            return

        # 3-3. ?쒓컙? ?꾪꽣 (?μ쨷 ?꾨땲硫?留ㅼ닔 ??蹂대깂, 濡쒓렇???④?)
        if not self._is_signal_window():
            self._stats["filtered"] += 1
            logger.info(f"?뱢 [?몄엯] {stock_code} - 嫄곕옒?쒓컙 ?? 留ㅼ닔 蹂대쪟")
            return

        # ?? 紐⑤뱺 ?꾪꽣 ?듦낵 ??
        logger.info(f"?뱢 [?몄엯] {stock_code} ??留ㅼ닔 ?쒕룄")
        self._stats["buy_attempted"] += 1

        try:
            # OrderManager.try_buy???숆린 ?⑥닔
            self.order_mgr.try_buy(stock_code)
        except Exception:
            logger.exception(f"留ㅼ닔 泥섎━ 以??덉쇅: {stock_code}")

        self._maybe_print_stats()

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?꾪꽣 ?ы띁
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_code(code: str) -> str:
        """'A005930' ??'005930', 怨듬갚/?댁긽媛?泥섎━"""
        if not code:
            return ""
        code = code.strip()
        if code.startswith("A"):
            code = code[1:]
        # 6?먮━ ?レ옄媛 ?꾨땲硫?臾댄슚
        if not (code.isdigit() and len(code) == 6):
            return ""
        return code

    def _is_duplicate(self, stock_code: str) -> bool:
        """媛숈? 醫낅ぉ ?좏샇媛 1珥??대궡 以묐났?쇰줈 ?ㅼ뼱?붾뒗吏"""
        now = time.time()
        last = self._last_signal_ts.get(stock_code, 0)
        if now - last < DEDUP_WINDOW_SEC:
            return True
        self._last_signal_ts[stock_code] = now
        return False

    @staticmethod
    def _is_signal_window() -> bool:
        """
        留ㅼ닔???좏샇 泥섎━ 媛???쒓컙?.
        OrderManager.TRADING_START~TRADING_END? 蹂꾨룄濡??ш린?쒕룄 ?쒕쾲 嫄곕쫫.
        """
        from core.order_manager import TRADING_START, TRADING_END
        now = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M")
        return TRADING_START <= now <= TRADING_END

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?듦퀎 異쒕젰
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def _maybe_print_stats(self):
        """二쇨린?곸쑝濡??좏샇 ?듦퀎 濡쒓렇"""
        if time.time() - self._stats_last_print < SIGNAL_LOG_INTERVAL_SEC:
            return
        self._stats_last_print = time.time()
        s = self._stats
        logger.info(
            f"?뱤 [?좏샇?듦퀎] ?몄엯={s['insert']} ?댄깉={s['delete']} "
            f"?꾪꽣留?{s['filtered']} 留ㅼ닔?쒕룄={s['buy_attempted']}"
        )

    def get_stats(self) -> dict:
        return dict(self._stats)

"""

?????????????????????????????????????

StrategyManager ?듯빀:

from api.kiwoom_rest import KiwoomREST

# ?????????????????????????????????????
# ?꾨왂 ?뚮씪誘명꽣
# ?????????????????????????????????????
BUY_AMOUNT_PER_STOCK = 2_000_000     # 醫낅ぉ??留ㅼ닔湲덉븸 (200留뚯썝)
MAX_POSITIONS = 5                    # ?숈떆 蹂댁쑀 理쒕? 醫낅ぉ??
BUY_COOLDOWN_SEC = 300               # 媛숈? 醫낅ぉ ?щℓ??荑⑤떎??(5遺?

TAKE_PROFIT_PCT = 2.5                # +2.5% ?듭젅
STOP_LOSS_PCT = -1.5                 # -1.5% ?먯젅
TIME_STOP_MIN = 30                   # 30遺?蹂댁쑀 ??0% 誘몃쭔?대㈃ ?뺣━

TRADING_START = "09:03"              # 嫄곕옒 ?쒖옉
TRADING_END = "15:10"                # 嫄곕옒 醫낅즺 (?댄썑 ?좉퇋留ㅼ닔 X)
FORCE_CLOSE_TIME = "15:15"           # 媛뺤젣 泥?궛 ?쒓컖

BUY_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS = 1           # ?꾩옱媛 +1??留ㅼ닔
SELL_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS = -1         # ?꾩옱媛 -1??留ㅻ룄


class OrderManager:
    def __init__(self, rest: KiwoomREST):
        self.rest = rest
        self.positions: dict[str, dict] = {}
        self.last_buy_ts: dict[str, float] = {}
        self.buying: set[str] = set()
        self._name_cache: dict[str, str] = {}
        self._force_close_done = False
        self._sell_failed: set[str] = set()

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 醫낅ぉ紐??ы띁
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def get_stock_name(self, stock_code: str) -> str:
        if stock_code in self._name_cache:
            return self._name_cache[stock_code]
        info = self.rest.get_stock_info(stock_code)
        name = (info.get("stk_nm") or "").strip()
        if name:
            self._name_cache[stock_code] = name
        return name or "?"

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?붽퀬 ?숆린??
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def sync_positions_from_server(self):
        holdings = self.rest.get_holdings()
        new_positions = {}
        for code, info in holdings.items():
            if info["qty"] <= 0:
                continue
            new_positions[code] = {
                "qty": info["qty"],
                "avg_price": info["avg_price"],
                "name": info["name"] or self.get_stock_name(code),
                "bought_at": self.positions.get(code, {}).get("bought_at", time.time()),
            }
            if info["name"]:
                self._name_cache[code] = info["name"]
        self.positions = new_positions
        logger.info(f"?벀 ?붽퀬 ?숆린?? 蹂댁쑀 {len(new_positions)}醫낅ぉ")
        return new_positions

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ??StrategyManager???⑥닚 wrapper
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def buy(self, stock_code: str, qty: int, price: int = 0) -> dict:
        """?⑥닚 留ㅼ닔 wrapper (StrategyManager ?몄텧??.

        Args:
            stock_code: 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶
            qty: 留ㅼ닔 ?섎웾
            price: 0?대㈃ ?꾩옱媛 +1?? >0?대㈃ 洹?媛寃?吏?뺢?

        Returns:
            {"success": bool, "ord_no"?: str, "price"?: int, "error"?: str}
        """
        if qty <= 0:
            return {"success": False, "error": f"qty={qty}"}
        try:
            if price <= 0:
                cur = self.rest.get_current_price(stock_code)
                if cur <= 0:
                    return {"success": False, "error": "?꾩옱媛 議고쉶 ?ㅽ뙣"}
                price = round_to_tick(add_ticks(cur, BUY_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS))

            result = self.rest.buy_market_order(
                stock_code, qty=qty, price=price, trde_tp="0"
            )
            rc = result.get("return_code")
            if rc != 0:
                return {"success": False, "error": result.get("return_msg", f"rc={rc}")}

            # ?ъ???湲곕줉 (StrategyManager???먯껜 holdings 愿由ы븯吏留?sync ?쇨????꾪빐)
            name = self.get_stock_name(stock_code)
            self.positions[stock_code] = {
                "qty": qty,
                "avg_price": price,
                "bought_at": time.time(),
                "name": name,
                "ord_no": result.get("ord_no", ""),
            }
            self.last_buy_ts[stock_code] = time.time()

            return {
                "success": True,
                "ord_no": result.get("ord_no", ""),
                "price": price,
            }
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception(f"[{stock_code}] buy() ?덉쇅")
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}

    def sell(self, stock_code: str, qty: int, price: int = 0) -> dict:
        """?⑥닚 留ㅻ룄 wrapper (StrategyManager ?몄텧??.

        Args:
            stock_code: 醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶
            qty: 留ㅻ룄 ?섎웾
            price: 0?대㈃ ?꾩옱媛 -1?? >0?대㈃ 洹?媛寃?吏?뺢?

        Returns:
            {"success": bool, "ord_no"?: str, "price"?: int, "error"?: str}
        """
        if qty <= 0:
            return {"success": False, "error": f"qty={qty}"}
        try:
            if price <= 0:
                cur = self.rest.get_current_price(stock_code)
                if cur <= 0:
                    return {"success": False, "error": "?꾩옱媛 議고쉶 ?ㅽ뙣"}
                price = round_to_tick(add_ticks(cur, SELL_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS))
                if price <= 0:
                    price = cur

            result = self.rest.sell_market_order(
                stock_code, qty=qty, price=price, trde_tp="0"
            )
            rc = result.get("return_code")
            if rc != 0:
                err_msg = result.get("return_msg", f"rc={rc}")
                # ?곴뎄 ?ㅽ뙣 ?먮떒
                if any(kw in str(err_msg) for kw in ["?섎웾", "?붽퀬", "蹂댁쑀", "泥닿껐", "遺議?]):
                    self._sell_failed.add(stock_code)
                    self.positions.pop(stock_code, None)
                return {"success": False, "error": err_msg}

            self.positions.pop(stock_code, None)
            return {
                "success": True,
                "ord_no": result.get("ord_no", ""),
                "price": price,
            }
        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception(f"[{stock_code}] sell() ?덉쇅")
            return {"success": False, "error": str(e)}

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 湲곗〈 留ㅼ닔 (?명솚?? ConditionManager ?먮쫫 ?깆뿉???ъ슜 媛??
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def try_buy(self, stock_code: str) -> bool:
        if not self._is_trading_time():
            logger.debug(f"[留ㅼ닔蹂대쪟] {stock_code} - 嫄곕옒?쒓컙 ??)
            return False
        if stock_code in self.buying:
            return False
        if stock_code in self.positions:
            logger.debug(f"[留ㅼ닔蹂대쪟] {stock_code} - ?대? 蹂댁쑀")
            return False
        if len(self.positions) >= MAX_POSITIONS:
            logger.info(f"[留ㅼ닔蹂대쪟] {stock_code} - 理쒕? 蹂댁쑀 {MAX_POSITIONS}醫낅ぉ ?꾨떖")
            return False

        last = self.last_buy_ts.get(stock_code, 0)
        if time.time() - last < BUY_COOLDOWN_SEC:
            return False

        orderable = self.rest.get_orderable_amount()
        if orderable < BUY_AMOUNT_PER_STOCK:
            logger.warning(
                f"[留ㅼ닔蹂대쪟] {stock_code} - 二쇰Ц媛?κ툑??遺議?"
                f"(?꾩슂 {BUY_AMOUNT_PER_STOCK:,} / 媛??{orderable:,})"
            )
            return False

        self.buying.add(stock_code)
        try:
            return self._execute_buy_legacy(stock_code)
        finally:
            self.buying.discard(stock_code)

    def _execute_buy_legacy(self, stock_code: str) -> bool:
        cur_price = self.rest.get_current_price(stock_code)
        if cur_price <= 0:
            logger.warning(f"[留ㅼ닔?ㅽ뙣] {stock_code} - ?꾩옱媛 議고쉶 ?ㅽ뙣")
            return False

        order_price = round_to_tick(add_ticks(cur_price, BUY_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS))
        qty = BUY_AMOUNT_PER_STOCK // order_price
        if qty <= 0:
            logger.warning(f"[留ㅼ닔?ㅽ뙣] {stock_code} - ?섎웾 0 (price={order_price})")
            return False

        name = self.get_stock_name(stock_code)

        result = self.rest.buy_market_order(
            stock_code, qty=qty, price=order_price, trde_tp="0"
        )

        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            msg = (f"??[留ㅼ닔?ㅽ뙣] {name}({stock_code}) {qty}二?@ {order_price:,}??n"
                   f"?ъ쑀: {result.get('return_msg')}")
            logger.error(msg)
            send_telegram(msg, target="order")
            return False

        self.positions[stock_code] = {
            "qty": qty,
            "avg_price": order_price,
            "bought_at": time.time(),
            "name": name,
            "ord_no": result.get("ord_no", ""),
        }
        self.last_buy_ts[stock_code] = time.time()

        msg = (f"?? [留ㅼ닔二쇰Ц] {name} ({stock_code})\n"
               f"?섎웾: {qty}二?n"
               f"二쇰Ц媛: {order_price:,}??(?꾩옱媛 {cur_price:,}+{BUY_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS}??\n"
               f"湲덉븸: {qty * order_price:,}??n"
               f"ord_no: {result.get('ord_no')}")
        logger.info(msg)
        send_telegram(msg, target="order")
        return True

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # 留ㅻ룄 (?먯껜 泥?궛 濡쒖쭅, ?꾩옱 ?ъ슜 ??????StrategyManager媛 ?대떦)
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def check_and_sell_positions(self):
        if not self.positions:
            return

        if self._should_force_close():
            self.force_close_all()
            return

        for stock_code in list(self.positions.keys()):
            if stock_code in self._sell_failed:
                continue
            try:
                self._evaluate_sell(stock_code)
            except Exception:
                logger.exception(f"?ъ????됯? ?덉쇅: {stock_code}")

    def _evaluate_sell(self, stock_code: str):
        pos = self.positions.get(stock_code)
        if not pos:
            return

        cur_price = self.rest.get_current_price(stock_code)
        if cur_price <= 0:
            return

        avg = pos["avg_price"]
        pnl_pct = (cur_price - avg) / avg * 100
        held_min = (time.time() - pos["bought_at"]) / 60

        if pnl_pct >= TAKE_PROFIT_PCT:
            self._execute_sell(stock_code, reason=f"?듭젅 +{pnl_pct:.2f}%")
            return
        if pnl_pct <= STOP_LOSS_PCT:
            self._execute_sell(stock_code, reason=f"?먯젅 {pnl_pct:.2f}%")
            return
        if held_min >= TIME_STOP_MIN and pnl_pct < 0:
            self._execute_sell(stock_code, reason=f"?쒓컙?뺣━ {pnl_pct:.2f}% ({held_min:.0f}遺?")
            return

    def _execute_sell(self, stock_code: str, reason: str = "") -> bool:
        pos = self.positions.get(stock_code)
        if not pos:
            return False

        cur_price = self.rest.get_current_price(stock_code)
        order_price = round_to_tick(add_ticks(cur_price, SELL_PRICE_OFFSET_TICKS))
        if order_price <= 0:
            order_price = cur_price

        name = pos.get("name") or self.get_stock_name(stock_code)

        result = self.rest.sell_market_order(
            stock_code, qty=pos["qty"], price=order_price, trde_tp="0"
        )

        if result.get("return_code") != 0:
            err_msg = str(result.get("return_msg", ""))
            msg = f"??[留ㅻ룄?ㅽ뙣] {name}({stock_code})\n?ъ쑀: {err_msg}"

            permanent_keywords = ["?섎웾", "?붽퀬", "蹂댁쑀", "泥닿껐", "遺議?]
            if any(kw in err_msg for kw in permanent_keywords):
                self._sell_failed.add(stock_code)
                self.positions.pop(stock_code, None)
                msg += "\n???ъ??섏뿉???쒓굅 (?섎룞 ?뺤씤 ?꾩슂)"

            logger.error(msg)
            send_telegram(msg, target="order")
            return False

        pnl = (order_price - pos["avg_price"]) * pos["qty"]
        pnl_pct_actual = (order_price - pos["avg_price"]) / pos["avg_price"] * 100

        msg = (f"?뮥 [留ㅻ룄二쇰Ц] {name} ({stock_code})\n"
               f"?ъ쑀: {reason}\n"
               f"?섎웾: {pos['qty']}二?n"
               f"二쇰Ц媛: {order_price:,}??n"
               f"?됯퇏?④?: {pos['avg_price']:,}??n"
               f"?덉긽?먯씡: {pnl:+,}??({pnl_pct_actual:+.2f}%)")
        logger.info(msg)
        send_telegram(msg, target="order")

        self.positions.pop(stock_code, None)
        return True

    def force_close_all(self):
        if self._force_close_done:
            return
        self._force_close_done = True

        if not self.positions:
            return

        logger.info(f"?뵒 ?λ쭏媛?媛뺤젣泥?궛: {len(self.positions)}醫낅ぉ")
        send_telegram(f"?뵒 ?λ쭏媛?媛뺤젣泥?궛 ?쒖옉: {len(self.positions)}醫낅ぉ", target="order")

        for stock_code in list(self.positions.keys()):
            self._execute_sell(stock_code, reason="?λ쭏媛?媛뺤젣泥?궛")

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?쒓컙 泥댄겕
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    @staticmethod
    def _is_trading_time() -> bool:
        now = datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M")
        return TRADING_START <= now <= TRADING_END

    @staticmethod
    def _should_force_close() -> bool:
        return datetime.now().strftime("%H:%M") >= FORCE_CLOSE_TIME

    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    # ?곹깭 異쒕젰
    # ?????????????????????????????????????
    def status_summary(self) -> str:
        if not self.positions:
            return "蹂댁쑀 醫낅ぉ ?놁쓬"
        lines = [f"?뱤 蹂댁쑀 {len(self.positions)}醫낅ぉ"]
        for code, pos in self.positions.items():
            held = (time.time() - pos["bought_at"]) / 60
            name = pos.get("name", "?")
            lines.append(f"  {name}({code}): {pos['qty']}二?@ {pos['avg_price']:,}??"
                         f"({held:.0f}遺?蹂댁쑀)")
        return "\n".join(lines)


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\core\phase1b_controller.py ===

"""Phase 1B 而⑦듃濡ㅻ윭 ??泥닿껐媛뺣룄 ?꾨왂 ?곗씠???뚯씠?꾨씪??

KiwoomWS??on_trade / on_orderbook 肄쒕갚?먯꽌 ?몄텧.
?대? ?몃옒而ㅻ뱾???낅뜲?댄듃?섍퀬 ChemulEvaluator濡?FSM ?됯?.
StrategyManager媛 寃곌낵(ChemulState)瑜?諛쏆븘 留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뻾 ?щ? 寃곗젙.
"""
from typing import Optional

from core.strategy.orderbook import OrderbookTracker
from core.strategy.trade_flow import TradeFlowTracker
from core.strategy.wall_detector import WallDetector
from core.strategy.chemul_evaluator import ChemulEvaluator, ChemulState


class Phase1BController:
    """泥닿껐媛뺣룄 ?꾨왂???곗씠???뚯씠?꾨씪??+ FSM ?듯빀 ?섑띁."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        # ?몃옒而??뚮씪誘명꽣 (TBD: ?ㅻ뜲?댄꽣濡??쒕떇)
        history_window_sec: float = 120,
        # WallDetector
        detect_multiplier: float = 5.0,
        shrink_ratio: float = 0.7,
        disappear_ratio: float = 0.2,
        avg_window_sec: float = 60,
        watch_levels: tuple = (1, 2),
        # ChemulEvaluator
        pullback_pct: float = -1.5,
        pullback_window_sec: float = 60,
        strength_short_window: float = 10,
        strength_long_window: float = 30,
        strength_min: float = 180,
        state_timeout_sec: float = 60,
    ):
        self.orderbook = OrderbookTracker(history_window_sec=history_window_sec)
        self.wall_detector = WallDetector(
            self.orderbook,
            detect_multiplier=detect_multiplier,
            shrink_ratio=shrink_ratio,
            disappear_ratio=disappear_ratio,
            avg_window_sec=avg_window_sec,
            watch_levels=watch_levels,
        )
        self.trade_flow = TradeFlowTracker(max_window_sec=history_window_sec)
        self.evaluator = ChemulEvaluator(
            trade_flow=self.trade_flow,
            wall_detector=self.wall_detector,
            orderbook=self.orderbook,
            pullback_pct=pullback_pct,
            pullback_window_sec=pullback_window_sec,
            strength_short_window=strength_short_window,
            strength_long_window=strength_long_window,
            strength_min=strength_min,
            state_timeout_sec=state_timeout_sec,
        )

        # 媛먯떆 以묒씤 醫낅ぉ 吏묓빀
        self.watched: set[str] = set()

    # ??? 媛먯떆 醫낅ぉ 愿由?????????????????????????
    def start_watching(self, stock_code: str):
        """Phase 1B ?꾨낫 媛먯떆 ?쒖옉."""
        self.watched.add(stock_code)

    def stop_watching(self, stock_code: str):
        """媛먯떆 以묐떒 + ?몃옒而?硫붾え由??뺣━."""
        self.watched.discard(stock_code)
        self.evaluator.reset(stock_code)
        self.orderbook.reset(stock_code)
        self.trade_flow.reset(stock_code)
        self.wall_detector.reset(stock_code)

    def is_watching(self, stock_code: str) -> bool:
        return stock_code in self.watched

    def get_state(self, stock_code: str) -> ChemulState:
        return self.evaluator.get_state(stock_code)

    # ??? WS 肄쒕갚 吏꾩엯??????????????????????????
    def on_trade(self, parsed_trade: dict, now: float = None) -> Optional[ChemulState]:
        """KiwoomWS on_trade?먯꽌 ?몄텧. 媛먯떆 醫낅ぉ?대㈃ ChemulState 諛섑솚."""
        code = parsed_trade.get("stock_code")
        if not code or code not in self.watched:
            return None
        self.trade_flow.add_tick(
            code,
            parsed_trade.get("price", 0),
            parsed_trade.get("side", "neutral"),
            parsed_trade.get("volume", 0),
            now=now,
        )
        return self.evaluator.evaluate(code, now=now)

    def on_orderbook(self, parsed_orderbook: dict, now: float = None) -> Optional[ChemulState]:
        """KiwoomWS on_orderbook?먯꽌 ?몄텧."""
        code = parsed_orderbook.get("stock_code")
        if not code or code not in self.watched:
            return None
        self.orderbook.update(code, parsed_orderbook, now=now)
        self.wall_detector.on_orderbook(code, now=now)
        return self.evaluator.evaluate(code, now=now)

def _load_fee_settings():
    is_mock = True
    commission = None
    tax = 0.0018
    try:
        import settings
        raw_mock = getattr(settings, "IS_MOCK", True)
        if isinstance(raw_mock, str):
            is_mock = raw_mock.strip().lower() in ("true", "1", "yes")
        else:
            is_mock = bool(raw_mock)
        # config??紐낆떆媛??덉쑝硫??곗꽑
        c = getattr(settings, "COMMISSION_RATE", None)
        if c not in (None, "", 0):
            commission = float(c)
        t = getattr(settings, "TAX_RATE", None)
        if t not in (None, ""):
            tax = float(t)
    except Exception:
        pass
    if commission is None:
        commission = 0.003 if is_mock else 0.00015   # 紐⑥쓽 0.3% / ?ㅼ쟾 0.015%
    return commission, tax


COMMISSION_RATE, TAX_RATE = _load_fee_settings()

            COMMISSION_RATE * 100, TAX_RATE * 100, ROUND_TRIP_COST * 100)

def _notify(msg: str):
    if send_telegram is None:
        return
    try:
        send_telegram(msg)

class StrategyManager:
    def __init__(
        self,
        kiwoom_rest,
        order_manager,
        phase1b_controller=None,
        phase3_controller=None,
        portfolio_optimizer=None,
        now_func=None,
    ):
        self.api = kiwoom_rest
        self.order_manager = order_manager
        self.phase1b = phase1b_controller
        self.phase3 = phase3_controller
        self.optimizer = portfolio_optimizer
        self._now = now_func or datetime.now

        self.holdings: dict[str, dict] = {}
        self.watch_list_today: set[str] = set()
        self.pending: set[str] = set()
        self._stock_names: dict[str, str] = {}
        
        # ?쇄뼹???ш린??異붽? ?쇄뼹??
        # HTS?먯꽌 ?섏뼱??1李??⑷꺽 醫낅ぉ?ㅼ쓽 ??먯쓣 湲곕떎由щ뒗 ?湲곗뿴 {醫낅ぉ肄붾뱶: ?ъ갑?쒓컙}
        self.watch_candidates: dict[str, datetime] = {}

        self._sell_fail_count: dict[str, int] = {}
        self._sell_blocked: set[str] = set()
        self._sold_at: dict[str, datetime] = {}
        self._buy_success_count = 0

        # ?먯닔 湲곕컲 吏꾩엯 ?ㅼ젙.
        # threshold_ratio=1.0 -> 湲곗〈 AND? (嫄곗쓽) ?숈씪. dry-run?먯꽌 score_breakdown 濡쒓렇 蹂???
        # 0.85 -> 0.75 ?앹쑝濡??④퀎?곸쑝濡???떠 near-miss 吏꾩엯 ?덉슜(=由ъ뒪???몄텧???④퍡 利앷?).
        self.score_cfg = ScoreConfig(
            surge_target=SURGE_THRESHOLD,
            surge_min=SURGE_ENTRY_MIN,
            ma_tolerance=MA_TOUCH_TOLERANCE,
            volume_target=VOLUME_SURGE_RATIO,
            threshold_ratio=1.0,
        )

        self._restore_from_db()
        self._last_phase = self.get_current_phase()

    # ========================================
    # ?쒖닔?듬쪧 怨꾩궛 (?섏닔猷?李④컧)
    # ========================================
    @staticmethod
    def _gross_rate(buy_price: float, current_price: float) -> float:
        return (current_price - buy_price) / buy_price if buy_price else 0.0

    @staticmethod
    def _net_rate(buy_price: float, current_price: float) -> float:
        """?섏닔猷??뺣났)+?멸툑 李④컧 ?쒖닔?듬쪧."""
        if not buy_price:
            return 0.0
        gross = (current_price - buy_price) / buy_price
        return gross - ROUND_TRIP_COST

    @staticmethod
    def _net_profit(buy_price: float, current_price: float, qty: int) -> float:
        """?ㅼ젣 ?쒖넀??湲덉븸 (?섏닔猷??멸툑 李④컧)."""
        buy_amt = buy_price * qty
        sell_amt = current_price * qty
        cost = buy_amt * COMMISSION_RATE + sell_amt * (COMMISSION_RATE + TAX_RATE)
        return (sell_amt - buy_amt) - cost

    # ========================================
    # ?곹깭 蹂듭썝
    # ========================================
    def _restore_from_db(self):
        warmup_until = self._now() + RESTART_WARMUP
        for h in TradeRepository.find_holdings():
            buy_price = float(h["buy_price"])
            self.holdings[h["stock_code"]] = {
                "trade_id": h["id"],
                "buy_price": buy_price,
                "buy_quantity": int(h["buy_quantity"]),
                "buy_time": h["buy_time"],
                "stock_name": h["stock_name"],
                "strategy_phase": h["strategy_phase"],
                "sub_strategy": h.get("sub_strategy"),
                "highest_price": buy_price,
                "ma20": None,                 # 20MA 罹먯떆 (誘멸퀎??
                "ma20_updated": None,         # 20MA 媛깆떊 ?쒓컖
                "warmup_until": warmup_until,
            }
        for w in WatchListRepository.find_by_date(self._now().date()):
            self.watch_list_today.add(w["stock_code"])

        logger.info(
            "DB 蹂듭썝: 蹂댁쑀 %d (1A=%d, 1B=%d, 2=%d, 3=%d) / ?뚯튂 %d / ?뚮컢??%ds",
            len(self.holdings),
            self.count_holdings_by_strategy("1A"),
            self.count_holdings_by_strategy("1B"),
            self.count_holdings_by_strategy("2"),
            self.count_holdings_by_strategy("3"),
            len(self.watch_list_today),
            int(RESTART_WARMUP.total_seconds()),
        )

    # ========================================
    # 雅뚯눊由??紐꾪뀱 (二쇨린 ?몄텧)
    # ========================================
    def tick(self):
        now = self._now()

        cur_phase = self.get_current_phase()
        if cur_phase != self._last_phase:
            # (以묐왂... ?꾨왂 ?꾪솚 濡쒓렇 李띾뒗 遺遺?
            self._last_phase = cur_phase

        # ?쇄뼹???ш린????踰덉㎏ 蹂듭궗蹂?for code in list(self.watch_candidates.keys()): 遺遺???遺숈뿬?ｌ쑝?몄슂 ?쇄뼹??
        for code in list(self.watch_candidates.keys()):
            # ?대? ?嫄곕굹 ?щ뵫(二쇰Ц 以??대㈃ ?щ’?먯꽌 鍮꾩썙以?
            if code in self.holdings or code in self.pending:
                del self.watch_candidates[code]
                continue

            try:
                # 1遺꾨큺 ?곗씠??70媛??몄텧 (CandleCache媛 諛⑹뼱?댁쨲)
                candles = self.api.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=70)
                
                # N???뚮┝紐?????됯?!
                is_timing, info = self.evaluate_morning_pullback(candles)
                
                if is_timing:
                    stock_name = self._stock_names.get(code, code)
                    logger.info("?렞 [%s] %s 10MA ?뚮┝紐?????ъ갑! 留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뻾", code, stock_name)
                    
                    # 留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뻾 (?쒕툕 ?꾨왂 ?대쫫 '1N' - N???뚮┝紐?
                    self._execute_buy(code, stock_name, phase=cur_phase or 1, info=info, sub_strategy="1N")
                    
                    # 留ㅼ닔 ???щ’ 鍮꾩슦湲?
                    del self.watch_candidates[code]

            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning("[%s] 愿李?醫낅ぉ ????됯? 以??먮윭: %s", code, e)
        # ?꿎뼯???ш린源뚯? ?꿎뼯??

        if self.phase1b and now.time() >= PHASE2_END:
            for code in list(self.phase1b.watched):
                if code not in self.holdings:
                    self.phase1b.stop_watching(code)
        # 蹂댁쑀醫낅ぉ 20MA 罹먯떆 媛깆떊 (泥?궛??
        self._refresh_exit_ma()

        self.check_timeouts()

    # ========================================
    # 20MA 罹먯떆 媛깆떊 (泥?궛 湲곗???
    # ========================================
    def _refresh_exit_ma(self):
        """蹂댁쑀醫낅ぉ蹂꾨줈 20MA瑜?二쇨린 媛깆떊??罹먯떆. 遺꾨큺 遺議??ㅽ뙣 ??None ?좎?."""
        now = self._now()
        for code, pos in list(self.holdings.items()):
            if code in self._sell_blocked:
                continue
            last = pos.get("ma20_updated")
            if last and (now - last) < EXIT_MA_REFRESH:
                continue
            try:
                candles = self.api.get_minute_candles(
                    code, interval=1, count=EXIT_MA_FETCH_COUNT)
                if candles and len(candles) >= EXIT_MA_PERIOD:
                    ma20 = calc_ma(candles, EXIT_MA_PERIOD)
                    if ma20:
                        pos["ma20"] = ma20
                        pos["ma20_updated"] = now
                else:
                    # 遺꾨큺 遺議??? ?μ쨷 1媛?踰꾧렇) -> 20MA 泥?궛 ?ㅽ궢, ?먯젅/?듭젅罹≪? 怨꾩냽 ?묐룞
                    logger.debug("[%s] 20MA 媛깆떊 蹂대쪟: 遺꾨큺 %d媛?,
                                 code, len(candles) if candles else 0)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning("[%s] 20MA 媛깆떊 ?ㅽ뙣: %s", code, e)

    # ========================================
    # Phase ?먮퀎
    # ========================================
    def get_current_phase(self) -> Optional[int]:
        t = self._now().time()
        if PHASE1_START <= t < PHASE1_END:
            return 1
        if PHASE2_START <= t < PHASE2_END:
            return 2
        if PHASE3_START <= t < PHASE3_END:
            return 3
        return None

    def can_buy_more(self) -> bool:
        return len(self.holdings) < MAX_HOLDINGS

    def count_holdings_by_strategy(self, sub: str) -> int:
        return sum(1 for h in self.holdings.values() if h.get("sub_strategy") == sub)

    def can_buy_phase1a(self) -> bool:
        return (self.can_buy_more()
                and self.count_holdings_by_strategy("1A") < PHASE1A_MAX_SLOTS
                and PHASE1_START <= self._now().time() < PHASE1_END)

    def can_buy_phase1b(self) -> bool:
        return (self.can_buy_more()
                and self.count_holdings_by_strategy("1B") < PHASE1B_MAX_SLOTS
                and PHASE1_START <= self._now().time() < PHASE2_END)

    def can_buy_phase3(self) -> bool:
        return (self.can_buy_more()
                and self.count_holdings_by_strategy("3") < PHASE3_MAX_SLOTS
                and PHASE3_START <= self._now().time() < PHASE3_END)

    def can_buy_surge(self) -> bool:
        return (self.can_buy_more()
                and self.count_holdings_by_strategy("1S") < SURGE_MAX_SLOTS
                and PHASE1_START <= self._now().time() < PHASE2_END)

    # ========================================
    # 荑⑤떎??/ 李⑤떒
    # ========================================
    def _is_rebuy_blocked(self, stock_code: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        if stock_code in self._sell_blocked:
            return True, "留ㅻ룄 李⑤떒 (?곴뎄?ㅽ뙣)"
        if stock_code in self._sold_at:
            elapsed = self._now() - self._sold_at[stock_code]
            if elapsed < REBUY_COOLDOWN:
                remaining = REBUY_COOLDOWN - elapsed
                return True, f"荑⑤떎??(?붿뿬 {int(remaining.total_seconds())}珥?"
        return False, ""

    # ========================================
    # 吏꾩엯
    # ========================================
    def on_condition_hit(self, stock_code: str, stock_name: str, is_surge: bool = False):
        phase = self.get_current_phase()
        if phase is None:
            return
        if stock_code in self.holdings or stock_code in self.pending:
            return

        blocked, reason = self._is_rebuy_blocked(stock_code)
        if blocked:
            logger.info("[%s] %s 留ㅼ닔 李⑤떒: %s", stock_code, stock_name, reason)
            return

        self._stock_names[stock_code] = stock_name

        # ?? Phase 3 (10:41~): 泥닿껐媛뺣룄 ?⑥“利앷? 媛먯떆 ??
        if phase == 3:
            if not self.phase3:
                return
            if not self.can_buy_phase3():
                logger.info("[%s] Phase 3 ?щ’ 遺議?- 媛먯떆 嫄대꼫?", stock_code)
                return
            if not self.phase3.is_watching(stock_code):
                self.phase3.start_watching(stock_code)
            return

        try:
            candles = self.api.get_minute_candles(stock_code, interval=1, count=15)
            if not candles or len(candles) < VOLUME_LOOKBACK + 1:
                logger.warning("[%s] 遺꾨큺 遺議?(%d媛?", stock_code,
                               len(candles) if candles else 0)
            else:
                # ?? 湲됰벑(surge) 議곌굔: 09:00~10:40 MA?곗튂 ?놁씠 利됱떆留ㅼ닔 (1S) ??
                if is_surge:
                    ok, info = self.evaluate_surge(candles)
                    self._record_watch_list(stock_code, stock_name, phase, info)
                    if ok:
                        if self.can_buy_surge():
                            self._execute_buy(stock_code, stock_name, phase, info, sub_strategy="1S")
                            return
                        else:
                            logger.info("[%s] 湲됰벑 議곌굔 OK but ?щ’ 遺議?, stock_code)
                    else:
                        logger.info("[%s] %s 湲됰벑 誘몄땐議? %s",
                                    stock_code, stock_name, info.get("reason"))

                # ?? 鍮?湲됰벑 議곌굔: Phase1留?5MA ?됯? (Phase2 30MA 留ㅼ닔???쒓굅) ??
                elif phase == 1:
                    ok, info = self.evaluate_phase1(candles)
                    self._record_watch_list(stock_code, stock_name, phase, info)
                    if ok:
                        if self.can_buy_phase1a():
                            self._execute_buy(stock_code, stock_name, phase, info, sub_strategy="1A")
                            return
                        else:
                            logger.info("[%s] Phase1A 議곌굔 OK but ?щ’ 遺議?, stock_code)
                    else:
                        logger.info("[%s] %s Phase1 誘몄땐議? %s",
                                    stock_code, stock_name, info.get("reason"))

            # ?? Phase1 ?덈룄?? 泥닿껐媛뺣룄(1B) 媛먯떆 ?쒖옉 (湲됰벑/鍮꾧툒??怨듯넻, 湲곗〈 ?좎?) ??
            if phase == 1 and self.phase1b and not self.phase1b.is_watching(stock_code):
                self.phase1b.start_watching(stock_code)
                logger.info("[%s] Phase 1B 媛먯떆 ?쒖옉", stock_code)

        except Exception as e:
            logger.exception("[%s] on_condition_hit ?ㅽ뙣: %s", stock_code, e)
            SystemEventRepository.log("STRATEGY_ERROR", f"{stock_code}: {e}", "ERROR")
            _notify(f"?꾨왂 ?먮윭\n{stock_code}: {e}")

    # ========================================
    # ?ㅼ떆媛?肄쒕갚
    # ========================================
    def on_trade(self, parsed_trade: dict, now: float = None):
        code = parsed_trade.get("stock_code")
        if not code:
            return

        if code in self.holdings:
            price = parsed_trade.get("price")
            if price:
                self.on_price_update(code, price)
            return

        if self.phase1b and self.phase1b.is_watching(code):
            state = self.phase1b.on_trade(parsed_trade, now=now)
            if state == ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY:
                self._try_phase1b_buy(code, now)

        if self.phase3 and self.phase3.is_watching(code):
            from core.strategy.phase3_controller import Phase3State
            new_state = self.phase3.on_trade(parsed_trade)
            if new_state == Phase3State.READY_TO_BUY:
                self._try_phase3_buy(code)

    def on_orderbook(self, parsed_orderbook: dict, now: float = None):
        code = parsed_orderbook.get("stock_code")
        if not code:
            return
        if self.phase1b and self.phase1b.is_watching(code):
            state = self.phase1b.on_orderbook(parsed_orderbook, now=now)
            if state == ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY:
                self._try_phase1b_buy(code, now)

    def _try_phase1b_buy(self, stock_code: str, now: float = None):
        if not self.can_buy_phase1b():
            logger.info("[%s] Phase 1B READY but ?щ’ 遺議?, stock_code)
            return
        if stock_code in self.holdings or stock_code in self.pending:
            return
        blocked, reason = self._is_rebuy_blocked(stock_code)
        if blocked:
            logger.info("[%s] Phase 1B 留ㅼ닔 李⑤떒: %s", stock_code, reason)
            return

        current_price = self.phase1b.trade_flow.get_latest_price(stock_code)
        if not current_price:
            logger.warning("[%s] Phase 1B 留ㅼ닔 ?쒕룄 but 媛寃??놁쓬", stock_code)
            return

        stock_name = self._stock_names.get(stock_code, stock_code)
        info = {"current_price": current_price, "volume_ratio": 0.0}
        self._execute_buy(stock_code, stock_name, phase=1, info=info, sub_strategy="1B")
        self.phase1b.stop_watching(stock_code)

    def _try_phase3_buy(self, stock_code: str):
        if not self.can_buy_phase3():
            logger.info("[%s] Phase 3 READY but ?щ’ 遺議?, stock_code)
            self.phase3.stop_watching(stock_code)
            return
        if stock_code in self.holdings or stock_code in self.pending:
            return
        blocked, reason = self._is_rebuy_blocked(stock_code)
        if blocked:
            logger.info("[%s] Phase 3 留ㅼ닔 李⑤떒: %s", stock_code, reason)
            self.phase3.stop_watching(stock_code)
            return

        try:
            candles = self.api.get_minute_candles(stock_code, interval=1, count=1)
            current_price = candles[0]["close"] if candles else 0
        except Exception:
            current_price = 0

        if not current_price:
            logger.warning("[%s] Phase 3 留ㅼ닔 ?쒕룄 but 媛寃??놁쓬", stock_code)
            self.phase3.stop_watching(stock_code)
            return

        stock_name = self._stock_names.get(stock_code, stock_code)
        info = {"current_price": current_price, "volume_ratio": 0.0}
        self._execute_buy(stock_code, stock_name, phase=3, info=info, sub_strategy="3")
        self.phase3.stop_watching(stock_code)

    # ========================================
    # 吏꾩엯 ?됯? (?먯닔 湲곕컲 ??scoring.py ?꾩엫)
    #   諛섑솚 怨꾩빟/?똧nfo ?ㅻ뒗 湲곗〈怨??숈씪. threshold_ratio濡?媛뺣룄 議곗젅.
    # ========================================
    def evaluate_phase1(self, candles: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
        code = candles[0].get("stock_code") or list(self.watch_candidates.keys())[0]
        current_strength = self.phase1b.trade_flow.compute_strength(code, window_sec=10)
        return score_phase1(candles, self._volume_ratio(candles), current_strength, self.score_cfg)

    def evaluate_surge(self, candles: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
        code = candles[0].get("stock_code") or list(self.watch_candidates.keys())[0]
        current_strength = self.phase1b.trade_flow.compute_strength(code, window_sec=10)
        return score_surge(candles, self._volume_ratio(candles), current_strength, self.score_cfg)

    def evaluate_phase2(self, candles: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
        code = candles[0].get("stock_code") or list(self.watch_candidates.keys())[0]
        current_strength = self.phase1b.trade_flow.compute_strength(code, window_sec=10)
        return score_phase2(candles, self._volume_ratio(candles), PHASE2_MA_PERIOD, current_strength, self.score_cfg)

    @staticmethod
    def _volume_ratio(candles: list[dict]) -> float:
        cur_vol = candles[0]["volume"]
        prev = candles[1:1 + VOLUME_LOOKBACK]
        if not prev:
            return 0.0
        avg = sum(c["volume"] for c in prev) / len(prev)
        return cur_vol / avg if avg > 0 else 0.0

    # ?쇄뼹???ш린??泥?踰덉㎏ 蹂듭궗蹂?evaluate_morning_pullback ?꾩껜)??遺숈뿬?ｌ쑝?몄슂 ?쇄뼹??
    # ========================================
    # ?ㅼ쟾??湲됰벑 ??泥??뚮┝紐??ㅻ굹?댄띁 留ㅼ닔 ???(N??諛섎벑)
    # ========================================
    def evaluate_morning_pullback(self, candles: list[dict]) -> tuple[bool, dict]:
        # ... (?댁쟾 ?듬????⑥닔 ?댁슜) ...
    # ?꿎뼯???ш린源뚯? ?꿎뼯??

    # ========================================
    # ?쇻끉????쎈뻬 (留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뻾 ?뚰듃)
    # ========================================
    def _resolve_position_amount(self, stock_code: str, sub_strategy: str) -> tuple[int, Optional[dict]]:
        # ...

    # ========================================
    # 留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뻾
    # ========================================
    def _resolve_position_amount(self, stock_code: str, sub_strategy: str) -> tuple[int, Optional[dict]]:
        if self.optimizer is None:
            return POSITION_AMOUNT, None
        try:
            opt_info = self.optimizer.calculate_position_amount(stock_code, sub_strategy)
            amount = int(opt_info.get("amount", 0))
            if amount <= 0:
                return POSITION_AMOUNT, None
            return amount, opt_info
        except Exception:
            logger.exception(f"[{stock_code}] 鍮꾩쨷 怨꾩궛 ?ㅽ뙣, fallback")
            return POSITION_AMOUNT, None

    def _execute_buy(self, stock_code, stock_name, phase, info, sub_strategy):
        current_price = info["current_price"]

        position_amount, opt_info = self._resolve_position_amount(stock_code, sub_strategy)
        quantity = int(position_amount // current_price)
        if quantity < 1:
            logger.warning("[%s] %s ?섎웾 0 -> skip", stock_code, stock_name)
            return

        if opt_info:
            logger.info("[%s] ?숈쟻 鍮꾩쨷 %.2fx -> %s??, stock_code,
                        opt_info.get("final_weight", 1.0), f"{position_amount:,}")

        self.pending.add(stock_code)
        try:
            ma_val = info.get("ma5") or 0
            if sub_strategy == "1B":
                entry_reason = f"Phase 1B 泥닿껐媛뺣룄 (?꾩옱媛 {current_price:,})"
            elif sub_strategy == "3":
                entry_reason = f"Phase 3 ?⑥“利앷? 1遺꾩쑀吏 (?꾩옱媛 {current_price:,})"
            elif sub_strategy == "1S":
                entry_reason = (f"湲됰벑 吏꾩엯 | ?쒖큹媛+{info.get('surge_rate', 0)*100:.2f}% "
                                f"| vol x{info.get('volume_ratio', 0):.2f} (?꾩옱媛 {current_price:,})")
            else:
                # 1A=5MA, 2=30MA (PHASE2_MA_PERIOD)
                ma_label = "5" if sub_strategy == "1A" else str(PHASE2_MA_PERIOD)
                entry_reason = (f"Phase{sub_strategy} | "
                                f"MA{ma_label}={ma_val:,.0f} "
                                f"| vol x{info.get('volume_ratio', 0):.2f}")
                if sub_strategy == "1A":
                    entry_reason += f" | ?쒖큹媛+{info.get('surge_rate', 0)*100:.2f}%"
            if opt_info:
                entry_reason += f" | 鍮꾩쨷x{opt_info.get('final_weight', 1.0):.2f}"

            result = self.order_manager.buy(stock_code, quantity, price=0)
            if not result or not result.get("success"):
                err = (result or {}).get("error", "unknown")
                logger.error("[%s] 留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뙣: %s", stock_code, err)
                SystemEventRepository.log("ORDER_FAIL", f"BUY {stock_code}: {err}", "ERROR")
                _notify(f"留ㅼ닔 ?ㅽ뙣\n{stock_code} {stock_name}\n?ъ쑀: {err}")
                return

            trade_id = TradeRepository.insert_buy(
                stock_code=stock_code, stock_name=stock_name,
                buy_price=current_price, buy_quantity=quantity,
                strategy_phase=phase, sub_strategy=sub_strategy,
                entry_reason=entry_reason,
            )

            self.holdings[stock_code] = {
                "trade_id": trade_id,
                "buy_price": current_price,
                "buy_quantity": quantity,
                "buy_time": self._now(),
                "stock_name": stock_name,
                "strategy_phase": phase,
                "sub_strategy": sub_strategy,
                "highest_price": current_price,
                "ma20": None,
                "ma20_updated": None,
                "position_weight": (opt_info or {}).get("final_weight", 1.0),
                "warmup_until": self._now() + BUY_WARMUP,
            }
            self._sold_at.pop(stock_code, None)
            self._buy_success_count += 1

            logger.info("BUY [%s] %s %d二?@ %s??(%s) = %s??| ?뚮컢??%ds",
                        stock_code, stock_name, quantity, f"{current_price:,}",
                        sub_strategy, f"{current_price * quantity:,}",
                        int(BUY_WARMUP.total_seconds()))
            SystemEventRepository.log("BUY",
                f"{stock_code} {stock_name} {quantity}二?@ {current_price:,}??[{sub_strategy}]", "INFO")
            weight_str = f" (鍮꾩쨷 {opt_info['final_weight']:.2f}x)" if opt_info else ""
            _notify(f"留ㅼ닔 泥닿껐 [{sub_strategy}]\n醫낅ぉ: {stock_name} ({stock_code})\n"
                    f"?섎웾: {quantity}二?@ {current_price:,}??weight_str}\n"
                    f"湲덉븸: {current_price * quantity:,}??n?꾨왂: {entry_reason}")
            self._mark_watch_bought(stock_code)
        finally:
            self.pending.discard(stock_code)

    # ========================================
    # ?뚯튂由ъ뒪??
    # ========================================
    def _record_watch_list(self, stock_code, stock_name, phase, info):
        if stock_code in self.watch_list_today:
            return
        try:
            extra = {}
            for k in ("ma5", "current_price", "volume_ratio"):
                if k in info:
                    extra[k] = info[k]
            if "surge_rate" in info:
                extra["surge_rate"] = info["surge_rate"] * 100
            if "reason" in info:
                extra["reason_not_bought"] = info["reason"]
            WatchListRepository.add(stock_code=stock_code, stock_name=stock_name, phase=phase, **extra)
            self.watch_list_today.add(stock_code)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning("[%s] ?뚯튂由ъ뒪???ㅽ뙣: %s", stock_code, e)

    def _mark_watch_bought(self, stock_code: str):
        try:
            for w in WatchListRepository.find_by_date(self._now().date()):
                if w["stock_code"] == stock_code and not w.get("is_bought"):
                    WatchListRepository.mark_bought(w["id"])
                    break
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning("[%s] mark_bought ?ㅽ뙣: %s", stock_code, e)

    # ========================================
    # 泥?궛 (5/22 媛쒗렪: ?먯젅 -2.5% / ?듭젅罹?+2.5% / 20MA ?댄깉 / ?쒓컙?뺣━)
    # ========================================
    def on_price_update(self, stock_code: str, current_price: float):
        pos = self.holdings.get(stock_code)
        if not pos or not current_price:
            return
        if stock_code in self._sell_blocked:
            return

        buy_price = pos["buy_price"]
        if not buy_price:
            return

        if current_price > pos["highest_price"]:
            pos["highest_price"] = current_price

        warmup_until = pos.get("warmup_until")
        if warmup_until and self._now() < warmup_until:
            return

        gross_rate = self._gross_rate(buy_price, current_price)   # 媛寃?湲곗?
        net_rate   = gross_rate - ROUND_TRIP_COST                 # ?쒖씡 湲곗?

        exit_reason = None

        # 1) ?먯젅: 媛寃?湲곗? -2.5%
        if gross_rate <= STOP_LOSS_RATE:
            exit_reason = f"?먯젅 媛寃?gross_rate*100:.2f}% (??{net_rate*100:.2f}%)"

        # 2) ?듭젅 罹? ?쒖씡 湲곗? +2.5%
        elif net_rate >= TAKE_PROFIT_CAP:
            exit_reason = f"?듭젅 罹???{net_rate*100:.2f}% (媛寃?+{gross_rate*100:.2f}%)"

        # 3) 20MA ?댄깉: ?꾩옱媛媛 20MA瑜?0.3% ?댁긽 ?섑쉶 (?몃젅?쇰쭅 ?泥?
        #    20MA 罹먯떆媛 ?덉쓣 ?뚮쭔 ?묐룞. 遺꾨큺 遺議깆쑝濡?罹먯떆 None?대㈃ ?ㅽ궢.
        else:
            ma20 = pos.get("ma20")
            if ma20:
                break_line = ma20 * (1 - EXIT_MA_BREAK_PCT)
                if current_price < break_line:
                    below_pct = (current_price - ma20) / ma20 * 100
                    exit_reason = (f"20MA ?댄깉 ({below_pct:+.2f}%, "
                                   f"??{net_rate*100:+.2f}%)")

        # 4) ?쒓컙?뺣━ 30遺?
        if exit_reason is None:
            if self._now() - pos["buy_time"] >= HOLDING_TIMEOUT:
                exit_reason = f"?쒓컙?뺣━ 30遺?(??{net_rate*100:+.2f}%)"

        if exit_reason:
            self._execute_sell(stock_code, current_price, exit_reason)

    def _execute_sell(self, stock_code, current_price, exit_reason):
        pos = self.holdings.get(stock_code)
        if not pos or stock_code in self.pending:
            return
        if stock_code in self._sell_blocked:
            return

        logger.info("泥?궛 ?몃━嫄?[%s] %s | ?ъ쑀: %s | ?꾩옱媛 %s",
                    stock_code, pos.get("stock_name", ""), exit_reason, f"{current_price:,}")

        self.pending.add(stock_code)
        try:
            quantity = pos["buy_quantity"]
            result = self.order_manager.sell(stock_code, quantity, price=0)

            if not result or not result.get("success"):
                err = (result or {}).get("error", "unknown")
                cnt = self._sell_fail_count.get(stock_code, 0) + 1
                self._sell_fail_count[stock_code] = cnt

                logger.error("[%s] 留ㅻ룄 ?ㅽ뙣 (%d/%d): %s", stock_code, cnt, MAX_SELL_FAIL, err)
                SystemEventRepository.log("ORDER_FAIL",
                    f"SELL {stock_code}: {err} ({cnt}/{MAX_SELL_FAIL})", "ERROR")

                if cnt >= MAX_SELL_FAIL:
                    self._sell_blocked.add(stock_code)
                    stock_name = pos.get("stock_name", stock_code)
                    self.holdings.pop(stock_code, None)
                    logger.warning("[%s] %s 留ㅻ룄 %d???ㅽ뙣 -> 李⑤떒", stock_code, stock_name, cnt)
                    SystemEventRepository.log("SELL_BLOCKED",
                        f"{stock_code} 留ㅻ룄 {cnt}???ㅽ뙣 -> 李⑤떒", "WARNING")
                    _notify(f"留ㅻ룄 李⑤떒\n{stock_name} ({stock_code})\n"
                            f"留ㅻ룄 {cnt}???ㅽ뙣 -> ?섎룞 ?뺤씤 ?꾩슂")
                else:
                    _notify(f"留ㅻ룄 ?ㅽ뙣 ({cnt}/{MAX_SELL_FAIL})\n"
                            f"{pos.get('stock_name', stock_code)} ({stock_code})\n?ъ쑀: {err}")
                return

            self._sell_fail_count.pop(stock_code, None)
            self._sold_at[stock_code] = self._now()

            TradeRepository.update_sell(
                trade_id=pos["trade_id"], sell_price=current_price,
                sell_quantity=quantity, exit_reason=exit_reason,
            )

            # ?쒖넀??(?섏닔猷??멸툑 李④컧)
            gross_profit = (current_price - pos["buy_price"]) * quantity
            net_profit = self._net_profit(pos["buy_price"], current_price, quantity)
            gross_rate = self._gross_rate(pos["buy_price"], current_price) * 100
            net_rate = self._net_rate(pos["buy_price"], current_price) * 100
            stock_name = pos["stock_name"]
            sub = pos.get("sub_strategy", "?")
            del self.holdings[stock_code]

            logger.info("SELL [%s] %s %d二?@ %s??-> %s | ?쒖넀??%s??(??%.2f%%, 媛寃?%.2f%%) [%s]",
                        stock_code, stock_name, quantity, f"{current_price:,}", exit_reason,
                        f"{net_profit:+,.0f}", net_rate, gross_rate, sub)
            SystemEventRepository.log("SELL",
                f"{stock_code} {stock_name} {quantity}二?@ {current_price:,}??[{sub}] | "
                f"{exit_reason} | ?쒖넀??{net_profit:+,.0f}??, "INFO")
            emoji = "+" if net_profit > 0 else "-"
            _notify(f"留ㅻ룄 泥닿껐 [{sub}] ({emoji})\n醫낅ぉ: {stock_name} ({stock_code})\n"
                    f"?섎웾: {quantity}二?@ {current_price:,}??n"
                    f"?쒖넀?? {net_profit:+,.0f}??(??{net_rate:+.2f}%, 媛寃?{gross_rate:+.2f}%)\n"
                    f"?ъ쑀: {exit_reason}\n?щℓ??李⑤떒: {int(REBUY_COOLDOWN.total_seconds()/60)}遺?)
        finally:
            self.pending.discard(stock_code)

    # ========================================
    # ??꾩븘??
    # ========================================
    def check_timeouts(self):
        now = self._now()
        for code in list(self.holdings.keys()):
            pos = self.holdings[code]
            warmup_until = pos.get("warmup_until")
            if warmup_until and now < warmup_until:
                continue
            if now - pos["buy_time"] < HOLDING_TIMEOUT:
                continue
            if code in self._sell_blocked:
                continue
            try:
                candles = self.api.get_minute_candles(code, interval=1, count=1)
                if candles:
                    self._execute_sell(code, candles[0]["close"], "?쒓컙?뺣━ 30遺?)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.exception("[%s] ??꾩븘??泥?궛 ?ㅽ뙣: %s", code, e)


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\core\strategy\chemul_evaluator.py ===

"""Phase 1B 泥닿껐媛뺣룄 ?꾨왂 FSM.

5?④퀎 ?쒖감 議곌굔 異붿쟻:
  1. 1遺꾨큺 ?뚮┝ (-1.5%) ??WAITING_WALL
  2. 留ㅻ룄踰??깆옣 (WallState.DETECTED) ??WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH
  3. 留ㅻ룄踰?異뺤냼 (SHRINKING) + 泥닿껐媛뺣룄 湲됱긽????WAITING_DISAPPEAR
  4. 留ㅻ룄踰??뚯떎 (DISAPPEARED) ??READY_TO_BUY
  5. 留ㅼ닔 ??reset() ?먮뒗 ??꾩븘????WAITING_PULLBACK 蹂듦?

?뚮씪誘명꽣??placeholder (?ㅻ뜲?댄꽣 諛쏄퀬 ?쒕떇 ?덉젙).
"""
import time
from enum import Enum
from typing import Optional

from core.strategy.orderbook import OrderbookTracker
from core.strategy.trade_flow import TradeFlowTracker
from core.strategy.wall_detector import WallDetector, WallState


class ChemulState(str, Enum):
    WAITING_PULLBACK = "waiting_pullback"
    WAITING_WALL = "waiting_wall"
    WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH = "waiting_shrink_strength"
    WAITING_DISAPPEAR = "waiting_disappear"
    READY_TO_BUY = "ready_to_buy"


class ChemulEvaluator:
    """泥닿껐媛뺣룄 ?꾨왂 ??醫낅ぉ蹂?5?④퀎 FSM."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        trade_flow: TradeFlowTracker,
        wall_detector: WallDetector,
        orderbook: OrderbookTracker,
        # ?뚮씪誘명꽣 (TBD: ?ㅻ뜲?댄꽣濡??쒕떇)
        pullback_pct: float = -1.5,          # 1遺꾧컙 -1.5% ?댄븯硫??뚮┝
        pullback_window_sec: float = 60,
        strength_short_window: float = 10,
        strength_long_window: float = 30,
        strength_min: float = 180,            # ?④린 媛以?媛뺣룄 ?꾧퀎媛?
        state_timeout_sec: float = 60,        # 媛??곹깭 理쒕? 泥대쪟 ?쒓컙
    ):
        self.tf = trade_flow
        self.wd = wall_detector
        self.ob = orderbook

        self.pullback_pct = pullback_pct
        self.pullback_window_sec = pullback_window_sec
        self.strength_short_window = strength_short_window
        self.strength_long_window = strength_long_window
        self.strength_min = strength_min
        self.state_timeout_sec = state_timeout_sec

        # {code: {state, ts_entered_state}}
        self._state: dict[str, dict] = {}

    def evaluate(self, stock_code: str, now: float = None) -> ChemulState:
        """留??대깽??泥닿껐/?멸?)留덈떎 ?몄텧. 媛?ν븯硫??щ윭 ?곹깭 ?곗냽 ?꾩씠."""
        now = now if now is not None else time.time()

        s = self._state.get(stock_code)
        if s is None:
            s = {"state": ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK, "ts": now}
            self._state[stock_code] = s

        # ??꾩븘??泥댄겕 (PULLBACK / READY_TO_BUY???쒖쇅)
        if s["state"] not in (ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK, ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY):
            if now - s["ts"] > self.state_timeout_sec:
                s["state"] = ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK
                s["ts"] = now

        # 媛?ν븳 留뚰겮 ?곗냽 ?꾩씠
        while True:
            prev = s["state"]
            self._try_transition(stock_code, now)
            if s["state"] == prev:
                break

        return s["state"]

    def _try_transition(self, code: str, now: float):
        s = self._state[code]
        st = s["state"]

        if st == ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK:
            pct = self.tf.get_price_change_pct(
                code, self.pullback_window_sec, now
            )
            if pct is not None and pct <= self.pullback_pct:
                self._advance(code, ChemulState.WAITING_WALL, now)

        elif st == ChemulState.WAITING_WALL:
            ws = self.wd.get_state(code)
            # ?대? SHRINKING/DISAPPEARED?쇰룄 DETECTED瑜?嫄곗퀜??嫄곕땲 吏꾪뻾
            if ws in (WallState.DETECTED, WallState.SHRINKING, WallState.DISAPPEARED):
                self._advance(code, ChemulState.WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH, now)

        elif st == ChemulState.WAITING_SHRINK_STRENGTH:
            ws = self.wd.get_state(code)
            if ws in (WallState.SHRINKING, WallState.DISAPPEARED):
                if self.tf.is_strength_rising(
                    code,
                    short_window=self.strength_short_window,
                    long_window=self.strength_long_window,
                    now=now,
                    min_short_strength=self.strength_min,
                ):
                    self._advance(code, ChemulState.WAITING_DISAPPEAR, now)

        elif st == ChemulState.WAITING_DISAPPEAR:
            if self.wd.get_state(code) == WallState.DISAPPEARED:
                self._advance(code, ChemulState.READY_TO_BUY, now)

    def _advance(self, code: str, new_state: ChemulState, now: float):
        self._state[code]["state"] = new_state
        self._state[code]["ts"] = now

    def get_state(self, stock_code: str) -> ChemulState:
        s = self._state.get(stock_code)
        return s["state"] if s else ChemulState.WAITING_PULLBACK

    def get_info(self, stock_code: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        return self._state.get(stock_code)

    def reset(self, stock_code: str):
        """留ㅼ닔 ?깃났 ???먮뒗 媛뺤젣 由ъ뀑."""
        self._state.pop(stock_code, None)

"""
湲곗닠??吏??怨꾩궛 紐⑤뱢
?????????????????????????????????????
?대룞?됯퇏??MA), MA ?곗튂 ?먯젙 ??
蹂몄씤 ?꾨왂???듭떖 吏??怨꾩궛 ?⑥닔??
"""


def calc_ma(candles: list[dict], period: int) -> float:
    """
    ?대룞?됯퇏??(Simple Moving Average) 怨꾩궛.
    
    Args:
        candles: 遺꾨큺 由ъ뒪??(?쒓컙 ??닚, [0]??理쒖떊).
                 媛???ぉ? {'close': int, ...} ?뺥깭?ъ빞 ??
        period: 湲곌컙 (?? 5, 20, 60, 120).
    
    Returns:
        吏곸쟾 period媛?遊됱쓽 醫낃? ?됯퇏.
        遊됱씠 遺議깊븯硫?0.
    
    Examples:
        >>> candles = [{'close': 100}, {'close': 102}, {'close': 98},
        ...            {'close': 105}, {'close': 103}]
        >>> calc_ma(candles, 5)
        101.6
    """
    if len(candles) < period:
        return 0.0
    closes = [c["close"] for c in candles[:period]]
    return sum(closes) / period


def is_ma_touch(price: int, ma: float, tolerance_pct: float = 0.3) -> bool:
    """
    ?꾩옱媛媛 ?대룞?됯퇏?좎뿉 '?곗튂'?덈뒗吏 ?먯젙.
    
    ?곗튂 ?뺤쓽: ?꾩옱媛媛 MA??짹tolerance_pct% ?대궡.
    
    Args:
        price: ?꾩옱媛.
        ma: ?대룞?됯퇏媛?
        tolerance_pct: ?덉슜 踰붿쐞 (%). 0.3?대㈃ 짹0.3%.
    
    Returns:
        True硫??곗튂.
    
    Examples:
        >>> is_ma_touch(100, 100.0, 0.3)   # ?뺥솗???곗튂
        True
        >>> is_ma_touch(100, 100.2, 0.3)   # +0.2% 李⑥씠 ???곗튂
        True
        >>> is_ma_touch(100, 100.5, 0.3)   # +0.5% 李⑥씠 ??誘명꽣移?
        False
    """
    if ma == 0:
        return False
    diff_pct = abs(price - ma) / ma * 100
    return diff_pct <= tolerance_pct


def is_volume_breakout(
    candles: list[dict],
    multiplier: float = 1.5,
    avg_window: int = 5,
) -> bool:
    """
    理쒓렐 遊됱쓽 嫄곕옒?됱씠 吏곸쟾 ?됯퇏??multiplier諛??댁긽?몄? ?먯젙.
    
    Args:
        candles: 遺꾨큺 由ъ뒪??(?쒓컙 ??닚, [0]??理쒖떊).
        multiplier: 諛곗닔 (1.5?대㈃ ?됯퇏??1.5諛??댁긽).
        avg_window: ?됯퇏 怨꾩궛??遊?媛쒖닔 (5?대㈃ [1:6] ?ъ슜).
    
    Returns:
        True硫?嫄곕옒????쬆.
    
    Examples:
        >>> candles = [{'volume': 1000}, {'volume': 500}, {'volume': 600},
        ...            {'volume': 550}, {'volume': 450}, {'volume': 500}]
        >>> is_volume_breakout(candles, 1.5)   # 1000 vs ?됯퇏 520
        True
    """
    if len(candles) < avg_window + 1:
        return False
    
    latest_vol = candles[0]["volume"]
    prev_volumes = [c["volume"] for c in candles[1:1 + avg_window]]
    
    if not prev_volumes:
        return False
    
    avg_vol = sum(prev_volumes) / len(prev_volumes)
    if avg_vol == 0:
        return False
    
    return latest_vol >= avg_vol * multiplier


def get_volume_ratio(
    candles: list[dict],
    avg_window: int = 5,
) -> float:
    """
    理쒓렐 遊?嫄곕옒??/ 吏곸쟾 ?됯퇏 嫄곕옒??鍮꾩쑉.
    
    is_volume_breakout()??吏꾨떒/濡쒓렇??踰꾩쟾.
    
    Returns:
        鍮꾩쑉 (?? 2.5 = ?됯퇏??2.5諛?. ?곗씠??遺議깊븯硫?0.
    """
    if len(candles) < avg_window + 1:
        return 0.0
    
    latest_vol = candles[0]["volume"]
    prev_volumes = [c["volume"] for c in candles[1:1 + avg_window]]
    
    if not prev_volumes:
        return 0.0
    
    avg_vol = sum(prev_volumes) / len(prev_volumes)
    if avg_vol == 0:
        return 0.0
    
    return latest_vol / avg_vol


def is_bullish_candle(candle: dict) -> bool:
    """
    ?묐큺(?곸듅 遊? ?щ?.
    
    Args:
        candle: 遊?dict, {'open': int, 'close': int, ...}.
    
    Returns:
        醫낃? > ?쒓?硫?True.
    """
    return candle["close"] > candle["open"]


def is_bearish_candle(candle: dict) -> bool:
    """?뚮큺 ?щ? (李멸퀬??"""
    return candle["close"] < candle["open"]


def get_today_first_candle(candles: list[dict], target_date: str) -> dict | None:
    """
    ?뱀씪 泥?1遺꾨큺 (=?쒖큹媛 遊? 李얘린.
    
    Args:
        candles: 遺꾨큺 由ъ뒪??(?쒓컙 ??닚).
        target_date: YYYYMMDD.
    
    Returns:
        ?ㅻ뒛 09:01遊?dict (?먮뒗 媛???대Ⅸ ?ㅻ뒛 遊?.
        ?놁쑝硫?None.
    """
    today_candles = [c for c in candles if c["time_str"].startswith(target_date)]
    if not today_candles:
        return None
    
    # ?쒓컙 ??닚?대땲 留덉?留됱씠 媛???대Ⅸ 遊?
    return today_candles[-1]


def calc_rise_pct_from_open(current: int, today_open: int) -> float:
    """
    ?쒖큹媛 ?鍮??곸듅瑜?(%).
    
    Args:
        current: ?꾩옱媛.
        today_open: ?ㅻ뒛 ?쒖큹媛.
    
    Returns:
        ?곸듅瑜?(?? 5.3 = +5.3%). today_open=0?대㈃ 0.0.
    """
    if today_open == 0:
        return 0.0
    return (current - today_open) / today_open * 100


=== FILE: C:\Users\rober\OneDrive\문서\vscode\AutoTrader_Project\core\strategy\orderbook.py ===

"""?ㅼ떆媛??멸?李??ㅻ깄???몃옒而?

KiwoomWS??on_orderbook 肄쒕갚?먯꽌 update() ?몄텧.
WallDetector媛 ?닿구 李몄“?댁꽌 留ㅻ룄踰?異붿쟻.
"""
import time
from collections import deque
from typing import Optional


class OrderbookTracker:
    """醫낅ぉ蹂??멸?李?理쒖떊 ?곹깭 + ?붾웾 ?덉뒪?좊━."""

    def __init__(self, history_window_sec: float = 60):
        # ?꾩옱 ?ㅻ깄?? {code: snapshot_dict}
        self.snapshots: dict[str, dict] = {}
        # ?멸? ?붾웾 ?덉뒪?좊━: {code: deque[(ts, ask_volumes_list, bid_volumes_list)]}
        self.history: dict[str, deque] = {}
        self.history_window_sec = history_window_sec

    def update(self, stock_code: str, snapshot: dict, now: float = None):
        """0D 硫붿떆吏 ?ㅼ뼱???뚮쭏???몄텧."""
        now = now if now is not None else time.time()
        self.snapshots[stock_code] = snapshot

        h = self.history.setdefault(stock_code, deque())
        h.append((
            now,
            list(snapshot.get("ask_volumes") or []),
            list(snapshot.get("bid_volumes") or []),
        ))
        # ?ㅻ옒???곗씠???쒓굅
        cutoff = now - self.history_window_sec
        while h and h[0][0] < cutoff:
            h.popleft()

    def get_snapshot(self, stock_code: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        return self.snapshots.get(stock_code)

    def get_ask_volume(self, stock_code: str, level: int = 1) -> int:
        """?꾩옱 留ㅻ룄 N?멸? ?붾웾 (level=1~10)."""
        snap = self.snapshots.get(stock_code)
        if not snap:
            return 0
        vols = snap.get("ask_volumes") or []
        idx = level - 1
        return vols[idx] if 0 <= idx < len(vols) else 0

    def get_bid_volume(self, stock_code: str, level: int = 1) -> int:
        snap = self.snapshots.get(stock_code)
        if not snap:
            return 0
        vols = snap.get("bid_volumes") or []
        idx = level - 1
        return vols[idx] if 0 <= idx < len(vols) else 0

    def get_ask_volume_avg(
        self,
        stock_code: str,
        level: int = 1,
        window_sec: float = None,
        exclude_latest: bool = False,
    ) -> float:
        """留ㅻ룄 N?멸???吏곸쟾 window_sec ?숈븞 ?됯퇏 ?붾웾.

        window_sec=None?대㈃ ?꾩껜 history ?ъ슜.
        exclude_latest=True硫?媛??理쒓렐 ?ㅻ깄???쒖쇅 (踰?媛먯? baseline ?곗텧??.
        """
        h = self.history.get(stock_code)
        if not h:
            return 0.0
        if window_sec is not None:
            now = h[-1][0]
            cutoff = now - window_sec
            samples = [ask for ts, ask, _ in h if ts >= cutoff]
        else:
            samples = [ask for _, ask, _ in h]

        if exclude_latest:
            if len(samples) <= 1:
                return 0.0  # baseline ?≪쓣 ?곗씠???놁쓬
            samples = samples[:-1]

        idx = level - 1
        values = [s[idx] for s in samples if idx < len(s)]
        return sum(values) / len(values) if values else 0.0

    def get_top_ask(self, stock_code: str) -> tuple[Optional[int], int]:
        """?꾩옱 留ㅻ룄 1?멸? (price, volume). ?놁쑝硫?(None, 0)."""
        snap = self.snapshots.get(stock_code)
        if not snap:
            return None, 0
        prices = snap.get("ask_prices") or []
        vols = snap.get("ask_volumes") or []
        if not prices:
            return None, 0
        return prices[0], (vols[0] if vols else 0)

    def get_top_bid(self, stock_code: str) -> tuple[Optional[int], int]:
        snap = self.snapshots.get(stock_code)
        if not snap:
            return None, 0
        prices = snap.get("bid_prices") or []
        vols = snap.get("bid_volumes") or []
        if not prices:
            return None, 0
        return prices[0], (vols[0] if vols else 0)

    def reset(self, stock_code: str):
        self.snapshots.pop(stock_code, None)
        self.history.pop(stock_code, None)
